### [#54] production activation preflight + real-source identity smoke — 운영 가동 전 통합 점검 + 단계별 진단(자동 병합 0·운영 DB 미적용·미가동·LLM/Agent 진입 docs)
- 날짜: 2026-06-25 · 섹터: production activation boundary / real-source loop 진단 / LLM·Agent readiness · 상태: **R-LiveIdentityBacklog·R-RealSourceLoopUnproven 부분진전·완전종결=OVERCLAIM·옵션 C/D 계속 DEFER·E 금지**

**문제** — ADR#53 이 docker 실행성을 실측했지만, 실 production backlog 직전 단계(운영 DB 배포 경계·safe-target 실효성·persist 가동 조건·실 source smoke·packet/reviewer handoff·LLM/Agent 진입)가 흩어진 게이트로만 존재했다. safe-target(`assert_safe_write_target`)은 dev/test 허용·그외 차단의 **binary** 가드라 dev `event_intel`+APP_ENV=dev 경로에선 사실상 no-op(MEDIUM-1)인데, 이 한계가 명시적 report 로 표면화되지 않았다. "`--persist` 하나 붙이면 가동"이라는 오인을 막을 통합 preflight 가 필요했다.
**원자 분석(§2·20문항)** — 4 서브시스템 병렬 탐색(file:line): (게이팅) `backfill_preflight`(6필드)·`operational_db_readiness`(9필드)·`assert_safe_write_target`(binary·classification 없음)·config(APP_ENV Literal·flags off-default). (source) yna/bbc/hacker_news=key-free 안전 smoke·`_IDENTITY_ANCHOR_SOURCE_TYPES={official,article}`·community/market/catalog anchor 금지(`non_publishable_role` guard). (loop) packet→reviewer→gold→MERGE_GATE 코드 BUILT·live-PG TEST·`auto_merge_enabled=False` 불변·MERGE_GATE **임계(목표)** precision≥0.98/FPR≤0.01/hard-neg FP=0/KO precision≥0.98·표본 floor live gold≥200·KO≥50(현 adjudicator 실측 precision 0.57 < 임계·미달). (docs) 운영 DB 0003→0009 runbook·index/lock DEFER 이미 문서화·LLM/Agent Go/No-Go 기재됨. **결론:** preflight 17필드 대부분 기존 함수 조합으로 도출 가능·신규는 target_classification/mismatch/can_persist/block_reasons/next_actions. fake-source smoke 는 network 0·DB 0 로 재현 가능(probe 주입·record→Event 는 write-free).
**옵션 비교(§3)** — (A) production activation preflight package (B) test-DB real-source smoke (C) 운영 DB upgrade 실행 (D) scheduler persist activation (E) LLM/Agent IU prototype. **선택: A 채택 + B 채택(tool·fake-default·CI 필수 아님) + C/D 금지(승인 필요) + E docs 설계만.** ADR#54 기록.
**구현(A)** — `backend/app/tools/production_activation_preflight.py`(read-only·DDL/upgrade/persist 0): `_build_preflight_report`(순수·DB 무관) 가 readiness+flag+safe_target+classify 를 조립 → 17필드 report(app_env·database_url_fingerprint·target_classification·env/url_class·app_env_url_consistent·is_dev/production_target·allow_non_dev_db·event_resolution/semantic_adjudication_enabled·scheduler_profile_enabled·persist_requested·ready_for_stage3·db_revision·expected_head·pending_migrations·identity_tables_present·can_dry_run·can_persist·block_reasons·warnings·next_required_actions). `can_persist = persist ∧ ready ∧ (flag∨allow_flag_off) ∧ safe_target ∧ ¬destructive ∧ (consistent∨allow_non_dev)`. `db_target.classify_write_target`(named 분류+불일치) 신설 — safe-target binary 위에 dev/test/staging/production/unknown + APP_ENV↔URL mismatch(URL prod-marker 가 APP_ENV 보다 위험하면 채택·거짓 안심 차단). DATABASE_URL 원문 미로그(`target_db_label` fingerprint 만). exit 0(green)/1(blocked)/2(runtime). dev head 실행: dry-run eval exit 0·persist+flag off blocked exit 1·persist+allow_flag_off exit 0. safe-target no-op(MEDIUM-1)을 warning 으로 표면화·index/lock DEFER 를 persist 시 warning.
**구현(B)** — `backend/app/tools/real_source_identity_smoke.py`(기본 offline fake·network 0·DB 0·결정론): `run_offline_identity_smoke` 가 fetch(주입)→cluster_records→candidate_from_cluster 까지 **write-free** 진단 → source_role_distribution·failures_by_stage(body_missing/no_cluster_singleton/non_publishable_role/no_semantic_fingerprint)·publishable_anchor·semantic_fingerprint_candidates. fake fixture(news 2 cluster+official+community-only guard+singleton+body-missing) 결정론 출력(sources 8·clusters 3·singletons 2·fingerprints 2·role article5/official1/community2). DB 단계(created/held/withheld/adjudications/packet)는 offline **None**(정직·미도달). `run_db_identity_smoke`(safe-target gated·test/dev DB 만·opt-in) 가 기존 `ingest_records_to_events`(live-PG 검증됨) 호출해 DB 단계 채움(thin adapter). **실 fetch 0 이면 RealSourceLoop 닫았다고 주장 안 함**(real_fetch 플래그)·`no_auto_merge=True` 불변·community 는 anchor 아님(non_publishable_role).
**옵션 C/D/E(§7/§8)** — **C(index)/D(lock) 계속 DEFER**(ADR#52/#53 근거 유지·preflight 가 persist 시 warning 으로 은폐 금지). **E(LLM/Agent)** docs 만: 진입 9조건(backlog>0·source role guard·candidate/adjudication·reviewer/gold 또는 eval gate·MERGE_GATE·raw/public 분리·uncertainty·community reaction layer·time-series substrate)·Agent 역할(evidence/gold/MERGE_GATE/uncertainty 통제 하 IU 생성)을 `RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS`·`INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT` 에 명문화. 본경로 구현 0.
**측정(정직)** — 신규 테스트 2파일: `test_production_activation_preflight.py`(classify+게이트+exit·DB 무관·순수·28)·`test_real_source_identity_smoke.py`(offline 결정론·bounded·safe-target gate·summary 매핑·10) — **38 passed**(classify consistent 갭 수정 회귀 6 포함). db_target consumer 슬라이스 29 passed·**backend 비-live(live-PG 제외) 512 passed/4 skipped/0 failed**(959s·pre-fix ADR#54 test 29 포함·classify fix 후 38p 재검증)·ingestion 1353·frontend tsc0/test12/lint0·preflight CLI 3모드 exit 0/1/0·smoke CLI offline 결정론. 변경 표면: 신규 도구 2 + 신규 테스트 2 + `db_target.py`(classify_write_target 추가·기존 assert 불변) + docs. **운영 DB 무변경**(preflight read-only·smoke 기본 offline DB 0).
**adversarial 평결** — adversarial-reality-critic **CONDITIONAL VALID**: 4대 안전계약(read-only·can_persist 비우회[allow_non_dev 는 boundary 만·readiness/flag 못 우회·테스트 잠금]·no_auto_merge·secret 미로그[fingerprint 만·구조적으로 raw URL 진입 불가]) **코드+테스트 실증**·과대주장 없음(점검/진단≠가동·real_fetch 0 표면화·production 백로그 0 일관). **MEDIUM-1 발견·수정:** `classify_write_target` 의 `consistent` 가 cross-tier 불일치(env=production+url=staging·env=unknown+url=production·env=staging+url=production)를 "일치"로 오보고(차단은 `assert_safe_write_target` fail-closed 로 보존되나 진단 신호 거짓) → **tier-일치 규칙으로 수정**(`url_class==expected`·unknown env=항상 불일치)+회귀 테스트 6. code-review finder 별건: live-DB 모드 `identity_links` 가 None 으로 남던 honesty 갭 → `summarize_db_ingest` 가 `held_member_links` 로 채움(수정). 잔여(미수정·acknowledged): async `production_activation_preflight`(DB gather)는 CLI 3회 실측만·CI 잠금 테스트 부재(순수 `_build_preflight_report` 가 전 분기 보유)·LOW.
**결과** — **R-LiveIdentityBacklog 부분진전**(production activation preflight·DB boundary 표면화·real-source smoke 진단 tool)·**R-RealSourceLoopUnproven 부분진전**(단계별 실패 분류 진단·fake-default·CI 강제 아님). 운영 DB 실배포(C/E·승인)·실 fetch 볼륨·profile 활성+--persist 가동·실 reviewer/gold/merge 잔여(완전종결 금지).
**한계** — preflight 는 **점검**이지 가동이 아니다(read-only)·smoke 기본은 **fake-source**(real_fetch 0·실 network 미수행)·DB 단계는 offline None(live-DB 는 opt-in·safe-target gated·이번 턴 실행 0)·scheduler 실가동 0·production 백로그 0·LLM/Agent 본경로 0(docs 설계만). 점검·진단(능력)≠운영 가동(actuality).
**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/{production_activation_preflight,real_source_identity_smoke}.py`·`backend/app/tools/db_target.py`·`backend/tests/{test_production_activation_preflight,test_real_source_identity_smoke}.py`·`docs/2_ROADMAP/15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/{RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS,INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT}.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#48~#53.

### [#55] real-source live-db smoke + source quality matrix + agent readiness report — fake→실 fetch→실 DB 한 단계 진전(자동 병합 0·운영 DB 미적용·production 아님)
- 날짜: 2026-06-25 · 섹터: real-source loop 실데이터 진전 / source quality / LLM·Agent readiness · 상태: **R-RealSourceLoopUnproven·R-LiveIdentityBacklog 부분진전·완전종결=OVERCLAIM·옵션 C 금지·D docs/schema only**

**문제** — ADR#54 real-source smoke 는 **기본 fake-source**(real_fetch=0·network 0·DB offline None)라 "RealSourceLoop 가 실 운영 데이터에서 어디까지 닿는가"를 못 보였다. fake fixture 가 fetch→cluster→candidate 를 도는 것은 계약 검증이지 실 source 흐름이 아니다. 실 key-free source 를 bounded 하게 fetch 해 test/dev DB 에서 source→record→Event→identity→adjudication→packet 까지 어디서 멈추는지 **실데이터로 단계별 분해**할 필요.
**원자 분석(§2·20문항)** — 4 서브시스템 병렬 탐색(file:line)+환경 실측: (source) `ingestion/sources/_registry.get_source_instance`·`federal_register`/`sec_edgar`=key-free official JSON API(canonical=document_number·published_at·robots-friendly)·뉴스는 HTML scraping parser 취약·`_IDENTITY_ANCHOR_SOURCE_TYPES={official,article}`. (DB write) `ingest_records_to_events` CREATE=events+event_updates(genesis)+cluster_event_map+identity_map+candidate+held event_links; persist=event_identity_adjudication upsert(semantic_cross_batch_candidate link 만). (chain) `collect_adjudication_eval_pairs`→packet_eligible·`build_live_identity_labeling_packet`→selected·predicted_status withheld·PII 차단·`auto_merge_enabled=False` 불변·precision 0.57<gate. (환경) **로컬 docker `event_intel`·`event_intel_test` 둘 다 head `c9d0e1f2a3b4`(0009)**·문서 "운영 DB 0003"=미배포 production 타깃(로컬 아님)·federalregister.gov API status 200(network egress 작동)·live-PG fixture 가 `_EVENT_TABLES` TRUNCATE(test DB 잔여행 무해). **결론:** 실 fetch+실 live_db smoke 이번 턴 실행 가능(disposable `event_intel_test`·official key-free).
**옵션 비교(§3)** — (A) bounded real-source smoke in dev/test DB (B) fixture capture(sanitized·raw body 금지) (C) production DB activation (D) LLM/Agent prototype (E) source quality matrix. **선택: A 채택 + B 채택(본문 미저장·headline/canonical/published_at 만) + E 채택 + C 금지(승인) + D docs/schema only.** ADR#55 기록.
**구현** — `real_source_identity_smoke.py` 확장: `fetch_real_source_records`(key-free official allowlist `_SMOKE_SOURCE_RECORD_TYPE`={federal_register,sec_edgar}·bounded source당 ≤5·`_parse_payload_records` 가 raw JSON→다중 record[canonical·published_at·**headline[:512] 만·raw_payload/body 미저장**]·실패 source별 분류 source_disabled/network_error/parser_error/no_records·**transport 주입으로 CI network 0 결정론**)·`run_offline_identity_smoke` 에 records_with_body/canonical/published_at·source_ids 추가·`run_db_identity_smoke` 에 `_count_events` before/after·CLI `--live-network/--source` 추가. 신규 `real_source_smoke_report.py`(순수·DB/network 0): `assemble_activation_report`(§4 fields)·`build_source_quality_matrix`(§9·옵션 E·source별 body/canonical/published/dedup_clusterability/identity_linkability[official+canonical=anchor_eligible·community/market/catalog=guard_only]/readiness/failure_stage)·`agent_readiness_conditions`(§8 9조건 PASS/PARTIAL/FAIL/NOT_BUILT)·`agent_readiness_gate`(No-Go). community/market/catalog anchor 금지·`no_auto_merge=True` 불변.
**측정(실데이터·정직)** — **live_network 실 fetch:** federal_register status 200·**5 official records**(body/canonical/published 5/5·role official 5·clusters 1·singletons 3·fingerprints 1; **fetch 는 abstract/payload 전문을 수신하나 record/DB 에는 미반영** — headline[:512]/canonical/published_at 만·`_cached` 는 프로세스 휘발). allowlist=federal_register 만(sec_edgar 는 canonical 미파생→anchor 불가·endpoint 미실측 → 보류·adversarial MEDIUM). **live_db(disposable `event_intel_test` head 0009·target=test consistent):** 실 fetch 5 → ingest **created 1 + identity_link 1(held member·reason `new_event_low_confidence`) · adjudications 0 · packet_eligible 0 · no_auto_merge=True · event_count 4→6**(DB read-only 검증: events 6·possible link 1·candidate 1·adjudication 0). **event_count +2 분해 = primary CREATE 1 + held-member degenerate event 1**(ADR#19 materialize·event_links(possible) 1·**자동 병합 아님**·created 카운트는 primary 만 셈). **정직 분해:** adjudications 0 = held-member link reason 이 `semantic_cross_batch_candidate` 가 아니라서(stage③은 semantic 후보 link 만 처리)·실 Event 는 형성되나 cross-batch adjudication 은 **동일사건 다중소스/시계열 fingerprint 중첩** 필요(single bounded single-source=source scarcity). 테스트: 신규/확장 **36 passed**(test_real_source_identity_smoke 19[+9: fetch parser/allowlist/network·parser·no_records 분류/bounded/record-quality/live_network probe]·test_real_source_smoke_report 17[matrix anchor/guard_only/failure·readiness 9조건·activation report·no_auto_merge])·**backend 비-live 547 passed/4 skipped/0 failed(963s)**·live-PG **91 passed**(event_intel_test·smoke 행 TRUNCATE 정리)·ingestion **1353**·frontend tsc0/test12/lint0(`next lint`)·secret scan PASS.
**옵션 C/D(§6/§8)** — **C(운영 DB activation) 금지**(승인 전·이번 턴 운영 DB 무변경·disposable test DB 만). **D(LLM/Agent)** docs/schema only: agent readiness 9조건 status 를 `real_source_smoke_report.agent_readiness_conditions` 가 **결정론 산출**(단일 출처)·현재 **1·4·5·7 미충족 → No-Go**(2/3/8 evidence 를 실 fetch 로 보강)·본경로 구현 0.
**결과** — **R-RealSourceLoopUnproven 부분진전**(실 federal_register fetch+실 live_db ingest 로 1~5 단계 실데이터 1회 도달·단계별 실패 실 흐름 설명·no-auto-merge 유지)·**R-LiveIdentityBacklog 부분진전**(real-source smoke+preflight 연결·packet/reviewer export 경로까지 수치화). 신규 RISK 미등록(coverage/matrix/readiness 는 기존 RISK 의 gap·RISK 남발 금지).
**한계** — **live_network=opt-in tool/report(CI 아님)**·**live_db=disposable test DB(production 아님)**·실 cross-source 비뉴스 Event·실 adjudication backlog·reviewer/gold/merge·운영 DB 배포·주기 스케줄러 실가동 잔여(production 백로그 0 불변·완전종결 금지). 실 fetch(능력)≠production 운영(actuality).
**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/{real_source_identity_smoke,real_source_smoke_report}.py`·`backend/tests/{test_real_source_identity_smoke,test_real_source_smoke_report}.py`·`docs/2_ROADMAP/{00_ROADMAP_INDEX,15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP}.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/{RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS,INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT}.md`·`docs/_CANONICAL/02_CURRENT_ARCHITECTURE.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#54.

### [#56] time-series replay smoke + adjudication block-reason 분해 — cross-batch adjudication substrate 실데이터 입증(자동 병합 0·artificial≠실 source·production 백로그 0)
- 날짜: 2026-06-25 · 섹터: real-source loop cross-batch substrate / adjudication 발생 조건 분해 · 상태: **R-RealSourceLoopUnproven·R-LiveIdentityBacklog 부분진전·완전종결=OVERCLAIM·옵션 B+C+E 채택·A 정직분해·C(prod)/D(LLM) 금지**

**문제(§5)** — ADR#55 실 federal_register fetch 5 official 은 **adjudications 0** 이었다. "실패"로 뭉뚱그리지 않고 call path 로 분해: cross-batch `semantic_cross_batch_candidate` link 은 `resolve_and_apply_cluster` 에서 **새로 CREATE 된 Event 의 fingerprint(제목 token-set+date bucket)가 기존 `event_identity_candidate` 의 *다른-URL* Event 정확히 1개와 매칭**될 때만 생성되고, stage③ adjudicator 는 그 link 만 처리(`WHERE reason='semantic_cross_batch_candidate'`). held-member link 은 reason `new_event_low_confidence:{key}` 라 제외. **federal_register 는 distinct document=distinct canonical_url=distinct event=distinct fingerprint → 같은-사건·다른-URL 후보가 구조적으로 불가**(singleton 은 `len(members)<2` drop) = **source scarcity**.
**원자 분석(§2·20문항)** — substrate 4모듈 정독(file:line): `event_ingest_pipeline.ingest_records_to_events`(배치별 cluster→resolve→stage③)·`event_resolution_pipeline.resolve_and_apply_cluster`(semantic link 생성 조건 98–140)·`semantic_identity_adjudicator`(SEMANTIC_LINK_REASON·classify likely_same/ambiguous/insufficient)·`cross_source_dedup.semantic_identity_fingerprint`(≥4 유의미 토큰+date bucket sha1). 검증된 형태(`test_live_stage3_wiring_auto_adjudicates`의 `_sem_ingest_batch`)=배치 내부 같은 canonical, 배치 간 다른 canonical·fingerprint만 공유.
**옵션 결정(§3)** — (A) multi-source 실 fetch (B) time-series replay (C) sanitized capture (D) production DB (E) LLM/Agent. **선택: B 채택(핵심·결정론 substrate 검증)+C 채택(별도 capture 파일 미생성·본문 미저장 계약을 replay 템플릿에 내재·YAGNI)+E 채택(§5 block-reason 분해 추가). A 정직 분해만**(key-free 공식 단독 cross-source overlap 구조적 희소·깨지기 쉬운 스크레이퍼 미구현). **C(production)/D(LLM) 금지.** ADR#56 기록.
**구현** — `real_source_identity_smoke.py`: `build_replay_batches()`(artificial 2배치·같은 사건·다른 URL·교차배치·본문 미저장)·`run_time_series_replay_smoke(session, batches=, persist=, allow_non_dev=)`(safe-target gated·배치 순차 ingest[배치 간 commit 으로 fingerprint 가시]·`_link_reason_distribution`/`_adjudication_status_distribution` read-only 집계·`artificial_replay=True`·no_auto_merge)·`run_db_identity_smoke` 에 link reason 분포 추가·CLI `--time-series-replay`. `real_source_smoke_report.py`: `classify_adjudication_block_reason`(§5 순수 분류기: db_not_reached/none/semantic_link_without_adjudication/non_publishable_role/no_fingerprint_overlap/no_cross_batch_overlap)·`assemble_activation_report` 에 smoke_mode/artificial_replay/batches/identity_link_reason_distribution/adjudication_status_distribution/semantic_cross_batch_candidates/adjudication_block_reason 추가·`_next_actions` replay 경고.
**측정(실데이터·정직)** — **artificial time-series replay**(`event_intel_test` head 0009·TRUNCATE 격리·live-PG 테스트 잠금): 2배치 → **created 2 · semantic_cross_batch_candidate link 1 · adjudications 1(likely_same_event 1) · event_count 0→2 · no_auto_merge=True** — **cross-batch adjudication substrate 가 같은-사건·다른-URL·교차배치 데이터에서 닫힘을 실데이터로 입증**. 단일소스(ADR#55)의 block reason = `no_cross_batch_overlap` 로 정확 귀속. 테스트: 신규/확장 **15**(unit 12[replay 빌더 3·block-reason 6·replay report 3]+live-PG 3[replay→semantic+adjudication·block none·safe-target gate])·smoke 2파일 unit **51 passed**·**backend 비-live 559 passed/4 skipped/0 failed(965s)**·live-PG **94 passed**(91→94)·ingestion **1353**·frontend tsc0/test12/lint0·secret scan PASS·docs_lifecycle conflicts 0.
**옵션 A/D(§3)** — **A(multi-source 실 fetch)**: key-free 공식 레지스트리(federal_register)와 뉴스는 event-space/domain 이 달라 bounded fetch 에서 같은-사건 overlap 이 구조적으로 희소 → **정직 분해만**(allowlist gate 유지·깨지기 쉬운 스크레이퍼 미구현·source scarcity 를 모델 실패로 단순화하지 않음). **D(LLM/Agent)** 본경로 금지(readiness 조건 3 evidence 만 ADR#56 replay 로 보강·여전히 No-Go[1·4·5·7]).
**결과** — **R-RealSourceLoopUnproven 부분진전**(단계 5[stage③ adjudication]을 artificial replay 로 실데이터 도달·block-reason 분해)·**R-LiveIdentityBacklog 부분진전**(백로그가 채워지는 조건[동일사건·다른-URL·교차배치]을 실데이터 입증·"왜 0/N 인가" source/data/fingerprint/cross-batch 귀속). 신규 RISK 미등록(replay validity/coverage 는 기존 RISK 의 gap·RISK 남발 금지).
**한계** — **artificial_replay=True ≠ 실 source behavior**(실 동일사건 다중소스/시계열 fetch 로 재확인 필요)·실 cross-source 비뉴스 Event·운영 DB 배포·주기 스케줄러 실가동·reviewer/gold/merge·LLM 본경로 잔여(production 백로그 0 불변·완전종결 금지). substrate 입증(능력)≠production 운영(actuality).
**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/{real_source_identity_smoke,real_source_smoke_report}.py`·`backend/tests/{test_real_source_identity_smoke,test_real_source_smoke_report,test_event_resolution_live_pg}.py`·`docs/2_ROADMAP/{00_ROADMAP_INDEX,15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP}.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/{RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS,INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT}.md`·`docs/_CANONICAL/02_CURRENT_ARCHITECTURE.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#55.

### [#57] source overlap discovery — 실 cross-source overlap 다입도 분해 + GDELT 429 blocker 실측(write-free·no-merge·LLM 호출 0·production 백로그 0)
- 날짜: 2026-06-25 · 섹터: real-source loop / cross-source same-event overlap discovery / source quality·agent orchestration substrate · 상태: **R-RealSourceLoopUnproven·R-LiveIdentityBacklog 부분진전·R-SourceOverlapScarcity 신규·완전종결=OVERCLAIM·옵션 A+B+C 채택·D docs/schema only·E 금지**

**문제(§2 통찰)** — ADR#56 artificial replay 가 cross-batch adjudication substrate 를 닫았으나 **실 source behavior 가 아니다**. 다음 hard blocker = 실 동일사건 다중소스 overlap 을 재현하거나, 안 되면 원인을 수치 분해. 핵심 발견: 결정론 cross-batch identity 는 `semantic_identity_fingerprint`(**정확 token-set 일치 + date bucket**·≥4 토큰·고정밀 저재현)만 인정 → 실제 다른 매체의 같은 사건 헤드라인은 paraphrase 되어 token-set 정확 불일치 → **overlap 이 존재해도 deterministic fingerprint 사각지대**. within-batch 약신호(Jaccard≥0.8)와 달리 cross-batch 는 정확 일치만(false-merge 0).
**원자 분석(§2·20문항)** — substrate 정독(file:line): `event_resolution_pipeline.resolve_and_apply_cluster:98–140`(semantic link 생성 조건)·`event_timeline_service.{find_event_candidates_by_fingerprint,map_event_candidate_fingerprints}`(fingerprint claim/match)·`cross_source_dedup.semantic_identity_fingerprint:102–118`·`source_content_type`(role 분리). 2-agent 소스 레지스트리·fetch 인프라 조사: **key-free 검증 anchor 는 federal_register 단 1·GDELT 만 다출처 same-event overlap 생성(429 제약·R-Gdelt429)·공식↔공식 1문서=1URL=1event 비중첩·community=reaction layer non-publishable·뉴스 HTML 미allowlist**. 20문항 전부 코드 근거로 답(보고).
**옵션 결정(§3)** — (A) real same-event discovery probe (B) source overlap planning matrix (C) bounded time-window polling (D) LLM-assisted suggestion (E) production DB. **선택: A 채택(GDELT bounded·opt-in 실 fetch + write-free discovery)+B 채택(overlap_potential_matrix + agent orchestration schema)+C 부분채택(GDELT timespan·실패 시 분류)+D docs/schema only(near_match_below_fingerprint 분해로 LLM/adjudicator 영역 명문화·실 LLM 호출 0)·E 금지.** ADR#57 기록.
**구현** — 신규 `backend/app/tools/source_overlap_discovery.py`(write-free·no-DB·no-merge): `discover_overlap`(다입도 pairwise — `fingerprint_overlap`[deterministic 검출] vs `near_match_below_fingerprint`[adjudicator/LLM 영역]·canonical/date/title-token overlap·`possible_same_event_pairs`·`overlap_potential_matrix`·`block_reasons`)·`build_captured_overlap_fixture`(옵션 C sanitized·본문 미저장·verbatim wire 2+paraphrase 2+대조 1+community 1)·`parse_gdelt_articles`/`fetch_gdelt_overlap_records`(GDELT bounded·key-free·transport 주입 결정론·실패 분류 rate_limited/network_error/parser_error/no_records)·`build_agent_orchestration_schema`(§9·recommended_pairs/expected_overlap_reason/source_role_constraints/uncertainty/`no_merge_without_gate`/`no_public_intelligence_unit`/`llm_invoked=False`/next_fetch_plan)·CLI(`--live-gdelt` opt-in). `real_source_smoke_report.build_source_quality_matrix` §8 추가(overlap_potential·*_utility·community_reaction_layer_eligible·identity/adjudication/packet_failure_reason).
**측정(실데이터·정직)** — **실 GDELT bounded fetch 시도(`--live-gdelt`·query="port strike"·timespan=7d) → `rate_limited`(429·R-Gdelt429 발현) → captured fixture fallback**(`real_fetch=False` 정직 표면화). captured fixture(sanitized·본문 미저장): **possible_same_event 6 = fingerprint 1(verbatim wire) + near 5(paraphrase)** → deterministic 은 **1/6 만 검출**·5/6 은 adjudicator-zone(deterministic 사각지대). overlap_potential_matrix 10 pair(community 제외)·deterministic_detectable 1·adjudicator_zone_only 5·no_overlap 4. 테스트: 신규/확장 **34**(test_source_overlap_discovery **30**[overlap 분해·block-reason 6·GDELT parse/실패 분류·agent schema·fingerprint 근거]+test_real_source_smoke_report §8 매트릭스 **4**)·backend 비-live **593 passed/4 skipped/0 failed(959s)**·live-PG **94 passed**(단독)·ingestion **1353 passed**·frontend tsc0/test12/lint0·secret scan PASS(265)·docs_lifecycle conflicts 0. **자동 병합 0 불변.** (live-PG 1차 실행은 backend 스위트와 동시 실행으로 공유 `event_intel_test` 오염→`test_live_concurrent_create_no_orphan` false-fail[기대 1·실측 5]·**단독 재실행 94 green** — write-free 변경은 동시성 경로 무관 확정.)
**결과** — **R-RealSourceLoopUnproven 부분진전**(실 overlap 을 다입도 수치 분해·실 GDELT 시도→429 실측·"왜 안 닫히는가"를 source/fingerprint/coverage/provider 로 귀속)·**R-LiveIdentityBacklog 부분진전**(백로그 충원 source 의 구조적 희소성 분해)·**R-SourceOverlapScarcity 신규 등재**(key-free 실 cross-source overlap 구조적 희소·실 blocker — 미래 희망 아님). RISK 남발 금지(replay/coverage validity 는 기존 gap).
**한계** — **실 GDELT overlap 미관측(429)·captured fixture/합성 ≠ 실 source overlap**·paraphrase overlap 검출은 adjudicator(embedding/LLM·MERGE_GATE·gold) 영역 미충족·운영 DB·reviewer/gold/merge·LLM 본경로 잔여(production 백로그 0 불변·완전종결 금지). discovery(능력)≠실 운영 overlap(actuality).
**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/{source_overlap_discovery,real_source_smoke_report}.py`·`backend/tests/{test_source_overlap_discovery,test_real_source_smoke_report}.py`·`docs/2_ROADMAP/{00_ROADMAP_INDEX,15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP}.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/{RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS,INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT}.md`·`docs/_CANONICAL/02_CURRENT_ARCHITECTURE.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#56.

### [#58] real overlap acquisition strategy — GDELT governance 재사용 + key-free RSS governed fetch(실측) + acquisition planning matrix + near-match reviewer route(핵심)
- 날짜: 2026-06-25 · 섹터: real overlap acquisition / provider governance / source-pair planning / near-match→reviewer route / source quality matrix · 상태: **R-RealSourceLoopUnproven·R-LiveIdentityBacklog·R-SourceOverlapScarcity 부분진전·R-Gdelt429 부분진전·완전종결=OVERCLAIM·옵션 A+B+C+D(report) 채택·E 금지·near-match route 채택(detection 레이어 재구성)**

**문제(§2 통찰·디렉티브 전제 재구성)** — ADR#57 의 GDELT 429 근인은 "GDELT 가 막혔다"가 아니라 **backend 도구가 기존 governance 를 우회한 raw httpx** 였다. ingestion 에는 이미 성숙한 2계층 rate 인프라(`HostRateGate`[host floor·shared host_rate_gate.json·cross-process]·`rate_limit_policy.yaml`[gdelt min 60s·cooldown_on_429 900s·max_retries 1]·`source_strategy_memory`[gdelt `EXTERNAL_RATE_LIMITED_PENDING_RESUME`·`respect_cooldown`·`no_bypass`·`never_disable_on_single_429`])가 존재. `retry_policy.retry_on` 에 `RATE_LIMITED` 부재 → tight-retry 는 구조적으로 이미 차단. **진짜 overlap 생성원도 GDELT 보다 이미 검증된 key-free RSS 함대**(`_SERVICE_CONFIGS` auth=none·source_registry 등재·ingestion 수집 중 — yna/hankyung/maekyung/aljazeera/bbc/the_verge/techcrunch/cnbc 등; 이번 실 smoke `_RSS_OVERLAP_SOURCES`=**영문 4개 bbc/aljazeera/the_verge/techcrunch**).
**원자 분석(§2·20문항)** — governance 인프라(`ingestion/orchestration/host_rate_gate.py`·`ingestion/core/{rate_limit_policy,retry_policy,error_taxonomy}.py`·`ingestion/probes/api_probe.py`·`source_strategy_memory.yaml`)+소스 레지스트리(`_SERVICE_CONFIGS`·57 source·21 key-free·RSS endpoint auth=none)+near-match reviewer 재사용 경로(`export_identity_eval_pairs.collect_adjudication_eval_pairs`→`identity_human_labeling.build_labeling_packet`·`EvalPair`/`LabelingPacketItem` 스키마 near-match 수용·predicted_status 차단 `_PACKET_FORBIDDEN_VERDICT_KEYS`) 정독. 20문항 코드 근거 답+사용자 확인(범위 A+B+C+D 전부·near-match route 핵심 채택).
**옵션 결정(§3)** — (A) GDELT provider hardening (B) key-free RSS/news allowlist expansion (C) acquisition planning matrix (D) near-match reviewer candidate route (E) production DB. **선택: A+B+C+D(report-only)·E 금지.** 단 분석 재구성: A=**새 retry 코드 0·기존 governance honor**, B=**기존 RSS 함대 governed 실 fetch**(새 스크레이퍼 0), D=**핵심 deliverable**(paraphrase 사각지대를 reviewer/gold 로). ADR#58 기록.
**구현(새 파일 0·기존 도구 확장)** — `source_overlap_discovery.py`: **(A)** `gdelt_provider_status`(read-only preflight·network 0·write 0 — HostRateGate.decide+`in_cooldown`+`load_rate_limit_policy` honor·blocked→fetch 미시도)·`fetch_gdelt_overlap_records` short-circuit(provider_status≠ok→network 0·우회 재발 차단). **(B)** `parse_rss_items`(stdlib ET·RSS/Atom·RFC822→ISO·본문 미저장)·`fetch_rss_overlap_records`(registry endpoint[key-free 만]·shared host gate 참여·bounded·failure 분류[network/rate_limited/parser/no_records/no_endpoint]·transport 주입 결정론). **(C)** `build_acquisition_plan`(source_pair_plan/topic_window_plan/time_window_plan·expected_overlap_utility·LLM 0·no_merge_without_gate). **(D)** `discover_overlap` near_match_pairs 캡처 + `build_near_match_reviewer_candidates`(label=unlabeled·predicted_status **미포함**·publishable×publishable 만·`no_merge_without_gold`). `assemble_acquisition_report`(§4 필드). `real_source_smoke_report.py` §9: `_ROLE_UTILITY` title_paraphrase_risk/overlap_acquisition_utility/cross_source_pairability/same_event_likelihood/body_policy + `_acquisition_profile`(provider_accessibility/rate_limit_risk/robots_tos_status·하드 근거만·나머지 unknown)+agent_next_action.
**검증(실측 — 핵심 정직 결과)** — **실 RSS smoke 성공(network·429 0)**: bbc/aljazeera/the_verge/techcrunch **55 record**(전부 ok·canonical 55·published 55)·same-beat tech(the_verge+techcrunch) **30 record** → **cross-source overlap 0(`no_title_overlap`)**. 즉 **governance 재사용은 검증(RSS 는 429 안 남·GDELT 우회와 대조)·실 same-event overlap 은 untargeted feed 에서 구조적으로 희소**(R-SourceOverlapScarcity 실데이터 확증). captured fixture/transport-RSS 에서 near-match route 결정론 입증(paraphrase 5→reviewer candidate 5·예: bbc "Major port strike…nationwide" vs aljazeera "Port strike…nationwide today" jaccard 0.778). 테스트 신규/확장 **32**(discovery +24·report §9 +8)·discovery+report **93 passed**·backend 비-live **622 passed/4 skipped/0 failed(962s full run)** + 감사-정정 3 테스트(targeted 재실행 green·source_overlap_discovery 는 자기 테스트만 import→격리) = **effective 625**·live-PG **94 passed(217s·단독)**·ingestion **1353 passed**·frontend **tsc0/test12/lint0**·secret PASS·docs_lifecycle 0.
**감사(§15)** — adversarial-reality-critic **PROCEED·HIGH 0**(안전계약 4종 VALID·정직 경계 유지·RISK 과대종결 0·fabrication 0)·MEDIUM 2+LOW 1 **정정**: ① near-match candidate risk_tags=`paraphrase`(다운스트림 `assign_candidate_bucket` 인식 토큰→`paraphrase` bucket 분류·"스키마 정합" claim 코드로 참 — MEDIUM-1) ② CLI live-rss `HostRateGate` 주입(shared gate 실제 참여·MEDIUM-2) ③ ADR 본문 RSS 목록을 코드 `_RSS_OVERLAP_SOURCES`(영문 4개)와 일치(LOW-1). code-review **CONFIRMED 1+PLAUSIBLE 1 정정**: ④ `parse_rss_items` Atom 다중 `<link>` rel=alternate 우선(self 오캡처 방지·`the_verge` Atom·[1] 중) ⑤ `gdelt_provider_status` cooldown 비-2-튜플 ValueError 방어([2] 낮). 정정 회귀 테스트 3 추가.
**RISK(§11)** — 종결 0. R-RealSourceLoopUnproven 부분진전(429 근인=우회 규명·governance 재사용 배선·실 RSS fetch 검증)·R-LiveIdentityBacklog 부분진전(near-match route 로 paraphrase 사각지대 충원 통로)·R-SourceOverlapScarcity 부분진전(다출처 RSS 55 record→overlap 0 실측 분해·source_pair/time/topic plan·near-match reviewer route·overlap_acquisition_utility 수치화)·R-Gdelt429 부분진전(provider preflight·cooldown honor·no-retry-storm·fallback=RSS). **완전종결 금지**(실 deterministic overlap 미관측·운영 DB·gold/merge·production 백로그 0 불변).
**다음 hard blocker(재구성)** — GDELT provider 정책이 아니라 **targeted same-event acquisition**(RSS 고정 feed 는 query 불가·GDELT query 가능하나 429): topic/time-windowed query-capable provider 가 실 near-match 후보 생성의 게이트 → 그 후 **detection 레이어**(embedding/LLM adjudicator + 실 gold·MERGE_GATE)가 paraphrase 사각지대를 닫는다.
**한계** — **실 cross-source same-event overlap 미관측**(다출처 RSS 55 record→0·합성 fixture ≠ 실 overlap)·deterministic fingerprint 는 paraphrase 구조적 미검출·near-match route 는 reviewer/gold 전 단계(병합 0·LLM 0)·운영 DB·scheduler·reviewer/gold/merge·LLM 본경로 잔여(production 백로그 0 불변). acquisition 검증(능력)≠실 overlap 확보(actuality).
**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/{source_overlap_discovery,real_source_smoke_report}.py`·`backend/tests/{test_source_overlap_discovery,test_real_source_smoke_report}.py`·`docs/2_ROADMAP/{00_ROADMAP_INDEX,15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP}.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/{RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS,INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT}.md`·`docs/_CANONICAL/02_CURRENT_ARCHITECTURE.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#57.

### [#59] near-match reviewer/gold queue operationalization — paraphrase 사각지대를 운영 reviewer/gold 큐로(병합 0·LLM 0·predicted_status 숨김·실 gold 0)
- 날짜: 2026-06-25 · 섹터: semantic identity / near-match reviewer queue / human labeling·gold·reviewer agreement / source acquisition linkage / agent orchestration substrate · 상태: **R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator·R-IdentityHumanLabeling·R-ReviewerAgreement·R-GoldSamplingBias·R-LiveIdentityBacklog·R-SourceOverlapScarcity 부분진전·완전종결=OVERCLAIM·옵션 A+B 채택·C bounded linkage·D No-Go 인터페이스·E 금지·신규 RISK 0**

**문제(§2 통찰)** — ADR#58 이 정직하게 드러낸 한계: untargeted RSS 는 same-event cross-source overlap 0·deterministic fingerprint 는 paraphrase(다른 매체 같은 사건)를 못 잡음(`near_match_below_fingerprint`). 그 paraphrase 후보를 **버리지도 병합하지도 않고** 운영 가능한 reviewer/gold 큐로 보내야 detection 레이어가 닫힌다(reviewer 큐≠병합·predicted_status 숨김·LLM 0).
**원자 분석(§2·20문항)** — 3-agent 서브시스템 매핑(labeling/eval/gold·MERGE_GATE/adjudicator·source-role)+핵심 파일 정독(file:line): `build_near_match_reviewer_candidates`(worksheet-row 모양·packet/gold 머신과 **코드 미연결**·predicted_status 부재)·`build_labeling_packet`(il:1062)·`assign_candidate_bucket`(il:923·`paraphrase`/`hard_negative` bucket)·`validate_labeling_packet`(il:1116·`_PACKET_FORBIDDEN_VERDICT_KEYS` verdict 차단·language/source_type enum)·`labeler_facing_view`(il:1100·bucket+판정 제거)·`resolve_gold_from_reviewers`(il:587·2+합의=gold·conflict→`adjudication_queue_from_resolved` human-only)·`EvalPair`(label∈GOLD_LABELS→"unlabeled" 직접변환 불가·라벨 후 물질화). 20문항 코드 근거로 답(보고). 다음 hard blocker 순서=① targeted same-event acquisition(큐를 채움) ② gold label volume(calibrate) ③ embedding/LLM adjudicator(gated·gold 없이 hallucination merge 위험).
**옵션 결정(§3)** — (A) near-match reviewer queue operationalization (B) gold seed packet (C) targeted acquisition (D) embedding/LLM adjudicator (E) production DB. **선택: A+B 채택·C bounded acquisition linkage 만·D No-Go 인터페이스 문서화만·E 금지.** ADR#59 기록.
**구현(새 파일 1·기존 머신 재사용·재구현 0)** — 신규 `near_match_reviewer_queue.py`(오케스트레이터): `build_near_match_reviewer_queue`(near positive[paraphrase]+hard negative 정규화[language und→unknown·observed None→''·title str≤512]→`build_labeling_packet`→`validate_labeling_packet` fail-loud→검증된 packet+`labeler_facing_view`)·`build_synthetic_hard_negative_candidates`(trap-zone·**synthetic_fixture 명시**·분리 카운트)·`build_gold_seed_report`(queue/near/hard/fingerprint count·source_role·bucket·uncertainty·`reviewer_packet_exportable`·`labeler_prediction_hidden`·`gold_ready`[실 gold만]·`merge_allowed=False`)·`resolve_queue_gold`(`resolve_gold_from_reviewers`→gold/conflict adjudication queue/agreement connector)·`build_reviewer_queue_acquisition_linkage`(source_pair별 near_match_yield/reviewer/gold/hard_negative value·paraphrase_risk·`next_fetch_plan`→목적 기반 수집)·`augment_agent_schema_with_reviewer_queue`(near_match_queue_priority·hard_negative_sampling_plan·expected_gold/merge_gate_value·`EMBEDDING_LLM_ADJUDICATOR_INTERFACE` **No-Go**[output=provisional_score only·requires=gold+MERGE_GATE+adversarial·`semantic_score` seam])·CLI. `source_overlap_discovery.py`: `_HARD_NEG_FLOOR=0.2`+`discover_overlap` hard_negative_pairs 밴드 포착(publishable·same-date·cross-URL·jaccard [0.2,near) different-event lean)+`build_hard_negative_reviewer_candidates`(risk_tags=hard_negative) **순수 가산**(ADR#57/58 수치 불변: captured fixture fingerprint 1·near 5). honesty 봉인: worksheet `dataset_source`(live_derived/synthetic_fixture) 명시→`summarize_packet_sampling`(기본 live) 오집계 차단.
**검증(결정론·LLM 0·실측)** — captured fixture queue: near 5(paraphrase bucket·10 assignments)+synthetic hard 3(hard_negative bucket·6 assignments)·`labeler_facing_view` 에 sampling_bucket/predicted_status **부재**·gold_ready False·merge_allowed False·llm_invoked False·embedding No-Go. gold 경로 입증(synthetic human label): 2+합의→gold·conflict→adjudication queue·single→insufficient·human adjudication→gold. 신규/확장 테스트 **34**(near-match queue 30[§9 28+dataset_source 봉인 2]+discovery hard-neg 4)·discovery+queue **88 passed**·backend 비-live **657 passed/4 skipped/0 failed(961s full run·LOW 정정 이전)**+dataset_source 봉인 2(near_match_reviewer_queue.py 자기 테스트만 import→격리·targeted 재실행 30 green)=**effective 659**·live-PG **94 passed(215s·단독)**·ingestion **1353 passed(27.9s)**·frontend **tsc0/test12/lint0**·secret PASS(10)·docs_lifecycle conflicts 0·ruff 실게이트(E/F/I/B/W) 0[UP045 noise 는 기존 49건과 일관·codebase Optional 스타일].
**감사(§14)** — adversarial-reality-critic **PROCEED·HIGH 0·MEDIUM 0**(claim A–H 8개 중 7 코드 증거 VALID·honesty boundary **구조적**[merge/persist 경로 grep ZERO·predicted_status 4중 차단·source role guard 이중·hard-neg=stratum(단정 아님·gold label 있어야 음성)·synthetic 완전 분리·gold_ready 정직·discover_overlap 순수 가산·RISK partial 정직]). **LOW 2 정정**: ① `_to_worksheet_row` `dataset_source` 명시→synthetic 이 `summarize_packet_sampling`(기본 live)에서 live 오집계되는 latent hazard 봉인(회귀 테스트 2) ② "음성 floor 채운다"→"calibration substrate(통계 floor 충족 아님)" 톤다운. code-review **0 결함**([]·10 초점 전부 검증·benign edge[near_jaccard<floor 시 hard-neg 밴드 도달불가·실사용 무발생] noted·코드변경 불요).
**RISK(§10)** — 종결 0·신규 0(total 36 불변). 부분진전: R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator(paraphrase 사각지대→reviewer/gold 큐·embedding/LLM No-Go 인터페이스)·R-IdentityHumanLabeling(near-match→packet 운영 큐+hard negative+gold seed report)·R-ReviewerAgreement(hard negative calibration substrate+resolve_queue_gold connector)·R-GoldSamplingBias(near positive+hard negative 균형 표집+dataset_source 봉인)·R-LiveIdentityBacklog(통로→운영 큐 물질화)·R-SourceOverlapScarcity(acquisition linkage 목적 기반 수집). 디렉티브 신규 RISK 후보(R-NearMatchFalsePositive/R-NearMatchReviewerQueue/R-AgentGoldAcquisitionPlanning)는 **독립 blocker 아님**(near-match 는 자동행동 아닌 reviewer 질문·route 미배선·reviewer 충원 0→adversarial 도 등재 불요 판정)→R-SourceOverlapScarcity·R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator 에 포섭(RISK 남발 금지). **완전종결 금지**(실 reviewer/gold 0·운영 DB·embedding/LLM adjudicator·production 백로그 0 불변).
**다음 hard blocker** — ① **targeted same-event acquisition**(query-capable provider·untargeted RSS overlap 0→큐가 빔) → ② **gold label volume**(reviewer 충원·실 라벨→MERGE_GATE 평가 가능) → ③ **embedding/LLM adjudicator**(gold calibration 후·gated). 큐는 ①과 ② 사이 substrate 를 놓고 ③을 No-Go 로 고정.
**한계** — **실 reviewer/gold 0**(큐는 substrate·packet≠gold·synthetic human label 은 경로 입증용)·실 cross-source overlap 미관측(captured fixture·near positive 0 환경에선 큐 빔)·embedding/LLM adjudicator 미구현(No-Go 인터페이스만)·운영 DB·production 백로그 0 불변. 큐 운영성(능력)≠실 gold(actuality).
**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/{near_match_reviewer_queue,source_overlap_discovery}.py`·`backend/tests/{test_near_match_reviewer_queue,test_source_overlap_discovery}.py`·`docs/2_ROADMAP/{00_ROADMAP_INDEX,15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP}.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/{RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS,INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT}.md`·`docs/_CANONICAL/02_CURRENT_ARCHITECTURE.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#58.

### [#60] targeted same-event acquisition → near-match reviewer/gold operating readiness — captured fixture 큐를 targeted acquisition 과 연결(병합 0·LLM 0·실 reviewer/gold 0)
- 날짜: 2026-06-25 · 섹터: targeted same-event acquisition / near-match queue population / reviewer operating packet readiness / gold calibration simulation / source acquisition linkage / agent orchestration substrate · 상태: **R-SourceOverlapScarcity·R-IdentityHumanLabeling·R-ReviewerAgreement·R-GoldSamplingBias·R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator·R-LiveIdentityBacklog 부분진전·완전종결=OVERCLAIM·옵션 A+B+C 채택·D interface/eval plan 만(No-Go)·E 금지·신규 RISK 0**

**문제(§2 통찰)** — ADR#59 near-match reviewer/gold 큐는 **captured fixture 수준에서 멈춤**·untargeted RSS 는 same-event overlap 0(ADR#58). 큐를 **targeted same-event acquisition**(source-pair·topic·time-window) 결과와 연결해 실 near-match 후보를 채울 운영 경로를 닫아야 detection 레이어가 작동한다(자동 병합·LLM 본경로·운영 DB 배포 턴 아님).
**원자 분석(§2·20문항)** — 3-agent 서브시스템 매핑(source registry/fingerprint·labeling/gold·IU/API/frontend/readiness)+핵심 파일 정독: 파이프라인 부품(`fetch_rss/gdelt_overlap_records`·`discover_overlap`·`build_near_match_reviewer_queue`)은 **이미 존재**하나 **셋을 잇는 orchestrator·§4 output 부재**(`near_match_reviewer_queue.main` 은 captured fixture 만). 오늘의 query 현실(Q4~6): GDELT 만 key-free topic query 가능하나 **429 cooldown**·RSS 는 topic query 불가(time/source-pair targeting 만)·나머지 key 필요 → 실 targeted near-match yield 낮음(다음 hard blocker=targeted acquisition).
**옵션 결정(§3)** — (A) targeted acquisition→queue population (B) reviewer operating packet readiness (C) gold calibration simulation (D) embedding/LLM adjudicator (E) production DB. **선택: A+B+C 채택·D interface/eval plan 만(No-Go 유지)·E 금지.** ADR#60 기록.
**구현(새 파일 1·기존 머신 전부 재사용·재구현 0)** — 신규 `targeted_same_event_acquisition.py`: `build_provider_capability_matrix`(query_capability/status/rate_limit_risk/fallback — 오늘의 정직한 현실)·`build_targeted_acquisition_plan`(source-pair·topic·time-window)·`build_targeted_same_event_fixture`(중앙은행 금리결정 topic·실 `_title_tokens`/`_jaccard`/`semantic_identity_fingerprint` 로 band 수치검증: near 2·hard 3·fingerprint 1·**synthetic_fixture 명시·실 후보 아님**)·`run_targeted_acquisition`(주입 records>governed fetch>fixture→`discover_overlap`·실 0후보면 block_reason 정직)·`build_targeted_acquisition_report`(§4: acquisition_run_id·source_pair_plan·topic/time_window·candidate/near/hard/fingerprint count·reviewer_packet_exportable·labeler_prediction_hidden·gold_ready·agreement/conflict_queue_ready·merge_allowed False·dataset_source·honesty_boundary)·`build_reviewer_operating_checklist`(§5·hidden_prediction/raw_body absent **구조적 verify**·reviewer_instruction·allowed_labels·conflict/agreement/adjudication/gold_promotion/merge_policy)·`simulate_gold_calibration`(§6·synthetic label 로 unanimous/conflict/single/adjudicated 입증·**production_gold_count=0**)·`build_targeted_acquisition_linkage`(§8·expected near/hard/gold yield·reviewer_load·query_capability/provider_status/rate_limit_risk/fallback)·`build_targeted_agent_schema`(§9·agent_can_plan/agent_cannot·embedding No-Go)·CLI(기본 fixture·network 0). **honesty 코드 강제**: `_SYNTHETIC_FIXTURE_MARKER`→synthetic fixture record 는 real_fetch=True 여도 live_derived 도장 불가.
**검증(결정론·LLM 0·실측)** — fixture readiness: candidate 5(near 2+hard 3)·fingerprint 1·packet_exportable True·labeler_prediction_hidden True·gold_ready **False**(실 gold 0)·gold_sim simulated_gold 3/conflict 1/insufficient 1/**production_gold 0**·checklist hidden/raw verify True. real RSS transport(주입)→near≥1·dataset_source live_derived(fixture 와 정직 구분). 신규 테스트 **57**(§10 1-49+실 fetch provenance+adversarial 음성 가드 M1/M1b/M2b/M2c/M2d/M2e/M3 7). backend 비-live **716 passed/4 skipped/0 failed**(background 709+신규 57 additive·기존 파일 미수정)·live-PG **94 passed**(write-free·무영향)·ingestion **1353 passed**·frontend **tsc0/lint0/test12**·secret PASS·ruff 실게이트(E/F/I/B/W) 0.
**감사(§14)** — adversarial-reality-critic **PROCEED-WITH-FIXES**(production_gold=0 봉인·synthetic≠live 봉인·community anchor 차단·near/hard/fp 산술 실측·verify 계산값 전부 VALID). **HIGH-1**(ADR#60 docs 미등재)→본 갱신으로 해소. **MEDIUM-1**(synthetic+real_fetch=True seam)·**MEDIUM-2**(honesty 음성 케이스 미테스트)→**코드 강제(`_SYNTHETIC_FIXTURE_MARKER`)+음성 테스트 7 추가**. code-review(10 angle): **host_gate 미전달 GDELT(ADR#57 우회 회귀·3 finder 공통)** 정정·candidate_count 이름 분리(discovery_candidate_count)·fixture topic 라벨 일치·near_jaccard 死파라미터 제거·fixture 대체 정직 노출(block_reason)·reaction 중복 제거.
**RISK(§11)** — 종결 0·신규 0. 부분진전: R-SourceOverlapScarcity(targeted acquisition→queue 연결·provider capability 현실)·R-IdentityHumanLabeling(reviewer operating checklist·실 reviewer 직전)·R-ReviewerAgreement(gold path 5경로 simulation)·R-GoldSamplingBias(near+hard 균형·dataset_source 봉인·production_gold 0)·R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator(near→reviewer/gold 운영 경로·embedding No-Go)·R-LiveIdentityBacklog(captured fixture→targeted acquisition 연결). 신규 RISK 후보(R-ReviewerOpsReadiness/R-NearMatchQueuePopulation/R-GoldCalibrationReadiness)는 **독립 blocker 아님**→기존 RISK 에 포섭(남발 금지). **완전종결 금지**(실 reviewer/gold 0·실 targeted near-match 후보 0·embedding/LLM adjudicator·운영 DB·production 백로그 0 불변).
**다음 hard blocker** — ① **query-capable provider 확보**(GDELT 429 우회 또는 key-required provider key — 실 targeted near-match 후보 생성의 전제) → ② **real reviewer 충원**(실 라벨→gold→MERGE_GATE) → ③ **embedding/LLM adjudicator**(gold calibration 후·gated). 큐/checklist/gold-sim 은 ①·② 사이 운영 준비를 닫고 ③을 No-Go 로 고정.
**한계** — **실 targeted near-match 후보 0**(GDELT 429·RSS topic 불가·fixture=운영 경로 입증이지 실 데이터 아님)·**실 reviewer/gold 0**(synthetic label=경로 검증·packet≠gold·production_gold 0)·embedding/LLM adjudicator 미구현(No-Go interface)·운영 DB·production 백로그 0 불변. 운영 readiness(능력)≠실 gold(actuality).
**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/targeted_same_event_acquisition.py`·`backend/tests/test_targeted_same_event_acquisition.py`·`docs/2_ROADMAP/{00_ROADMAP_INDEX,15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP}.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/{RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS,INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT}.md`·`docs/_CANONICAL/02_CURRENT_ARCHITECTURE.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#59.

### [#61] query-capable provider acquisition readiness gate — provider 가용성 분류 + optional bounded live query + queue population(병합 0·LLM 0·운영 DB 0·실 후보 0)
- 날짜: 2026-06-25 · 섹터: provider acquisition readiness / credential(secret-safe) gate / host-gate·429 readiness / optional live query / near-match queue population(live_derived) / agent orchestration substrate · 상태: **R-SourceOverlapScarcity·R-RealSourceLoopUnproven·R-LiveIdentityBacklog·R-IdentityHumanLabeling·R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator·R-Gdelt429 부분진전·완전종결=OVERCLAIM·옵션 A+B+C+D 채택·E/F 금지·신규 RISK 0**

**문제(§2 통찰)** — ADR#60 가 남긴 정직한 한계: targeted same-event acquisition 의 detection-layer 운영 경로는 닫혔으나 **실 near-match 후보 0** — 그 직접 원인은 queue 실패가 아니라 **query-capable provider acquisition failure**(분석 §2-Q20). 후보가 0 에서 멈추지 않도록 provider 확보 가능성·env readiness·fallback·blocked/no-provider report·optional live candidate population 을 안전하게 닫아야 한다(자동 병합·scheduler persist·semantic merge·LLM 본경로·운영 DB 배포 턴 아님).
**원자 분석(§2·20문항·3-agent 병렬)** — provider inventory/credential·host-gate/429·live-smoke/queue 재사용을 매핑: ① query-capable key-free=gdelt(429)·sec_edgar·federal_register **3개뿐**·나머지 query 는 key 필요 ② credential 체크 secret-safe 단일 출처=`env_loader.env_status`(present/missing·값 0·alias 해소) ③ `.env.example` query provider placeholder **이미 완비**(누락=X/Twitter disabled→불요) ④ GDELT 429 견고(`gdelt_provider_status`=HostRateGate+in_cooldown 합성·no-tight-retry 구조적) ⑤ RSS topic 불가 반영됨 ⑥ 실 fetcher 는 `run_targeted_acquisition` 에 **gdelt/rss 만 배선**(sec_edgar/federal_register/news API 미배선) ⑦ provenance 봉인=real_fetch 단일 boolean+`_SYNTHETIC_FIXTURE_MARKER`.
**옵션 결정(§3)** — (A) provider readiness gate (B) optional live query (C) credential/runbook docs (D) live candidate→queue population (E) embedding/LLM adjudicator runtime (F) production DB activation. **선택: A+B+C+D 채택·E/F 금지.** ADR#61 기록.
**구현(새 파일 1·ADR#60 frozen·단방향 import·재구현 0)** — 신규 `provider_readiness.py`: curated query-capability catalog(11 query provider+rss_fleet·각 source_ids/query_capability/auth/required_env_vars[실 os.getenv 이름]/host/robots_tos/raw_body_policy)·`build_provider_readiness_report`(§5·key_free_query/key_required_query/key_free_non_query/blocked_rate_limited/disabled/unknown 분류 + credential[env_status]·host_gate_status[gdelt_provider_status]·rate_limit_policy·next_action·buckets[query_capable/key_free_ready/key_required_missing/blocked/unknown])·**honest `fetch_implemented` gate**(실 fetcher=gdelt/rss 만→미배선 provider 는 credential-ready 여도 `fetcher_not_wired`·live query 시 fixture 둔갑 코드 차단·dataset_source None)·`run_optional_live_query`(§6·opt-in flag+safe+credential+fetcher gated→ADR#60 `run_targeted_same_event_operating_readiness` 재사용·live_derived 후보→near-match queue·실패 분류 missing_credentials/provider_rate_limited/host_gate_blocked/fetcher_not_wired/no_records/no_near_match)·`run_provider_acquisition_readiness`(§4 통합 output 단일 dict)·`build_provider_readiness_agent_schema`(§9·agent_can_plan/agent_cannot·no_secret_fabrication·embedding No-Go)·CLI(기본 readiness·network 0·--live-query opt-in).
**검증(결정론·LLM 0·network 0·실측)** — 신규 테스트 **43**(§10 provider readiness 1-10·optional live query 11-20·live candidate queue 21-28·runbook/env 29·32·33·agent contract 34-39·통합/회귀 40-43+rss_fleet 정규화/source_ids 회귀 44-45; transport/env_status/gdelt_status 주입). injected GDELT transport(ADR#60 와 동일 wire/para/diff)→candidate 5(near 2·hard 3)·fingerprint 1·queue_pop 5·**dataset_source live_derived**·packet_exportable True·predicted_status 숨김·merge_allowed False·production_gold 0. backend 비-live **759 passed/4 skipped/0 failed**(716+신규 43·additive·ADR#60 파일 미수정)·live-PG **94 passed**(write-free·session 인자 부재·무영향)·ingestion **1353 passed**·frontend **tsc0/lint0/test12**·secret PASS·ruff 실게이트(E/F/I/B/W−E501 config ignore) 0(I001/F401 자동수정·UP045/UP035 sibling 일관 비게이트).
**감사(§15)** — adversarial-reality-critic **SOLID·HIGH 0**(synthetic→live 누출·secret 노출·과대종결 없음·6개 RISK 부분진전만·subsumption 정당) + code-review(10 angle·max effort). **두 감사 동일 MEDIUM 1건 = rss_fleet 명칭 이음새**(`run_optional_live_query` 가 'rss_fleet' 을 ADR#60 fetch layer['rss' 만 인식]에 미정규화 전달→fixture silent 낙하; 봉인 자체는 유지[dataset_source 정직 synthetic]이나 "정직 차단" 자기주장이 이 입력에서 거짓) → **정정**: `_ACQ_PROVIDER_ALIAS{rss_fleet→rss}` 정규화+rss_fleet source_ids 를 `_DEFAULT_TARGET_SOURCES` 단일 출처로+회귀 테스트 2(44 정규화·45 source_ids 일치). code-review cleanup 4 정정(and/or 의사삼항→명시 조건식·`readiness or`→`is not None`·blocked 세분류 substring→enum 동치·catalog query_capability 큐레이트 선언 주석). 핵심 안전축 CONFIRMED: fetch_implemented 가 fixture 둔갑 코드 차단(newsapi+creds 여도 dataset_source None)·credential secret-safe(env_present ∈ {present,missing})·blocked GDELT 시 transport 미호출·live_derived provenance 봉인·production_gold 0·no merge/LLM/DB(session 인자 부재).
**RISK(§11)** — 종결 0·신규 0. 부분진전: R-SourceOverlapScarcity(coarse matrix→registry/env/host-gate 구동 readiness gate·fetch_implemented honest 차단)·R-RealSourceLoopUnproven(live query path ready-or-honestly-blocked·DB/merge 0)·R-LiveIdentityBacklog(backlog 충원 source 다음 게이트 정량화)·R-IdentityHumanLabeling(live_derived queue path 입증·predicted_status 숨김)·R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator(agent schema embedding No-Go 고정)·R-Gdelt429(readiness/cooldown 표면화·acquisition 진입점 no-tight-retry). 신규 RISK 후보(R-ProviderCredentialReadiness/R-LiveQueryProviderCoverage/R-ProviderSecretHygiene)는 **독립 blocker 아님→R-SourceOverlapScarcity(provider acquisition closure)·R-Secret 에 포섭**(남발 금지). **완전종결 금지**(실 wired+working key-free query provider=gdelt[429]만·실 near-match 후보 0·reviewer/gold 0·embedding/LLM·운영 DB·production 백로그 0 불변).
**다음 hard blocker** — ① **provider credential/cooldown/fetcher 배선**(gdelt 429 우회[cooldown 경과] 또는 key-required provider key 설정+fetcher 배선 또는 sec_edgar/federal_register fetcher 배선 — 실 near-match 후보 생성의 전제) → ② **real reviewer 충원** → ③ **embedding/LLM adjudicator**(gold calibration 후·gated). readiness gate 는 ①의 정확한 미충족 항목(credential/cooldown/wiring)을 next_action 으로 표면화.
**한계** — **실 near-match 후보 0**(wired+working key-free provider=gdelt[429]만·sec_edgar/federal_register=non-news·미배선·news API=key+미배선)·readiness gate 는 **능력 표면화이지 실 데이터 아님**·실 reviewer/gold 0·embedding/LLM adjudicator No-Go·운영 DB·production 백로그 0 불변. provider readiness(능력)≠실 후보(actuality).
**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/provider_readiness.py`·`backend/tests/test_provider_readiness.py`·`docs/2_ROADMAP/{00_ROADMAP_INDEX,15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP}.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/{RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS,INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT}.md`·`docs/_CANONICAL/02_CURRENT_ARCHITECTURE.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#60.

### [#62] provider query adapter contract + first wired key-required adapter (Guardian) — fetcher_not_wired 병목을 실 adapter contract 로 축소(병합 0·LLM 0·운영 DB 0·실 후보 0)
- 날짜: 2026-06-25 · 섹터: provider fetcher contract(옵션 A) / credential-safe adapter wiring(B·Guardian) / GDELT cooldown hygiene(C) / adapter→near-match queue(D) / governed(host-gate·rate-limit·no-tight-retry) · 상태: **R-SourceOverlapScarcity·R-RealSourceLoopUnproven·R-LiveIdentityBacklog·R-IdentityHumanLabeling·R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator·R-Gdelt429 부분진전·완전종결=OVERCLAIM·옵션 A+B+C+D 채택·E/F 금지·신규 RISK 0**

**문제(§2 통찰)** — ADR#61 이 남긴 정직한 병목: query-capable provider 10종이 registry/credential/host-gate 까지 분류되나 실 fetcher 는 gdelt/rss 만 배선(`fetcher_not_wired`) → 실 near-match 후보 0 의 직접 원인. 이 턴은 그 병목을 한 단계 줄인다 — query provider fetch 의 공통 contract 를 명시하고 첫 실 adapter 를 wire(자동 병합·scheduler persist·semantic merge·LLM 본경로·운영 DB 배포 턴 아님).
**원자 분석(§2·20문항·3-agent 병렬)** — ① fetch_implemented=False=10종(sec_edgar·federal_register key-free + newsapi·gnews·guardian·nyt·naver·serper·tavily·exa key-required) ② 10종 전부 source_registry+_SERVICE_CONFIGS+.env.example placeholder 보유 ③ **1순위=guardian**(registry+단일 env var `GUARDIAN_API_KEY`+topic(`q`)+time(`from-date`/`to-date`)+평탄 안정 JSON[response.results[].webTitle/webUrl/webPublicationDate]+canonical/title/published 본문없이+fake-transport 가능+key 없으면 clean missing_credentials·news 타입=제품 정합) ④ 실 collector 0(전부 미배선)→`fetch_X_overlap_records`+`parse_X`+`_rec`+transport 주입 패턴이 검증된 contract 모델(재발명 0) ⑤ ADR#60 동결 seam=`run_targeted_same_event_operating_readiness(records=,real_fetch=True)` 주입 경로(provider= 로 넘기면 fixture silent 낙하=rss_fleet seam 재발) ⑥ host gate=generic `decide(host,min_spacing)`(상수 편집 불요) ⑦ Guardian Content API shape 공식 문서 확정(anti-skeleton).
**옵션 결정(§3)** — (A) provider fetcher contract (B) 1개 key-required adapter wiring (C) GDELT cooldown-aware hygiene (D) adapter→queue integration (E) embedding/LLM adjudicator runtime (F) production DB activation. **선택: A+B+C+D 채택·E/F 금지.** ADR#62 기록.
**구현(새 파일 1·ADR#60/#57 frozen·단방향 import·재구현 0)** — 신규 `provider_query_adapters.py`: ProviderQueryAdapter/ProviderQueryResult 계약(§5)·`run_provider_query`(gate 순서 fetcher_not_wired→missing_credentials[**network 전**]→rate_limited[in_cooldown]→host_gate_blocked→fetch→parse·status 분류 ok/missing_credentials/rate_limited/host_gate_blocked/network_error/parser_error/no_records)·**실 Guardian parser**(공식 shape·title≤512+canonical+published·**본문 미저장**)·`provider_adapter_contract`/`adapter_descriptor`·secret hygiene(`env_status` present/missing·key 는 실 network 경로만 `os.getenv`·로그/result 0·transport 경로 key 불요). `provider_readiness.py` 보강: guardian→`_FETCH_WIRED_PROVIDERS`·**adapter-wired 분기**(직접 fetch→records= 주입·real_fetch=True·fixture 둔갑 0)·adapter 필드(adapter_contract_version/adapter_module/tested_with_fake_transport/parser_contract_status/record_normalization_status/queue_integration_status/live_query_capable_if_credentials_present/missing_credentials_next_action)·agent schema(provider_adapter_contract·wired_providers·provider_adapter_readiness_review). `rate_limit_policy.yaml`: guardian per-source 정책(min_interval 5s·cooldown_on_429 600s·max_retries 1·no tight retry).
**검증(결정론·LLM 0·network 0·실측)** — 신규 테스트 **29**(test_provider_query_adapters 22: adapter contract 1-8·key-required 9-16·governance 17-21·max_records=0 엣지 22 + test_provider_readiness +7: adapter→queue/readiness 회귀 46-52; transport/env_status/host_gate 주입). guardian fake transport(wire/para/diff)→status ok·records 4·**live_derived**·near 2·queue_pop 5·raw_body_stored False·secret_exposed False·request URL api-key 미노출·hidden_prediction True·raw_body_absent True·production_gold 0·merge_allowed False. missing creds→transport 미호출·dataset_source None. backend 비-live **788 passed/4 skipped/0 failed**(759+신규 29·additive·ADR#60/#57 파일 미수정)·live-PG **94 passed**·ingestion **1353 passed**·frontend **tsc0/lint0/test12**·secret PASS·ruff 실게이트(E/F/I/B/W−E501) 0.
**감사(§17)** — adversarial-reality-critic(synthetic→live 봉인·secret hygiene·rss_fleet seam 미재발·fetch_implemented honesty·anti-skeleton parser·no merge/LLM/DB·RISK 과대종결 0·ToS 경계) + code-review(10 angle·max effort). 결과·정정은 closeout stamp `audit_evidence` 단일 출처 참조.
**RISK(§13)** — 종결 0·신규 0. 부분진전 6: R-SourceOverlapScarcity(provider adapter contract+guardian wired+fetch_implemented 병목 일부 축소[10종 중 1 wired]·adapter→queue 통합)·R-RealSourceLoopUnproven(live query path wired-or-honestly-blocked·DB/merge 0)·R-LiveIdentityBacklog(adapter 후보 queue 충원 경로 입증)·R-IdentityHumanLabeling(adapter-derived candidate→packet·predicted_status 숨김)·R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator(embedding No-Go 고정·candidate scoring interface 만)·R-Gdelt429(cooldown hygiene 유지·adapter no-tight-retry). 신규 RISK 후보(R-ProviderAdapterCoverage/R-ProviderParserContract/R-ProviderSecretHygiene)는 **독립 blocker 아님→R-SourceOverlapScarcity(provider acquisition closure)·R-Secret 포섭**(남발 금지). **완전종결 금지**(실 key 미주입·실 near-match 후보 0·reviewer/gold 0·production 백로그 0 불변).
**다음 hard blocker** — ① **실 credential 주입**(GUARDIAN_API_KEY 등·코드 아닌 secret/ops — live query 가 실 records 생산하려면) → ② **real reviewer 충원**(gold) → ③ **embedding/LLM adjudicator**(paraphrase near-match·gold calibration 후·gated). adapter 는 ①의 코드측 전제(fetcher 배선)를 닫음.
**한계** — **실 near-match 후보 0**(guardian wired 이나 실 key 미주입·fake transport 만 검증)·adapter contract+1 wired=**능력이지 실 데이터 아님**·미배선 9종(sec_edgar/federal_register/nyt/newsapi/gnews/naver/serper/tavily/exa)·실 reviewer/gold 0·embedding/LLM No-Go·운영 DB·production 백로그 0 불변. provider readiness/adapter(능력)≠실 후보(actuality).
**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/provider_query_adapters.py`·`backend/app/tools/provider_readiness.py`·`backend/tests/{test_provider_query_adapters,test_provider_readiness}.py`·`ingestion/configs/rate_limit_policy.yaml`·`docs/2_ROADMAP/{00_ROADMAP_INDEX,15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP}.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/{RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS,INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT}.md`·`docs/_CANONICAL/02_CURRENT_ARCHITECTURE.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#61.

### [#63] secret-safe Guardian live query smoke + live-derived queue population gate — 실 key 로 live 경로 실증·단일 소스 same-event overlap 구조적 부재 발견(병합 0·LLM 0·운영 DB 0)
- 날짜: 2026-06-26 · 섹터: secret-safe live query smoke(옵션 A) / secret hygiene hardening(B) / no-key blocked report(C) / env_not_loaded vs missing_credentials 구분 / governed live-derived queue population · 상태: **R-SourceOverlapScarcity·R-RealSourceLoopUnproven·R-LiveIdentityBacklog·R-IdentityHumanLabeling·R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator·R-Gdelt429 부분진전·완전종결=OVERCLAIM·옵션 A+B+C 채택·D(2nd adapter)/E/F 금지·신규 RISK 0**

**문제(§2 통찰)** — ADR#62 가 Guardian adapter 를 wire 했으나 **fake transport 로만 검증**(실 key 미사용). 이 턴은 실 network 직전 마지막 경계를 검증한다 — credential 이 secret-safe 하게 준비된 경우 bounded governed live query 를 opt-in 실행하고 records 를 ADR#60 운영경로로 연결해 live-derived near-match queue 를 만들 수 있는지 **실제로** 확인(2nd provider adapter·semantic merge·LLM 본경로·운영 DB 배포 턴 아님).
**원자 분석(§2·20문항)** — ① env var=`GUARDIAN_API_KEY`(`.env.example:229` 존재) ② readiness 함수=`ingestion.core.env_loader.env_status`(present/missing·값 0) ③ 프로세스 자동 load 아님(env_status→load_env 호출 시 `os.environ.setdefault`) ④ **현재 missing_credentials 와 env_not_loaded 미구분**(둘 다 missing_credentials 로 뭉갬)→ADR#63 에서 `.env` Path.exists 로 구분 ⑤ secret 값은 adapter 내부 `os.getenv`가 real-network 분기에서만·httpx params 전용·url keyless(ADR#62 LOW-2) ⑥ `LQ_NO_NEAR_MATCH`(provider_readiness.py:577) 이미 배선 ⑦ live query=CI flaky→opt-in manual 만 ⑧ **다음 hard blocker(실 데이터로 확정)=2nd publishable provider(cross-source)**, auto-merge·LLM 아님.
**옵션 결정(§3)** — (A) Guardian secret-safe live query smoke (B) secret hygiene hardening (C) no-key blocked report (D) 2nd provider adapter (E) embedding/LLM adjudicator runtime (F) production DB activation. **선택: A+B+C 채택·D/E/F 금지.** ADR#63 기록.
**구현(새 파일 1·ADR#62 커밋분 frozen·단방향 import·재구현 0)** — 신규 `guardian_live_query_smoke.py`: §4 smoke 계약 단일 dict(smoke_name·live_query_requested/attempted·env_var_name·credential_present·**credential_value_exposed=False·env_file_read=False** 불변·env_example_checked·provider_status·host_gate_status·rate_limit_status·records/candidate/near/hard/queue_pop·dataset_source·provenance·block_reasons·next_actions·production_gold 0·merge_allowed False·db_write False·llm_invoked False)·**env_not_loaded vs missing_credentials 구분**(`.env` 부재→env_not_loaded·존재·키 미설정→missing_credentials·둘 다 network 전·값 미열람)·credential present+opt-in 시 `run_optional_live_query` 위임(재구현 0)·CLI(`--live-query` opt-in·`--json`·값 미출력). `env_loader.py` 보강: `probe_env_var`(present/missing + `.env` Path.exists + `.env.example` 이름 선언·**전부 값 미열람**)·`env_example_declares`.
**검증(결정론 25 + 실 호출 2)** — 신규 테스트 **26**(test_guardian_live_query_smoke: secret boundary·env_not_loaded/missing 구분·fake transport 성공·no_records/no-overlap/network_error 분류·queue 충원·agent contract·CLI·probe 헬퍼·**real-network secret 경로[httpx monkeypatch·os.getenv→params·url keyless]**; provider_transport/env_probe_fn 주입 hermetic·실 `.env` 미접촉). **실 Guardian 호출 2회**(opt-in·bounded·governed·secret-safe): topic "Ukraine"/"earthquake" 7d → 각 **records 10·candidate 0·`no_title_overlap`·dataset_source live_derived·secret_exposed False·env_file_read False·host_gate passed·rate_limit ok**. → **live 경로 실증**(실 key·실 fetch·정규화·secret 경계) 그러나 **단일 소스(Guardian) 내 same-event overlap 0**(구조적: 이 토픽/윈도우에서 같은 날 기사 제목 Jaccard<near 임계·near-dup recall 한계 포함·deterministic near-match 는 cross-source wire syndication 설계). backend 비-live **814 passed**(759+ADR#62 29+ADR#63 26 additive)·live-PG 94·full `backend/tests` DB-up 실측 **908 passed/4 skipped/0 failed**·ingestion 1353·frontend tsc0/lint0/test12·secret PASS·ruff 0(closeout stamp 실측 단일 출처).
**감사(§15)** — adversarial-reality-critic(secret 경계: env_file_read/credential_value_exposed 단언이 실 호출에서 성립·fixture 둔갑 0·실 records→live_derived 정직·single-source overlap 0 정직 노출·no merge/LLM/DB) + code-review. 결과·정정은 closeout stamp `audit_evidence` 단일 출처.
**RISK(§11)** — 종결 0·신규 0. 부분진전 6: R-SourceOverlapScarcity(**실 key live query 실증·records 10×2**·단 overlap 0=cross-source 필요 확정)·R-RealSourceLoopUnproven(live path 실 fetch 입증·DB/merge 0)·R-LiveIdentityBacklog(queue 충원 경로 실 records 로 입증·단 overlap 0 으로 queue_pop 0)·R-IdentityHumanLabeling(packet 경로 유지·gold 0)·R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator(embedding No-Go 고정)·R-Gdelt429(Guardian 실 대체 fetch 입증·단일 의존 완화). 후보 R-GuardianCredentialReadiness/R-LiveProviderSmokeReliability/R-SecretBoundary **부재→R-SourceOverlapScarcity·R-Secret 포섭**(남발 금지). **완전종결 금지**(실 same-event overlap 0·reviewer/gold 0·production 백로그 0 불변).
**다음 hard blocker(실 데이터로 확정)** — ① **2번째 publishable provider 배선(cross-source)** — 단일 소스 same-event near-dup 은 구조적으로 희소(실 호출 2회 모두 overlap 0). cross-source(Guardian+another) 가 실 near-match 의 실제 unblock(옵션 D·다음 턴) → ② real reviewer/gold → ③ embedding/LLM adjudicator(gated). 실 key·live 경로는 이번 턴에 닫음(능력 완비).
**한계** — **실 same-event overlap 0**(live 경로·실 fetch 는 성공[records 10×2]이나 단일 소스 내 near-dup 구조적 부재)·queue_pop 0·reviewer/gold 0·embedding/LLM No-Go·운영 DB·production 백로그 0·미배선 provider 9종 불변. live query 능력·실증≠실 near-match 후보(cross-source 필요).
**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/guardian_live_query_smoke.py`·`ingestion/core/env_loader.py`·`backend/tests/test_guardian_live_query_smoke.py`·`docs/2_ROADMAP/{00_ROADMAP_INDEX,15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP,19_WEB_INTELLIGENCE_IMPLEMENTATION_SPEC}.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/{RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS,INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT}.md`·`docs/_CANONICAL/02_CURRENT_ARCHITECTURE.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#62.

### [#64] 2nd publishable provider adapter(NYT) + cross-source live overlap smoke — 실 cross-source pair 100 생성 입증·deterministic title-Jaccard 0 검출→embedding adjudicator 가 다음 unblock(병합 0·LLM 0·운영 DB 0)
- 날짜: 2026-06-26 · 섹터: 2nd provider adapter wiring[NYT](옵션 A) / cross-source live overlap smoke(B) / secret-safe blocked report(C) · 상태: **R-SourceOverlapScarcity·R-RealSourceLoopUnproven·R-LiveIdentityBacklog·R-IdentityHumanLabeling·R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator·R-Gdelt429 부분진전·완전종결=OVERCLAIM·옵션 A+B+C 채택·D(3rd provider)=docs only·E(embedding/LLM)/F(production DB) 금지·신규 RISK 0**

**문제(§2 통찰)** — ADR#63 가 실 key 로 입증: Guardian **단일 소스** same-event overlap 0(`no_title_overlap`·구조적·단일 매체는 같은 사건 1회/다른 제목 보도). 다음 hard blocker(실데이터 확정)=cross-source. 이 턴은 Guardian 과 같은 영문 quality **단일 publisher**(NYT)를 붙여 다출처 같은 사건 cross-source near-match 가 reviewer queue 로 들어갈 수 있는지 확인(semantic merge·LLM 본경로·운영 DB·reviewer/gold 턴 아님).
**원자 분석(§2·20문항)** — ① Guardian candidate 0=`no_title_overlap`(같은 날 publishable cross-URL pair 있으나 제목 Jaccard<near) ② records 충분(record scarcity 아님)·**단일-source 구조**(cross-source 가 해법) ③ 2nd provider=**NYT**(영문 quality **단일 publisher**·aggregator(newsapi/gnews)는 Guardian 자기기사 재유입=same-source 오염→배제) ④ env=`NYT_API_KEY`(`.env.example:233`) ⑤ key-required ⑥ topic(q)+time_window(begin_date/end_date YYYYMMDD) ⑦ headline.main/web_url/pub_date ⑧ 본문 미저장 가능 ⑨ ToS 무료 500/day·비상업·title+canonical 만→재배포 아님(Guardian 동일 경계) ⑩ **auth=query_param `api-key`(Guardian 동일)→`run_provider_query` params 무수정 재사용**(newsapi=`apiKey`/gnews=`token`은 코드변경 필요→NYT 최소변경) ⑪ combined records→`run_targeted`/`discover_overlap`(주입) ⑫ source_id 보존·near_match_pairs source_id_left/right 로 cross-source pair 식별 ⑬ 둘 다 성공·candidate 0→no_cross_source_overlap/no_title_overlap/no_near_match 분해 ⑭ key 없으면 env_not_loaded/missing_credentials(per-provider·network 전) ⑳ **다음 hard blocker=embedding/LLM adjudicator**(deterministic title-Jaccard paraphrase 약).
**옵션 결정(§3)** — (A) 2nd publishable provider adapter[NYT] (B) cross-source live overlap smoke (C) secret-safe blocked report (D) 3rd/4th provider planning (E) embedding/LLM adjudicator runtime (F) production DB activation. **선택: A+B+C 채택·D=docs/schema only·E/F 금지.** ADR#64 기록.
**구현(새 파일 1·adapter 1·ADR#63 커밋분 frozen·단방향 import·재구현 0)** — `provider_query_adapters.py`: `NYT_ADAPTER`(key-required·news·topic+time_window·host `api.nytimes.com`·12s floor)+`_nyt_url`(begin_date/end_date YYYYMMDD·대시 제거·**keyless**)+`parse_nyt_items`(headline.main/web_url/pub_date→`_rec`·본문 미저장)·`api-key` param=Guardian 동일→`run_provider_query` 무수정. 신규 `cross_source_live_overlap_smoke.py`(얇은 composition): §4 cross-source 계약(smoke_name·providers·provider_a/b·credential_status_by_provider·**credential_value_exposed=False·env_file_read=False**·provider/host_gate/rate_limit_status_by_provider·records_count_by_provider·combined_records_count·**cross_source_pair_count**·fingerprint/near/hard/queue_pop·dataset_source_by_provider·block_reasons·next_actions·production_gold 0·merge_allowed False·db_write False·llm 0)·**둘 다 성공만 cross-source 인정**(single-source 둔갑 금지·한쪽만 ok→no_records_provider_a/b·queue 0)·near/hard pair 를 **cross-source(source_id 상이)만** 필터해 ADR#59 `build_near_match_reviewer_queue` 충원(same-source guardian↔guardian/nyt↔nyt 오염 구조 차단)·CLI(`--live-query`·`--provider-b`·`--json`·값 미출력).
**검증(결정론 39 + 실 호출 4)** — 신규 테스트 **39**(test_cross_source_live_overlap_smoke 30 + test_provider_query_adapters NYT Section D 9; test_provider_readiness test_49 회귀 정정 1[nyt wired]): cross-source 분류·single-source 둔갑 차단·no_cross_source_overlap/no_title_overlap/no_near_match 분해·secret boundary(real-network httpx monkeypatch·**양 provider params 전용·url keyless**)·agent contract(cross-source readiness·no secret fabrication·embedding No-Go)·CLI hermetic·NYT adapter(parse·missing_credentials·**date YYYYMMDD**·max_records·keyless URL). **실 Guardian+NYT 호출 4회**(2 topic×2 provider·opt-in·bounded·governed·secret-safe): "Ukraine"/"earthquake" 7d → 각 **Guardian 10+NYT 10=combined 20·`cross_source_pair_count` 100·fingerprint 0·near 0·hard 0·`no_title_overlap`·dataset_source live_derived·credential_value_exposed False·env_file_read False·host_gate passed·rate_limit ok**. → **cross-source pair 100 생성 입증**(단일 소스 구조적 0→cross 100·**수집/source/key/fetch 능력 입증**) 그러나 **deterministic title-Jaccard 0 검출**(hard band 0.2 까지 0)=이 0 은 (i) deterministic 의 paraphrase recall 한계 **또는** (ii) 두 매체가 같은 토픽의 **다른 사건/측면** 보도(real scarcity) 둘 다 가능·n=2 토픽으로 미구분(100 쌍=비교 *대상*이지 same-event match 아님). 다음 방향=embedding/LLM adjudicator 는 deterministic precision 0.57<0.98(ADR#42/#43) **별도 근거**로 정당화·이 4회 호출이 입증은 아님(adversarial MEDIUM-2). backend 비-live **853 passed**(814+39)·full `backend/tests` DB-up **947**(잠정·재측정)·ingestion 1353·frontend tsc0/lint0/test12·secret PASS·ruff 0(closeout stamp 실측 단일 출처).
**감사(§15)** — adversarial-reality-critic + code-review. 결과·정정은 closeout stamp `audit_evidence` 단일 출처.
**RISK(§11)** — 종결 0·신규 0. 부분진전 6: R-SourceOverlapScarcity(**실 cross-source pair 100 입증·단일 소스 0→cross-source 100**·단 deterministic 검출 0=embedding 필요 확정)·R-RealSourceLoopUnproven(2nd publishable provider 실 fetch·DB/merge 0)·R-LiveIdentityBacklog(cross-source queue 경로 실 records 로 입증·단 deterministic 0 으로 queue_pop 0)·R-IdentityHumanLabeling(packet 경로 유지·gold 0)·R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator(**다음 hard blocker 로 실데이터 확정**·No-Go 유지)·R-Gdelt429(Guardian+NYT 2 publishable 실 fetch 입증·GDELT 단일 의존 완화). 후보 R-CrossSourceProviderCoverage/R-SecondProviderCredentialReadiness/R-CrossSourceLiveSmokeReliability **부재→R-SourceOverlapScarcity·R-Secret 포섭**(남발 금지). **완전종결 금지**(deterministic cross-source overlap 0·reviewer/gold 0·production 백로그 0 불변).
**다음 hard blocker(실 데이터로 확정)** — ① **embedding/LLM semantic adjudicator(gated·옵션 E)** — cross-source pair 는 생성되나(100×2 topic) deterministic title-Jaccard 가 100 쌍 중 0 검출(hard band 0.2 까지 0) → semantic similarity 가 다음 **후보**(0 검출이 real scarcity[다른 사건]인지 paraphrase recall 한계인지 n=2 로 미구분; embedding 방향은 deterministic precision 0.57<0.98·gold/MERGE_GATE·adversarial validation 필수의 **별도 근거**로 정당화) → ② real reviewer/gold → ③ MERGE_GATE → ④ Agent/IU. cross-source 능력·실증은 이번 턴에 닫음(2 publishable provider·실 pair 100).
**한계** — **deterministic cross-source overlap 0**(cross-source pair 100 생성·실 fetch 성공이나 title-Jaccard paraphrase 약·near 0)·queue_pop 0·reviewer/gold 0·embedding/LLM No-Go·운영 DB·production 백로그 0·미배선 provider 8종(NYT 배선으로 9→8). cross-source 능력≠deterministic 검출(embedding 필요).
**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/{cross_source_live_overlap_smoke,provider_query_adapters}.py`·`backend/tests/{test_cross_source_live_overlap_smoke,test_provider_query_adapters,test_provider_readiness}.py`·`docs/2_ROADMAP/{00_ROADMAP_INDEX,15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP}.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/{RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS,INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT}.md`·`docs/_CANONICAL/02_CURRENT_ARCHITECTURE.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#62/#63.

### [#65] offline/gated semantic candidate scorer + cross-source pair evaluation packet — cross-source pair scarcity→detection scarcity 재분해·candidate prioritization substrate(병합 0·LLM 0·embedding 실호출 0·운영 DB 0)
- 날짜: 2026-06-26 · 섹터: semantic candidate scorer contract(옵션 A) / offline deterministic+fake scaffold(B) / reviewer/eval packet export(D) / optional embedding·LLM scorer(C·injection-only) · 상태: **R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator·R-IdentityEvalDataset·R-ReviewerAgreement·R-GoldSamplingBias·R-SourceOverlapScarcity·R-RealSourceLoopUnproven·R-LiveIdentityBacklog·R-IdentityHumanLabeling 부분진전·완전종결=OVERCLAIM·옵션 A+B+D 채택·C=injection-only interface·E(production semantic merge)/F(production DB) 금지·신규 RISK 0**

**문제(§2 통찰)** — ADR#64 가 실 key 로 입증: cross-source pair 는 단일 소스 0→100 으로 **생성**됐으나 deterministic title-Jaccard 가 100 쌍 중 0 검출(`no_title_overlap`·hard band 0.2 까지 0). 즉 병목이 **source scarcity → detection scarcity** 로 재분해. 이 턴은 그 0 을 **버리지도 병합하지도 않고** semantic candidate scorer 로 점수화해 reviewer queue **prioritization** 으로 넘기되, gold/MERGE_GATE 전 어떤 병합도 없는 **offline candidate-prioritization substrate** 를 만든다(production semantic merge·운영 DB·scheduler·public IU 턴 아님).
**원자 분석(§2·20문항)** — ① pair 100 은 **어디에도 영속 안 됨**(smoke 가 discover 결과를 count·queue 만·no DB) ② pair metadata 충분(`_near_pair_record`가 source_id/role/title/canonical/observed_at/jaccard 보존·topic/time_window/provider/provenance 만 주입) ③ 최소 input=§5 `SemanticPairInput`≈pair record+context ④ 기존 `semantic_identity_adjudicator.classify_identity_candidate`=title-Jaccard×date_factor 결정론 분류·단 **DB-resolved Event(EventView) 기반**·`semantic_score` seam None·바로 그 0 신호 ⑤ `EvalPair.ALLOWED_KEYS`에 score/predicted_status 없음→scorer output 누출 시 `_validate_row`/`validate_labeling_packet` **fail-loud**(internal-only 구조 강제) ⑥ scorer 를 packet 밖에서 실행→score 로 top-k pair_id 만 선별→score 없는 pair record 만 queue ⑦ `SemanticPairScore` 별도 internal report ⑧ env var=**`OPENAI_API_KEY`**(LLM·embedding 공용·`.env.example:11`)·`LLM_PROVIDER`/`EMBEDDING_PROVIDER` 기본 mock ⑨ `probe_env_var`(present/missing·값 미열람) ⑩ **실호출 0**(fake/deterministic + injection-only interface) ⑪ gold 없이 threshold 금지→**top-k rank** ⑫ MERGE_GATE precision≥0.98/FPR≤0.01/hard_neg_fp=0/korean≥0.98(`identity_eval_dataset.MERGE_GATE`) ⑬ top-k rank(단정 0)+hard negative+predicted_status hidden+deterministic 정직 0 보고로 FP 차단 ⑭ discover hard_negative_pairs([0.2,0.5))+synthetic 유지 ⑮ language 보존(판정은 reviewer/calibration) ⑯ `source_role_compatible` publishable×publishable guard ⑰ DB/EventLink/adjudication 미접근·`semantic_score` 미주입·`merge_allowed=False` ⑱ R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator=contract+scaffold+score→queue+No-Go 까지(완전종결 금지) ⑲ scored→reviewer/eval packet·top-k+hard negative·production_gold 0 정직 ⑳ **다음 hard blocker=real reviewer labels**(우선)→embedding scorer opt-in 실호출→MERGE_GATE calibration.
**옵션 결정(§3)** — (A) semantic candidate scorer contract (B) offline deterministic/lexical+semantic feature scaffold (C) optional embedding/LLM scorer opt-in (D) reviewer/eval packet export from scored pairs (E) production semantic merge (F) production DB activation. **선택: A+B+D 채택·C=injection-only interface/No-Go(실호출 0)·E/F 금지.** ADR#65 기록.
**구현(새 파일 1·additive 2·ADR#64 커밋분 frozen·단방향 import·재구현 0)** — 신규 `semantic_candidate_scorer.py`: §5 `SemanticPairInput`/`SemanticPairScore`
