**검증(결정론 49·실호출 0)** — 신규 테스트 **49**(test_semantic_candidate_scorer **46**[scorer contract 1-8·deterministic/fake 9-16·reviewer queue 통합 17-24·embedding/LLM opt-in policy 25-32·agent contract 38-42·CLI/select_top_k 43-46·**감사 fix-lock 47-51**: cross_source_only same-source 제외·cross_source_only off·sub-floor candidate→above_near_floor 0·hard_negative band 미승격·fallback band] + test_cross_source_live_overlap_smoke **+3**[31 default off=ADR#64 보존·32 wired·33 single-provider skip]). backend 비-live **899 passed/101 skipped/0 failed**(DB 미기동→live-PG 101 skip)·ingestion **1353 passed**·frontend tsc0/lint0/**test12**·ruff(E/F/I/B/W−E501) **0**. **live-PG=미실행**(postgres:5432 CLOSED·docker 미기동) — 단 이 턴 변경은 **DB/session/ORM 경로 무접촉**(scorer write-free·`db_write:False`·session 인자 부재·`discover_overlap`/smoke additive 도 write-free)→live-PG 무영향(직전 baseline 94 불변). secret scan/closeout 은 stamp 단일 출처. **실호출 0 입증**: opt-in mode 도 default 미활성(scorer_disabled)·credential present+scorer_fn 미주입→provider_error(실 client No-Go)·주입 fake scorer_fn 만 실행(llm/embedding_invoked False·scorer_fn_invoked True 분리 보고).
**감사(§15)** — adversarial-reality-critic **PROCEED-WITH-FIXES**(안전 핵심 merge/secret/DB/labeler/network 전부 VALID·HIGH 0; MEDIUM 2 수정: **M-1** scorer 경로 cross-source 미강제→same-source pair 점수화·queue 진입 → `cross_source_only=True` 기본 필터+`same_source_pair_excluded` 분해 보고+"100쌍"→cross_source_pair_count 정정·테스트 47/48; **M-2** deterministic_scaffold 가 실 sub-floor 데이터에서 candidate>0 → "검출 진전" 오독 가능 → `above_near_floor_count`/`candidate_band_distribution` 추가·테스트 49) + code-review **HIGH 0**(MED-1 hard_negative band high score→near positive 승격 → top-k 를 hard band 제외 space rank·hard lane 보존·테스트 50; HIGH-1 fallback band 누락→hard lane 소실 → 명시 band 부여·테스트 51; LOW reuse/dead 정직 wording). 결과·정정 단일 출처=closeout stamp `audit_evidence`.
**감사(§15)** — adversarial-reality-critic + code-review. 결과·정정은 closeout stamp `audit_evidence` 단일 출처.
**RISK(§11)** — 종결 0·신규 0. 부분진전 8: R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator(scorer contract+offline scaffold+score→reviewer queue prioritization·No-Go 유지·embedding/LLM 실호출 0·**validated adjudicator 아님**)·R-IdentityEvalDataset(scored→reviewer/eval packet·top-k+hard negative·production_gold 0 정직)·R-ReviewerAgreement(top-k+hard negative packet·score labeler 숨김·실 합의 0)·R-GoldSamplingBias(top-k+hard negative 동시 표집·score 숨김 reviewer bias 차단·실 표집 0)·R-SourceOverlapScarcity(**cross-source pair scarcity→detection scarcity 재분해**·scorer 층 연결·검출 검증 아님)·R-RealSourceLoopUnproven(scorer 층·실 reviewer/gold/merge 0)·R-LiveIdentityBacklog(scorer→cross-source top-k queue 경로·실 backlog 0)·R-IdentityHumanLabeling(scored top-k→packet·score/predicted_status labeler 숨김·실 gold 0). 신규 RISK 후보 R-SemanticScorerCalibration/R-LLMAdjudicatorBias/R-EmbeddingProviderReadiness **부재→현 단계 독립 blocker 아님**(scorer 미배선·실호출 0이라 calibration/bias/provider readiness 가 아직 실재 X·R-LLMAdjudicatorBias 취지는 score labeler 숨김으로 선제 완화)·등록 안 함(남발 금지). **완전종결 금지**(gold-calibrated adjudicator·MERGE_GATE 런타임·실 병합·실 reviewer/gold 0 불변).
**다음 hard blocker(실 데이터로 확정)** — ① **real reviewer labels**(우선·gold 없이는 어떤 scorer threshold/embedding 도 provisional) → ② embedding scorer opt-in 실호출(`create_embedding_client` seam 배선·secret-safe·bounded·internal-only) → ③ MERGE_GATE calibration(precision≥0.98) → ④ adjudicator runtime → ⑤ Agent/IU. scorer prioritization substrate·detection 재분해는 이 턴에 닫음(병합·검출 검증은 아님).
**한계** — **이 턴 진전=candidate prioritization substrate·validated adjudicator 아님**(deterministic_scaffold=ADR#64 의 0 신호와 동일·recall 개선 0·fake_semantic=배관 scaffold·실 embedding 아님)·reviewer_queue_population 은 scaffold/fixture 기준(실 reviewer/gold 0)·embedding/LLM 실호출 0(No-Go)·MERGE_GATE 미충족·production_gold 0·운영 DB·scheduler·semantic merge·public IU 0. score≠truth·prioritization≠검출.
**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/{semantic_candidate_scorer,source_overlap_discovery,cross_source_live_overlap_smoke}.py`·`backend/tests/{test_semantic_candidate_scorer,test_cross_source_live_overlap_smoke}.py`·`docs/2_ROADMAP/{00_ROADMAP_INDEX,15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP}.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/{RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS,INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT}.md`·`docs/_CANONICAL/02_CURRENT_ARCHITECTURE.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#42/#43/#57/#59/#64.

### [#66] reviewer label operations + gold calibration preflight — ADR#65 semantic top-k reviewer queue 를 실 사람 라벨 운영(export→import→agreement/conflict/adjudication→gold→calibration)으로 연결(병합 0·LLM 0·embedding 0·운영 DB 0·실 production gold 0)
- 날짜: 2026-06-26 · 섹터: reviewer label import/export contract(옵션 A) / agreement·conflict·adjudication workflow hardening(B) / gold calibration preflight(C) / optional real label file ingestion(D) · 상태: **R-IdentityHumanLabeling·R-ReviewerAgreement·R-GoldSamplingBias·R-IdentityEvalDataset·R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator·R-LiveIdentityBacklog·R-SourceOverlapScarcity·R-RealSourceLoopUnproven 부분진전·완전종결=OVERCLAIM·옵션 A+B+C+D 채택·E(embedding/LLM runtime)/F(production merge·DB) 금지·신규 RISK 0**
- **선행: ADR#65 안정 기준점 커밋**(`4e726ff`·13파일·메시지 제공본 그대로).

**문제(§2 통찰)** — ADR#65 가 만든 것: cross-source pair→semantic scorer top-k→near-match reviewer queue(score/rationale labeler 숨김). 다음 병목 = **그 queue 가 실제 사람 라벨 운영으로 이어지지 않는다**. packet export→label import→agreement/conflict/adjudication→gold 승격→MERGE_GATE calibration readiness 의 운영 경로를 닫는 턴(embedding 실호출·production semantic merge·운영 DB·scheduler·public IU 턴 아님). score 는 truth 가 아니라 reviewer worklist priority — gold 전 threshold 확정 금지.
**원자 분석(§2·20문항)** — ① scorer top-k→`build_near_match_reviewer_queue`→packet_rows(validate 통과)+labeler_view(score-free)·이미 연결 ② labeler-facing view 가 score/rationale/predicted_status/bucket 구조적 숨김(`validate_labeling_packet` fail-loud+allowlist 이중) ③ label import schema **이미 존재**(`load_reviewer_labels`/`_validate_reviewer_row`·allowlist 가 semantic_score/raw_body 구조 거부)→보강=pseudonymization·production/synthetic 집계·통합 output ④ single→`AGREE_INSUFFICIENT`(gold 아님) ⑤ 2+만장일치→`AGREE_AGREED`→GoldPair ⑥ conflict→`AGREE_CONFLICT`+`adjudication_queue_from_resolved` ⑦ conflict+human adjudication→`AGREE_ADJUDICATED`(gold)·`_validate_adjudication` **adjudicator_kind=human 강제**(LLM-as-judge 봉인) ⑧ dataset_source live_derived↔synthetic_fixture·`evaluate_gold_merge_readiness` **live only** ⑨ label_source 3-way(production/synthetic/test)는 frozen 계약 밖→operation-level tag(production gold=production AND live_derived) ⑩ reviewer_id=**PII 가능**→공개 report 는 결정론 pseudonym(`rv_<sha1[:12]>`)만 ⑪ raw body/secret/score 누출=allowlist fail-loud ⑫ `evaluate_gold_merge_readiness`+`evaluate_adjudicator`=precision/FPR/hard_neg_fp denominator ⑬ top-k=same-event-lean→positive 편향(완화=hard negative 동시 표집·`top_k_bias_warning`) ⑭ hard negative 보존(scorer band 제외 유지) ⑮ language ko 보존·KO floor 50 ⑯ `compute_reviewer_agreement`=per-pair+전체(단일 reviewer 분모 제외) ⑰ 빈 입력→gold 0·`gold_ready`=False 정직 ⑱ 실 production gold 있을 때만 gold_ready True ⑲ R-IdentityHumanLabeling/ReviewerAgreement/GoldSamplingBias=운영 배선+forbidden 거부+분리+pseudonym+calibration preflight 까지(완전종결 금지·실 production gold 0) ⑳ **다음 hard blocker=real reviewer 충원(실 human label file)**→embedding opt-in→MERGE_GATE runtime. **설계 긴장 표면화:** label enum 충돌(§5 unsure/needs_review vs frozen ambiguous/insufficient)→기존 유지(회귀 안전)·label_source 3-way=operation tag·기존 export 도구 2개 DB 바운드→비-DB 턴이라 순수 모듈만 재사용.
**옵션 결정(§3)** — (A) reviewer label import/export contract (B) agreement/conflict/adjudication hardening (C) gold calibration preflight (D) optional real label file ingestion (E) embedding/LLM scorer runtime (F) production semantic merge/DB activation. **선택: A+B+C+D 채택·E/F 금지.** ADR#66 기록.
**구현(새 파일 1·재구현 0·기존 머신 재사용·단방향 import·DB 0)** — 신규 `reviewer_label_operations.py`(얇은 orchestrator): `export_reviewer_packet`(queue→packet_rows+labeler_view·score/rationale/bucket 누출 재검증·옵션 A export)·`import_reviewer_labels`(`load_reviewer_labels` 래핑·파일 없음→**no_labels graceful**[실패 아님]·forbidden field→`forbidden_field_in_label`·malformed→분류·옵션 A/D)·`pseudonymize_reviewer_id`(결정론 sha1·raw PII 미노출·§5/§10-30)·`resolve_label_operations`(`resolve_gold_from_reviewers`+agreement+conflict queue+**production/synthetic gold 분리**[production=production AND live_derived]·옵션 B)·`build_calibration_preflight`(§7 전 필드: production/positive/negative/korean gold·language/source_pair 분포·agreement_rate·conflict_rate·positive_negative_balance·hard_negative_coverage·**top_k_bias_warning**·korean_calibration_ready·precision/fpr_denominator_ready·`evaluate_gold_merge_readiness` 재사용·merge_gate_ready·옵션 C)·`run_reviewer_label_operations`(§4 통합 output 31필드)·`REVIEWER_OPS_AGENT_CONTRACT`(§9·reviewer/gold 운영 계획 가능·merge/truth/anchor/secret 불가·`EMBEDDING_LLM_ADJUDICATOR_INTERFACE` No-Go 재참조)·CLI(`--synthetic-labels` 데모=production gold 0). **scorer/smoke 미변경**(orchestrator 가 queue 소비·최소 변경).
**검증(결정론 49·실호출 0·DB 0)** — 신규 테스트 **49**(test_reviewer_label_operations 1-49: export/import contract 1-10·gold promotion 11-18·agreement/calibration 19-27·optional real label path 28-34·no-merge/no-LLM/no-DB/secret 35-41[40=모듈 소스 env/secret 무접근 구조 검증·41=output secret 누출 0]·회귀 cross-check 42-43·validation guard 44-46·**감사 HIGH fix-lock 47-49**[47 resolve chokepoint model label 거부·48 in-memory 경로 model label→production_gold 0·block_reason·49 파일 경로 model label→model_label_rejected 분류]). backend 비-live **948 passed/101 skipped/0 failed**·ingestion **1353 passed**(불변)·frontend tsc0/lint0/**test12**(불변)·ruff(E/F/I/B/W−E501) **0**. **live-PG=미실행**(DB 미기동) — 이 턴 변경은 **DB/session/ORM 무접촉**(orchestrator write-free·`db_write:False`·session 인자 부재·DB 바운드 export 도구 미사용)→live-PG 무영향(baseline 불변). secret scan PASS(신규 2파일)·closeout 은 stamp 단일 출처. **honest 동작 입증:** 라벨 없음→production_gold 0·`no_labels`·synthetic 라벨→production_gold 0·synthetic_gold 카운트·conflict→queue·production unanimous→gold·single→insufficient·pseudonym 결정론(raw id 미노출).
**감사(§15)** — adversarial-reality-critic + code-review. **adversarial HIGH 1 수정(cardinal)**: "model/self/LLM label ≠ gold(human only)" 가 파일 경로(`_validate_reviewer_row`)에서만 강제되고 **in-memory `reviewer_labels` 경로는 reviewer_kind 무검증→model label 2개 만장일치가 production gold 로 승격 가능**(모듈 1급 입력·CLI demo 사용·무테스트) → `resolve_label_operations` chokepoint fail-loud 가드 + `run_reviewer_label_operations` in-memory 경로 reviewer_kind 거부(block_reason `model_label_rejected`·graceful) + 파일 경로 "cannot be gold"→`model_label_rejected` 분류·테스트 47-49. **adversarial MEDIUM 정정**: `pseudonymize_reviewer_id` "역산 불가"→"저엔트로피 id enumeration 가역·출력 표면 unlinkability 용" 정직화·`production_gold` "선언 기반 provenance(label_source/dataset_source forgeable·미검증)" 코드 주석 명시(현 production_gold 0=실 실행 부재). **adversarial REFUTE**: "scorer/smoke 무변경 미검증"은 **stale git 스냅샷**(대화 시작 시점 ADR#65 미커밋 상태) — 현 작업트리는 scorer/smoke/discovery 무접촉(`git status -sb` 확인·ADR#65 `4e726ff` 로 커밋됨). **code-review LOW**: 상태 비교 문자열 리터럴→frozen 상수(`AGREE_*`/`RESOLUTION_SINGLE`). 안전 핵심(no-merge/secret/labeler-hidden/production_gold honesty) 전부 VALID. 결과·정정 단일 출처=closeout stamp `audit_evidence`.
**RISK(§11)** — 종결 0·신규 0. 부분진전 8: R-IdentityHumanLabeling(label export/import contract 운영 배선+forbidden field 거부+production/synthetic 분리+pseudonymization·실 production gold/agreement 0 불변)·R-ReviewerAgreement(single/unanimous/conflict/adjudicated 경로 검증+agreement/conflict report+adjudication queue·실 다중 reviewer 합의 0)·R-GoldSamplingBias(top_k_bias_warning+hard negative coverage+positive/negative balance+score labeler 숨김·실 production 표집 0)·R-IdentityEvalDataset(production/synthetic gold 분리+calibration preflight+precision/FPR denominator readiness·MERGE_GATE evidence 0)·R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator(semantic scorer output→gold workflow 진입·scorer threshold uncalibrated·merge No-Go 유지)·R-LiveIdentityBacklog(scorer top-k queue→label 운영 경로·실 backlog/gold 0)·R-SourceOverlapScarcity(detection scarcity 후속 reviewer 운영층·검출 검증 아님)·R-RealSourceLoopUnproven(reviewer/gold 운영 substrate·실 병합 0). 신규 RISK 후보 R-ReviewerOpsReadiness/R-LabelLeakage/R-GoldCalibrationReadiness **부재→현 단계 독립 blocker 아님**(R-LabelLeakage 취지=score/rationale/predicted_status 누출은 allowlist+validate fail-loud+pseudonymization 으로 선제 봉인·calibration readiness 부족은 R-IdentityEvalDataset 가 추적)·등록 안 함(남발 금지). **완전종결 금지**(실 production reviewer label·실 gold·reviewer agreement·MERGE_GATE evidence 0 불변).
**다음 hard blocker(실 데이터로 확정)** — ① **real reviewer 충원**(실 human label JSONL·`label_path` import·gold 없이는 어떤 scorer threshold/embedding 도 provisional) → ② embedding scorer opt-in 실호출 → ③ MERGE_GATE calibration(precision≥0.98·표본 floor) → ④ adjudicator runtime → ⑤ Agent/IU. reviewer/gold 운영 substrate 는 이 턴에 닫음(실 라벨·실 gold·병합은 아님).
**한계** — **이 턴 진전=reviewer/gold operational readiness substrate·실 gold 아님**(production_gold_count 0·synthetic/test 라벨은 simulated only·실 human-reviewed live-derived gold 0·reviewer agreement 실측 0·MERGE_GATE 미충족·embedding/LLM 실호출 0·운영 DB·scheduler·semantic merge·public IU 0). label_source=production+live_derived+정책 충족만 production gold·그 입력(실 라벨) 0.
**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/reviewer_label_operations.py`·`backend/tests/test_reviewer_label_operations.py`·`backend/app/{services/identity_human_labeling,services/identity_eval_dataset,tools/near_match_reviewer_queue,tools/semantic_candidate_scorer}.py`(재사용)·`docs/2_ROADMAP/{00_ROADMAP_INDEX,15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP}.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/{RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS,INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT,EVENT_SCHEMA}.md`·`docs/_CANONICAL/02_CURRENT_ARCHITECTURE.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#43/#44/#45/#59/#65.

### [#67] reviewer batch launch pack + intake validation loop — ADR#66 reviewer label operations 를 **실제 사람이 라벨링을 시작할 수 있는 운영 패키지**(batch pack→assignment→intake validation)로 전환(병합 0·LLM 0·embedding 0·운영 DB 0·실 production gold 0)
- 날짜: 2026-06-26 · 섹터: reviewer batch launch pack(옵션 A) / assignment & duplication policy(B) / intake validation loop(C) / reviewer operations runbook(D) · 상태: **R-IdentityHumanLabeling·R-ReviewerAgreement·R-GoldSamplingBias·R-IdentityEvalDataset·R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator·R-LiveIdentityBacklog·R-SourceOverlapScarcity·R-RealSourceLoopUnproven 부분진전·완전종결=OVERCLAIM·옵션 A+B+C+D 채택·E(embedding/LLM runtime)/F(production merge·DB) 금지·신규 RISK 0**
- **선행: ADR#66 안정 기준점 커밋**(`8776be8`·10파일·제공 메시지 그대로).

**문제(§2 통찰)** — ADR#66 가 만든 것: reviewer queue→packet export→label import→agreement/conflict/adjudication→gold→calibration 의 운영 **함수**. 다음 병목 = **그 함수들이 사람이 바로 라벨링을 시작할 운영 패키지가 아니다**. reviewer instruction·label template·assignment manifest·intake directory·validation command·no-labels report 가 하나의 launch pack 으로 묶여있지 않다(embedding 실호출·production semantic merge·운영 DB·scheduler·public IU 턴 아님). 목표=scorer top-k queue→사람이 바로 라벨링할 batch artifact 로 export→intake validation→ADR#66 gold/calibration 경로 진입.
**원자 분석(§2·20문항)** — ① packet=ADR#66 export 가능하나 **single batch 묶음 없음** ② labeler-facing 에 score/rationale/predicted_status/raw body/secret 구조적 0(`validate_labeling_packet` fail-loud+export leaked 재검사+ADR#60 `hidden_prediction_verified`) ③ instruction=ADR#60 `_REVIEWER_INSTRUCTION` 있으나 §6 **구조적**(4-라벨 정의/금지/권장) 결손 ④ **4-라벨 불일치**: §5/§6 unsure/needs_review vs frozen `GOLD_LABELS`(ambiguous/insufficient)→정규화 매핑 결정(unsure≡insufficient·needs_review≡ambiguous) ⑤ assignment manifest **discrete artifact 없음**(queue 가 reviewers_per_pair=2 배정을 내포만) ⑥ batch_id/assignment_id 결손(pair/packet_id 존재) ⑦ reviewer_id=ADR#66 `pseudonymize_reviewer_id` 재사용 ⑧ roster=operator-local·commit 금지 ⑨ **label template 없음** ⑩ intake directory 관례 없음(`ingestion/outputs/*`만) ⑪ validation command 결손 ⑫ forbidden field=`_validate_reviewer_row` allowlist+intake dry-run 이중 ⑬ no_labels→`awaiting_labels`(정직) ⑭ 실 label→production gold=label_source production AND dataset_source live_derived AND 만장일치 human same/different ⑮ language 보존·KO floor 50 ⑯ hard negative+top-k balanced manifest ⑰ pair 당 ≥2 reviewer(`DEFAULT_REVIEWERS_PER_PAIR`·capacity<2→`insufficient_reviewer_capacity`) ⑱ conflict→`adjudication_queue_from_resolved`(human only) ⑲ R-IdentityHumanLabeling/ReviewerAgreement/GoldSamplingBias=launch-readiness substrate 까지(실 production label 0 불변) ⑳ **다음 hard blocker=first production labels import**(실 reviewer 가 batch pack 으로 라벨 작성→intake). **중복 방지:** ADR#60 `build_reviewer_operating_checklist`·ADR#66 ops·ADR#59 queue **조합**(재구현 0)·신규 파일 1.
**옵션 결정(§3)** — (A) reviewer batch launch pack (B) assignment & duplication policy (C) intake validation loop (D) reviewer operations runbook (E) embedding/LLM scorer runtime (F) production DB activation/semantic merge. **선택: A+B+C+D 채택·E/F 금지.** ADR#67 기록.
**구현(새 파일 1·재구현 0·기존 머신 조합·단방향 import·DB 0)** — 신규 `reviewer_batch_launch.py`(launch-readiness orchestrator): `build_reviewer_instruction`(§6 4-라벨 정의/금지/권장·`model_score_shown`/`predicted_status_shown`/`hidden_candidate_rank_shown`=False)·`build_label_template`(packet→`REVIEWER_ALLOWED_KEYS` 빈 worksheet·reviewer_id pseudonym·score/bucket 0·allowlist 밖 키 fail-loud)·`build_assignment_manifest`(pair 당 ≥2 reviewer·pseudonym only·top-k+hard negative·capacity<2→`insufficient_reviewer_capacity`·`raw_reviewer_pii_committed`=False)·`build_intake_plan`(intake_directory/expected_label_files/validation_command)·`normalize_label`+`_LABELER_TO_GOLD`(labeler vocab→canonical)·`validate_label_intake`(§8 import 前 dry-run: forbidden field/malformed/label_source/reviewer_kind/pair_id/duplicate·`REVIEWER_ALLOWED_KEYS`+enum frozen 재사용·통과 행 canonical 정규화)·`run_reviewer_batch_launch`(§4 통합 output·intake_status[awaiting_labels/labels_present/invalid_labels/imported]·라벨 시 `resolve_label_operations`+`build_calibration_preflight` 직접 재사용[ADR#66 building block·packet 재export 0]·**decisive gold=same/different 만**)·`BATCH_LAUNCH_AGENT_CONTRACT`·CLI(`--validate` dry-run·`--synthetic-labels` 데모). **ADR#66/#60/#59 미변경**(조합·최소 변경).
**검증(결정론 67·실호출 0·DB 0)** — 신규 테스트 **67**(test_reviewer_batch_launch 1-67: batch launch 1-8·reviewer-facing secrecy 9-15·assignment policy 16-22·label template/intake 23-30·agreement/calibration 31-39·no-merge/no-LLM/no-DB/secret 40-46·정규화/production path/drift lock/회귀 cross-check 47-57·**감사 fix-lock 58-67**[adversarial B-1/B-2/B-3·code-review CR-1/CR-3/CR-4 잠금]). backend 비-live **1015 passed/101 skipped/0 failed**(948+67)·ingestion **1353p**(불변)·frontend tsc0/lint0/**test12**(불변)·ruff(E/F/I/B/W−E501) **0**·dead-code(신규 모듈) 0. **live-PG=미실행**(DB 미기동) — 변경이 **DB/session/ORM 무접촉**(orchestrator write-free·`db_write:False`·session 인자 부재·DB 바운드 도구 미사용)→live-PG 무영향(baseline 불변). secret scan PASS(140 files). **자체 발견·수정(decisive gold)**: 2명 만장일치 needs_review(→ambiguous)가 frozen `resolve_gold_from_reviewers` 로 gold 승격 가능→§6 "unsure/needs_review only→not gold" 위반→**production/synthetic gold 를 same/different 만 카운트**(`build_calibration_preflight` 도 decisive production gold 로만·`non_decisive_gold_count` 표면화·test_49 잠금). **honest 동작 입증**: 라벨 없음→`awaiting_labels`·production_gold 0·malformed→`invalid_labels`·model label→거부·unknown pair_id→거부·production+live unanimous human→production_gold 1·calibration_ready False(floor 200)·order-invariant.
**감사(§16)** — adversarial-reality-critic **PROCEED-WITH-FIXES**(cardinal=false-merge/model→gold/labeler-leak/unsure→gold 전부 VALID) + code-review(2 HIGH 실질·3 test/cleanup). **MEDIUM/HIGH 8건 전부 수정**: **CR-1**(HIGH·crash) adjudication label 정규화 부재→labeler vocab(needs_review) adjudication 이 frozen `_validate_adjudication` 크래시→`_normalize_adjudications`(labeler→canonical·canonical passthrough)·테스트 67. **CR-2**(HIGH·latent) CLI `--validate` 가 `--batch-id` 무시·fixture pair_id 하드와이어→실 batch unknown_pair_id→**schema-only**(known_pair_ids=None·pair membership 는 full run). **B-2**(MED) intake 가 frozen `_validate_reviewer_row` 의 reviewed_at/dataset_source/risk_tags 3검사 누락→frozen `_validate_reviewed_at`+`DATASET_SOURCES` 재사용 추가·**검증 동등성 테스트**(test_65). **B-3**(MED) `normalized_rows` 가 raw reviewer_id/rationale 를 `--json` 출력에 노출(ADR#66 대비 PII 퇴행)→`_public_intake_report`(normalized_rows 제거)+duplicate key pseudonymize·테스트 66. **B-1**(MED) production_gold_count "0"=선언 기반→`production_gold_provenance_verified:False` 표면화(merge_allowed False 가 false-merge 방벽). **B-4**(LOW) `_MAX_TITLE_LEN` literal→frozen import. **CR-3** vacuous test_14 수정. **CR-4** coverage(non_decisive/labels_present/run_ block_reason/agreement_rate) 테스트 58-64·**CR-5** 미사용 `reviewers` param 제거. 결과·정정 단일 출처=closeout stamp `audit_evidence`.
**RISK(§11)** — 종결 0·신규 0. 부분진전 8: R-IdentityHumanLabeling(batch launch pack+instruction/template/assignment manifest+intake validation+no-labels 정직·실 production label/gold 0 불변)·R-ReviewerAgreement(pair 당 2-reviewer assignment policy+conflict/adjudication intake 분리·실 합의 0)·R-GoldSamplingBias(top-k+hard negative balanced manifest+top_k_bias_warning+korean floor+capacity warning·실 표집 0)·R-IdentityEvalDataset(batch label→eval/gold input 경로+calibration preflight decisive·MERGE_GATE evidence 0)·R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator(scored queue→reviewer labeling launch·scorer threshold uncalibrated·merge No-Go 유지)·R-LiveIdentityBacklog(scorer top-k queue→batch launch→intake 경로·실 backlog/gold 0)·R-SourceOverlapScarcity(detection scarcity 후속 reviewer launch 운영층·검출 검증 아님)·R-RealSourceLoopUnproven(reviewer launch readiness substrate·실 병합 0). 신규 RISK 후보 R-ReviewerCapacity/R-LabelIntakeOps/R-ReviewerPIIExposure **부재→현 단계 독립 blocker 아님**(capacity warning=manifest 표면화·intake ops=validate dry-run 으로 선제·PII=pseudonymization 구조 봉인)·등록 안 함(남발 금지). **완전종결 금지**(실 production reviewer label·실 gold·reviewer agreement·MERGE_GATE evidence 0 불변).
**다음 hard blocker(실 데이터로 확정)** — ① **first production labels import**(실 reviewer 가 batch pack 으로 라벨 작성→intake→production gold) → ② reviewer recruitment(운영·SLA·roster) → ③ embedding scorer opt-in 실호출 → ④ MERGE_GATE calibration(precision≥0.98·표본 floor) → ⑤ adjudicator runtime → ⑥ Agent/IU. batch launch readiness substrate 는 이 턴에 닫음(실 라벨·실 gold·병합 아님).
**한계** — **이 턴 진전=reviewer batch launch readiness substrate·실 gold 아님**(production_gold_count 0·synthetic/test 라벨은 simulated only·실 human-reviewed live-derived gold 0·reviewer agreement 실측 0·calibration_ready/merge_gate_ready False·embedding/LLM 실호출 0·운영 DB·scheduler·semantic merge·public IU 0). batch pack 은 사람이 라벨링을 *시작*할 운영 패키지이지 라벨/gold 자체가 아니다. labeler vocab(unsure/needs_review)은 frozen canonical(insufficient/ambiguous)로 정규화·둘 다 gold 비대상.
**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/reviewer_batch_launch.py`·`backend/tests/test_reviewer_batch_launch.py`·`backend/app/tools/{reviewer_label_operations,near_match_reviewer_queue,targeted_same_event_acquisition}.py`·`backend/app/services/{identity_human_labeling,identity_eval_dataset}.py`(재사용)·`docs/2_ROADMAP/{00_ROADMAP_INDEX,15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP}.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/{RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS,INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT}.md`·`docs/_CANONICAL/02_CURRENT_ARCHITECTURE.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#59/#60/#65/#66.

### [#68] first production labels import pilot + intake/gold/calibration dry-run — ADR#67 batch launch pack 을 **실제 운영 루프**(filesystem intake→validation→agreement→gold→calibration delta)에 연결(병합 0·LLM 0·embedding 0·운영 DB 0·실 production gold 0)
- 날짜: 2026-06-26 · 섹터: first production label intake pilot(옵션 A) / operator follow-up status report(B) / production label audit manifest(C) / calibration readiness delta report(D) · 상태: **R-IdentityHumanLabeling·R-ReviewerAgreement·R-GoldSamplingBias·R-IdentityEvalDataset·R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator·R-LiveIdentityBacklog·R-SourceOverlapScarcity·R-RealSourceLoopUnproven 부분진전·완전종결=OVERCLAIM·옵션 A+B+C+D 채택·E(embedding/LLM runtime)/F(production merge·DB) 금지·신규 RISK 1(R-ReviewerFollowupOps)**
- **선행: ADR#67 안정 기준점 커밋**(`65065dd`·10파일·제공 메시지 그대로·NO UPSTREAM).

**문제(§2 통찰)** — ADR#67 이 만든 것: reviewer batch launch pack(instruction·label template·assignment manifest·intake plan·validation command·no-labels report)과 in-memory/단일파일 intake dry-run. 다음 병목 = **그 pack 이 아직 실제 운영 루프에 연결되지 않았다** — 실 reviewer 가 작성한 label 파일이 intake_directory 에 들어왔을 때 production label import→validation→agreement→gold 승격→calibration delta 를 닫는 경로가 없다(embedding 실호출·production semantic merge·운영 DB·scheduler·public IU 턴 아님). 목표=batch pack 으로 실 label file 이 들어왔을 때 안전하게 통과/거부하는지 검증·label 없으면 `awaiting_production_labels`(정직)·operator actionable next_action 산출.
**원자 분석(§2·20문항)** — ① launch pack 경로=`build_intake_plan`→`outputs/reviewer_batch/{batch_id}/intake`(문자열만·파일 미작성·디렉토리 현재 **부재**) ② expected=`{batch_id}__{pseudonym}__labels.jsonl`+validation_command ③ **production label 파일 현재 0**(→이번 턴 실제 상태=`awaiting_production_labels`) ④ ADR#67 `awaiting_labels`+next_action 은 있으나 **operator-facing 구조화 no_labels_report 결손**→§5 채움 ⑤ import dry-run=`validate_label_intake`→`resolve_label_operations`→`build_calibration_preflight`(단 **단일파일/in-memory**만·디렉토리 다중파일 스캔 없음) ⑥ schema=template `REVIEWER_ALLOWED_KEYS`=intake `_INTAKE_REQUIRED_KEYS` 정확 일치 ⑦ forbidden field=`FORBIDDEN_LABEL_FIELDS` 행 거부·schema invalid→`normalized_rows=[]`(부분 import 금지) ⑧ reviewer_id PII=`_public_intake_report` strip+duplicate key pseudonymize(B-3) ⑨ pseudonym deterministic(sha1[:12]+`rv_`·salt 없음·저엔트로피 가역 주석) ⑩ pair_id=full run `known_pair_ids=queue['queue_pair_ids']` 강제 ⑪ duplicate=(pair,reviewer,round) 키 거부 ⑫ model/self/LLM=이중가드(validate+resolve fail-loud) ⑬ decisive=same/different 만(ADR#67 자체수정 상속) ⑭ unsure/needs_review→insufficient/ambiguous=non_decisive ⑮ production gold=`label_source==production AND dataset_source==live_derived` decisive·**선언 기반**→`production_gold_provenance_verified:False`(B-1) ⑯ synthetic/test=`evaluate_gold_merge_readiness` live only(자동 배제) ⑰ agreement/conflict=`resolve_label_operations`(agreement_rate/conflict_count/queue) ⑱ denominator=precision(n≥200)/FPR(n≥200&neg>0)/KO(≥50)·gold 0→전부 False ⑲ R-IdentityHumanLabeling/ReviewerAgreement/IdentityEvalDataset=filesystem intake+awaiting 정직+분리+delta 까지(실 label/gold/agreement 0 불변) ⑳ **다음 hard blocker=코드 아님·실 reviewer recruitment/SLA+첫 label 회수**(→신규 R-ReviewerFollowupOps). **추가 발견**: 최상위 `outputs/` 추적 파일 존재+`outputs/.gitignore` 부재→intake label(reviewer_id/rationale PII) **gitignore 안 됨**→`outputs/reviewer_batch/` 가드 추가. EVENT_SCHEMA=순수 Event(reviewer-label 무관·미변경)·docs/3_SOURCE_STATUS* 부재. **중복 방지:** ADR#67 building block(manifest/intake_plan/validate/resolve/preflight)+ADR#66 ops **조합**(재구현 0·새 파일 1).
**옵션 결정(§3)** — (A) first production label intake pilot (B) operator/reviewer follow-up status report (C) production label audit manifest (D) calibration readiness delta report (E) embedding/LLM scorer runtime (F) production DB activation/semantic merge. **선택: A+B+C+D 채택·E/F 금지.** ADR#68 기록.
**구현(새 파일 1·재구현 0·기존 머신 조합·단방향 import·DB 0)** — 신규 `production_label_intake.py`(first production label intake orchestrator): `_scan_intake_dir`(intake_directory `*.jsonl` 다중파일 스캔·basename only PII 차단·JSON 오류→malformed fail-loud·부분 import 금지)·`build_no_labels_report`(§5 operator actionable: intake_directory/expected files/validation command/reviewer count/instruction summary[모델 점수 0]/next action checklist)·`build_calibration_delta`(§8 before/after gold·positive·negative·korean·agreement·conflict delta+precision/FPR/KO denominator readiness+`next_needed_for_merge_gate`)·`run_production_label_intake`(§4 통합: intake_status[awaiting_production_labels/invalid_labels/imported/conflict_pending/calibration_pending]·라벨 시 ADR#66/#67 building block 직접 재사용[decisive gold only·resolve+preflight]·production gold=production&live_derived decisive·duplicate/unknown/forbidden/model count 표면화·pair coverage·`production_gold_provenance_verified:False`)·`PRODUCTION_INTAKE_AGENT_CONTRACT`·CLI(`--intake-dir`/`--synthetic-labels` 데모). **가드: `.gitignore` `outputs/reviewer_batch/`**(실 reviewer label PII 커밋 방지). **ADR#67/#66/#59 미변경**(조합·최소 변경).
**검증(결정론 52·실호출 0·DB 0)** — 신규 테스트 **57**(test_production_label_intake 1-57: no-labels intake 1-6·labels-present validation 7-16·gold policy 17-25·calibration delta 26-32·no-merge/no-LLM/no-DB/secret 33-39·filesystem 다중파일 40-44·contract/drift lock 45-52·감사 fix-lock 53-57). backend 비-live **1072 passed/101 skipped/0 failed**(1015+57)·ingestion **1353p**(불변·미변경)·frontend tsc0/lint0/**test12**(불변·미변경)·ruff(E/F/I/B/W−E501) **0**·dead-code(신규 모듈) 0(535 모듈 스캔·신규 미플래그). **live-PG=미실행**(DB 미기동) — 변경이 **DB/session/ORM 무접촉**(orchestrator write-free·`db_write:False`·session 인자 부재·DB 바운드 도구 미사용)→live-PG 무영향(baseline 불변). 인접 회귀(ADR#65/#66/#67 모듈) **192p**(신규 import 무손상). secret scan PASS·gitignore 가드 IGNORED 확인. **honest 동작 입증**: 파일 없음→`awaiting_production_labels`+no_labels_report·production_gold 0·malformed→`invalid_labels`·forbidden/api_key/raw_body/model label→거부·unknown pair_id→거부·duplicate→count·2인 production+live same→positive gold 1·different→negative gold 1·conflict→`conflict_pending`·adjudicated→gold·unsure/needs_review→non_decisive·synthetic/test/production-tag-but-synthetic-dataset→production gold 0·calibration_ready False(floor 200/50)·delta next_needed actionable.
**감사(§15)** — adversarial-reality-critic + code-review(high effort). cardinal(no-labels 성공포장/synthetic→production/model→human/PII 노출/single→gold/conflict 자동 다수결/실 label 없이 gold 증가/MERGE_GATE 전 merge) 전부 VALID·차단 유지 확인. 발견·수정 단일 출처=closeout stamp `audit_evidence`.
**RISK(§11)** — 종결 0·신규 **1**(R-ReviewerFollowupOps=batch pack 발행됐으나 label 미회수가 독립 blocker로 부상·실제 present blocker). 부분진전 8: R-IdentityHumanLabeling(filesystem production intake+awaiting 정직 보고+production/synthetic/model 분리+calibration delta·실 production label/gold 0 불변)·R-ReviewerAgreement(intake→agreement/conflict report+conflict_pending 분리+capacity warning·실 합의 0)·R-GoldSamplingBias(label coverage+hard negative balance+top_k_bias_warning+positive/negative 표면화·실 표집 0)·R-IdentityEvalDataset(first labels→eval/gold preflight 경로+denominator readiness delta·MERGE_GATE evidence 0)·R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator(production labels→scorer calibration 준비·threshold uncalibrated·merge No-Go 유지)·R-LiveIdentityBacklog(batch launch→production intake 경로·실 backlog/gold 0)·R-SourceOverlapScarcity(detection scarcity 후속 intake 운영층)·R-RealSourceLoopUnproven(intake readiness substrate·실 병합 0). R-ProductionLabelIntake/R-LabelProvenanceIntegrity=**현 단계 독립 blocker 아님**(intake 경로 막 생김·provenance 는 `production_gold_provenance_verified:False`로 R-IdentityHumanLabeling 에 흡수)·등록 안 함(남발 금지). **완전종결 금지**(실 production reviewer label·실 gold·reviewer agreement·MERGE_GATE evidence 0 불변).
**다음 hard blocker(실 데이터로 확정)** — ① **first production label file 회수**(실 reviewer 가 batch pack 으로 라벨 작성→intake_directory 배치·R-ReviewerFollowupOps) → ② reviewer recruitment(운영·SLA·roster) → ③ gold denominator 충족(live 200·KO 50) → ④ MERGE_GATE calibration(precision≥0.98·FPR≤0.01) → ⑤ embedding scorer opt-in 실호출 → ⑥ adjudicator runtime → ⑦ Agent/IU. production intake readiness 는 이 턴에 닫음(실 라벨·실 gold·병합 아님).
**한계** — **이 턴 진전=first production label intake readiness·실 gold 아님**(production_gold_count 0·synthetic/test 라벨은 simulated only·실 human-reviewed live-derived gold 0·reviewer agreement 실측 0·calibration_ready/merge_gate_ready False·embedding/LLM 실호출 0·운영 DB·scheduler·semantic merge·public IU 0). intake pilot 은 실 label file 이 들어왔을 때 안전 통과/거부를 *검증*하는 substrate 이지 라벨/gold 자체가 아니다. no-labels 는 시스템 실패가 아니라 정직한 운영 상태(awaiting)다.
**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/production_label_intake.py`·`backend/tests/test_production_label_intake.py`·`backend/app/tools/{reviewer_batch_launch,reviewer_label_operations,near_match_reviewer_queue}.py`·`backend/app/services/{identity_human_labeling,identity_eval_dataset}.py`(재사용)·`.gitignore`(가드)·`docs/2_ROADMAP/{00_ROADMAP_INDEX,15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP}.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/{RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS,INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT}.md`·`docs/_CANONICAL/02_CURRENT_ARCHITECTURE.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#60/#66/#67.

### [#69] reviewer follow-up operations + label collection status cockpit — ADR#68 이 정직하게 드러낸 운영 병목(batch pack 발행됐으나 실 label 미회수→영구 `awaiting_production_labels`)을 **추적 가능한 운영 상태**로 연결(병합 0·LLM 0·embedding 0·운영 DB 0·**실제 전송 0**·실 label 회수 0)
- 날짜: 2026-06-27 · 섹터: reviewer follow-up status cockpit(옵션 A) / reminder·escalation template(B) / partial label intake status(C) / reviewer SLA·capacity(D) · 상태: **R-ReviewerFollowupOps(#68→#69 진전)·R-IdentityHumanLabeling·R-ReviewerAgreement·R-GoldSamplingBias·R-IdentityEvalDataset·R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator·R-LiveIdentityBacklog·R-SourceOverlapScarcity·R-RealSourceLoopUnproven 부분진전·완전종결=OVERCLAIM·옵션 A+B+C+D 채택·E(embedding/LLM runtime)/F(production merge·DB) 금지·신규 RISK 0**
- **선행: ADR#68 안정 기준점 커밋**(`9fffd00`·11파일·제공 메시지 그대로·NO UPSTREAM).

**문제(§2 통찰)** — ADR#68 `production_label_intake` 는 intake readiness 이지 **reviewer follow-up 운영층이 아니다** — 누가 어떤 batch/pair 를 맡았고, 어떤 label 이 아직 missing 인지, 언제까지 회수해야 하는지, 어떤 reviewer 에게 reminder/escalation 해야 하는지를 PII-safe 하게 추적하는 cockpit 이 없다. no-labels 는 시스템 실패가 아니라 **운영 상태**이고, 운영 상태는 tracking 되어야 한다(embedding 실호출·production merge·운영 DB·scheduler·public IU 턴 아님). 목표=batch→assignment→follow-up→intake→validation→agreement→gold→calibration 전체를 운영 추적 가능하게·실제 email/slack 전송은 하지 않고 메시지 템플릿·operator checklist 만.
**원자 분석(§2·20문항)** — ① ADR#68 no_labels_report 는 operator next_action 은 있으나 reviewer 별 missing/부분제출/escalation 단위 결손→§A 보강 ② `build_assignment_manifest`(per `(reviewer_pseudonym, pair_id)`)+`build_intake_plan`(expected `{batch_id}__{pseudonym}__labels.jsonl`)=follow-up 단위 충분 ③ manifest assignment group→reviewer 별 assigned pairs·차집합=missing ④ template 의 reviewer_id 가 **이미 pseudonymize** → 제출행 reviewer_id == manifest pseudonym → **재pseudonymize 0** coverage(raw roster 불요) ⑤ pseudonym/basename/pair_id 만으로 cockpit 완결(local mapping 불요) ⑥ capacity<2=`manifest['capacity_status']` insufficient→escalation ⑦ expected(assignment 튜플) vs actual(valid 제출 튜플) 차집합 ⑧ `missing_by_reviewer_pseudonym`/`missing_by_pair_id` 대칭 ⑨ reminder 포함=batch/packet/pseudonym/missing count/expected filename/validation command/allowed labels·**금지**=raw name/email/phone·score·rationale·predicted_status·raw body·secret·hidden rank(allowlist+`_REMINDER_FORBIDDEN_KEYS` 가드) ⑩ escalation=조건별 action(capacity/no_labels/partial/invalid/conflict/calibration)·**전송 0** ⑪ partial=새 상태(intake 가 awaiting/imported 로 흡수하던 것 분리) ⑫ invalid→correction request(reason code+basename only·값 0) ⑬ conflict_pending→adjudicator follow-up(intake `conflict_count`) ⑭ **follow-up 이 production_gold_count 증가 0**(intake exact passthrough·test 39 lock) ⑮ 출력 표면 score/rationale/predicted/raw body/secret/raw reviewer_id 0 ⑯ output path gitignored(ADR#68 outputs/reviewer_batch/) ⑰ Agent contract=follow-up/reminder/capacity/calibration 계획 가능·조작/merge/전송 불가 ⑱ R-ReviewerFollowupOps=cockpit+reminder+SLA 까지(실 label 회수·실 SLA 운영 0 불변) ⑲ R-IdentityHumanLabeling/ReviewerAgreement/GoldSamplingBias=missing/partial 추적·reviewer coverage·hard-neg/korean gap 표면화(실 표본 0) ⑳ **다음 hard blocker=actual reviewer contact/첫 returned labels**(embedding scorer 는 그 다음·floor 미충족). 추가 발견: `production_label_intake` 출력에 `conflict_count` 미노출(conflict_rate 만)→followup 의 `conflict_pair_count`(§4 필수) 위해 **additive 1줄 노출**(reimplementation 회피). docs/3_SOURCE_STATUS* 부재·EVENT_SCHEMA(DB-free) 무변경. **중복 방지:** `run_production_label_intake`(단일 출처)+`build_assignment_manifest`/`build_intake_plan`(ADR#67) 조합·재구현 0.
**옵션 결정(§3)** — (A) reviewer follow-up status cockpit (B) reminder/escalation template pack (C) partial label intake status (D) reviewer SLA/capacity plan (E) embedding/LLM scorer runtime (F) production DB activation/semantic merge. **선택: A+B+C+D 채택·E/F 금지.** ADR#69 기록.
**구현(새 파일 1·재구현 0·기존 머신 조합·단방향 import·DB 0·전송 0)** — 신규 `reviewer_followup_ops.py`(follow-up orchestrator): `compute_coverage`(assignment(expected) vs 회수(actual)·가명 공간·`missing_by_reviewer_pseudonym`/`missing_by_pair_id`·pair/reviewer coverage rate·unmatched_submission)·`_attribute_files`(per-file 검증 attribution·basename→reason code·값 0·malformed fail-loud)·`build_reminder_templates`(§B reviewer 별 first/missing·PII-safe allowlist+`_REMINDER_FORBIDDEN_KEYS` 구조적 fail-loud·전송 0)·`build_escalation_actions`(§B 조건별 action·capacity/no_labels/partial/invalid[reason code]/conflict/calibration)·`run_reviewer_followup_ops`(§4 통합: **7-state** followup_status[not_launchable/no_labels/partial_labels/invalid_labels/conflict_pending/calibration_pending/imported_ready_for_merge_gate_review]·precedence **invalid>partial fail-loud**·`run_production_label_intake` 단일 출처 호출→intake_status/gold/calibration/`conflict_count` **exact passthrough**·reviewer SLA·`_operator_checklist`)·`REVIEWER_FOLLOWUP_AGENT_CONTRACT`·CLI(`--intake-dir`/`--synthetic-labels` partial 데모). **additive: `production_label_intake` 출력에 `conflict_count` 1줄 노출**(followup conflict_pair_count 소스·ADR#68 테스트 57 무영향). **ADR#68 커밋분(orchestrator/test/gitignore) 미변경**(intake additive 1줄·최소 변경).
**검증(결정론 57·실호출 0·DB 0·전송 0)** — 신규 테스트 **61**(test_reviewer_followup_ops 1-61: follow-up status 1-7·expected vs actual 8-18·reminder/escalation 19-28·PII/secret 29-34·no-merge/LLM/DB 35-40·filesystem 41-43·contract/policy lock 44-57·감사 fix-lock 58-61). backend 비-live **1133 passed/101 skipped/0 failed**(1072+61)·ingestion **1353p**(불변)·frontend tsc0/lint0/**test12**(무변경·프론트 변경 0)·ruff(E/F/I/B/W−E501) **0**·dead-code 0(537 모듈·reviewer_followup_ops 미플래그)·secret scan **PASS(288 files)**. **live-PG=미실행**(DB 미기동) — 변경이 **DB/session/ORM 무접촉**(orchestrator write-free·`db_write:False`·session 인자 부재·DB 바운드 도구 미사용)→무영향(baseline 91 불변). **honest 동작 입증**: assignment 0→`not_launchable`·라벨 0→`no_labels`(first reminder)·일부→`partial_labels`(missing reminder·pair_rate<1·reviewer_rate 1.0)·forbidden/duplicate/unknown pair/model label→`invalid_labels`(correction request·reason code only)·full+conflict→`conflict_pending`(adjudicator action)·full+무충돌+floor 미달→`calibration_pending`(collect more)·capacity<2→insufficient escalation·**production_gold_count=intake exact passthrough(follow-up 미증가)**·merge_allowed False·전송 0(smtp/webhook/mailto 미존재)·raw reviewer id/email 미노출·basename only·절대경로 사용자명 미노출.
**감사(§15)** — adversarial-reality-critic + code-review(high effort). cardinal(production intake 만으로 follow-up 불필요/no-labels 성공포장/synthetic→production/model→human/PII 노출/single→gold/conflict 자동 다수결/실 label 없이 gold 증가/MERGE_GATE 전 merge/실제 전송) 전부 차단 유지 확인. **발견·수정 2 MEDIUM+1 LOW**: ① adversarial MEDIUM(`_attribute_files` 임의 파일명 verbatim→운영자 실명 파일 시 PII 누출·'reviewer raw PII 0' OVERCLAIM)→기대 가명 패턴 밖 파일명 `nonconforming_file_N` 마스킹+`nonconforming_filenames_count`+test_60. ② code-review MEDIUM(filesystem 다중파일에서 per-file attribution≠intake combined→cross-file duplicate 누락·malformed 단락 시 forbidden/unknown/model 카운트·basename 불일치)→`_attribute_files` 를 **단일 combined validation+row→file attribution** 으로 재작성·rejection 카운트/invalid_by_file_basename/INVALID sub-reason 단일 출처+test_58/59. ③ LOW(not_launchable 시 assign_more_reviewers escalation noise)→assignments>0 가드+test_61. 코어(coverage math/precedence/passthrough/conflict_count UnboundLocal) 전부 REFUTED(정상). 테스트 작성 중 self-fix=test_17(rationale 는 reviewer 허용 필드·forbidden 아님→predicted_status)·test_23(1-reviewer queue 빌드 크래시→reviewers_per_pair=1)·test_28(agent_contract 의 "webhook 전송 금지" 명시→검사 범위를 reminder/escalation artifact 로 한정). 발견·수정 단일 출처=closeout stamp `audit_evidence`.
**RISK(§11)** — 종결 0·신규 **0**. 부분진전 9: **R-ReviewerFollowupOps**(#68→#69 진전: follow-up status cockpit+reminder/escalation template[전송 0]+expected vs actual+7-state+PII-safe·**실 label 회수·실 SLA 운영 0 불변→완전종결 금지**)·R-IdentityHumanLabeling(reviewer 별 missing/partial 추적+production_gold_count exact passthrough)·R-ReviewerAgreement(reviewer coverage+missing reviewer+conflict/adjudication follow-up)·R-GoldSamplingBias(pair/reviewer coverage+hard-negative/korean gap+calibration_pending action·**R-PartialLabelDrift watch**[편향 회수 시 denominator 편향·현재 실 회수 0이라 미등록])·R-IdentityEvalDataset(label collection status→denominator planning)·R-SemanticIdentityAdjudicator(follow-up→실 label 회수 운영층·merge No-Go 유지)·R-LiveIdentityBacklog(follow-up→실 label 회수 추적)·R-SourceOverlapScarcity·R-RealSourceLoopUnproven(follow-up 운영 cockpit substrate·실 병합 0). **신규 RISK 후보(R-ReviewerSLA/R-ReviewerPIIInArtifacts/R-PartialLabelDrift)=현 단계 present blocker 아님**(실 회수 0·PII 구조적 차단·partial-drift 가설)→미등록(남발 금지). **완전종결 금지**(실 production reviewer label·실 gold·실 label 회수·실 SLA 운영 0 불변).
**다음 hard blocker(실 데이터로 확정)** — ① **actual reviewer contact + 첫 returned labels 회수**(follow-up cockpit 으로 추적·R-ReviewerFollowupOps) → ② reviewer recruitment(운영·SLA·roster) → ③ gold denominator 충족(live 200·KO 50) → ④ MERGE_GATE calibration(precision≥0.98·FPR≤0.01) → ⑤ embedding scorer opt-in 실호출 → ⑥ adjudicator runtime → ⑦ Agent/IU. follow-up 운영 readiness 는 이 턴에 닫음(실 라벨·실 gold·실 회수 아님).
**한계** — **이 턴 진전=follow-up 운영 cockpit substrate·실 label 회수 아님**(production_gold_count 0·intake exact passthrough·follow-up 만으로 미증가·실 production reviewer label·실 gold·실 회수·실 SLA 운영 0·reviewer 합의 실측 0·calibration_ready/merge_gate_ready False·**실제 email/slack/webhook 전송 0**·embedding/LLM 실호출 0·운영 DB·scheduler·semantic merge·public IU 0). reminder/escalation 은 **메시지 템플릿·operator checklist** 일 뿐 실 전송이 아니다. no-labels/partial 은 시스템 실패가 아니라 정직한 운영 상태다.
**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/reviewer_followup_ops.py`·`backend/tests/test_reviewer_followup_ops.py`·`backend/app/tools/production_label_intake.py`(conflict_count additive)·`backend/app/tools/{reviewer_batch_launch,reviewer_label_operations,near_match_reviewer_queue}.py`·`backend/app/services/identity_human_labeling.py`(재사용)·`docs/2_ROADMAP/{00_ROADMAP_INDEX,15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP}.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/{RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS,INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT}.md`·`docs/_CANONICAL/02_CURRENT_ARCHITECTURE.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#66/#67/#68.

### [#70] actual reviewer pilot handoff bundle + returned-label gate — ADR#69 follow-up cockpit 을 **실 reviewer pilot 을 시작 가능한 handoff** 로 전환(병합 0·LLM 0·embedding 0·운영 DB 0·**실제 전송 0**·실 reviewer contact 0·실 returned labels 0)
- 날짜: 2026-06-27 · 섹터: actual reviewer pilot handoff bundle(옵션 A) / returned-label gate runner(B) / pilot status report(C) / ops UI seed contract(D) · 상태: **R-ReviewerPilotExecution(신규 MEDIUM)·R-OpsUIPrematureTruth(신규 LOW)·R-ReviewerFollowupOps(#69→#70 진전)·R-IdentityHumanLabeling·R-ReviewerAgreement·R-GoldSamplingBias·R-IdentityEvalDataset 부분진전·완전종결=OVERCLAIM·옵션 A+B+C+D 채택·E(embedding/LLM runtime)/F(production merge·DB) 금지·신규 RISK 2**
- **선행: ADR#69 안정 기준점 커밋**(`8587d53`·11파일·제공 메시지 그대로·NO UPSTREAM).

**문제(§2 통찰)** — ADR#69 `reviewer_followup_ops` 는 누가 무엇을 빠뜨렸는지 **추적**하는 운영 cockpit 이지, 운영자가 실 reviewer 에게 **무엇을 건네야** 첫 라벨 회수가 시작되는지(단일 handoff bundle)와 "아직 접촉 전(ready_to_contact)"인지 "회수 대기(awaiting_reviewer_return)"인지가 분리돼 있지 않다. 그리고 returned label 이 들어오면 intake→followup→agreement/gold/calibration delta 를 **end-to-end** 로 닫는 단일 entrypoint 와, 미래 internal ops UI 가 읽을 status contract 가 없다. 목표=actual sending 은 하지 않되 operator 가 그대로 쓸 수 있는 pilot handoff package 를 만들고, labels 가 있으면 즉시 import 검증(embedding 실호출·production merge·운영 DB·scheduler·public IU 턴 아님).
**원자 분석(§2·20문항)** — ① handoff artifacts 는 전부 기존 pure builder(`build_reviewer_instruction`/`build_label_template`/`build_assignment_manifest`/`build_intake_plan`) ② 최소 bundle=instruction+reviewer 별 assignment summary+expected filename+template schema+intake dir+validation command+allowed labels+due_hint ③ intake_directory=`outputs/reviewer_batch/{batch_id}/intake`·expected=`{batch_id}__{pseudonym}__labels.jsonl` ④ returned files 현재 0(gitignore·실 회수 0)→기본 ready_to_contact/awaiting ⑤ 있으면 followup→intake passthrough 로 즉시 end-to-end(새 코드 불필요) ⑥ 없으면 followup 은 no_labels·reminder 산출하나 "단일 handoff bundle"·"접촉 전/후 구분" 결손→pilot 이 채움 ⑦ reminder(재촉)≠최초 handoff(무엇을 주는가)→bundle manifest 필요 ⑧⑨ raw PII 없이 bundle 구성 가능(전부 pseudonym·allowlist·roster mapping operator-local) ⑩ 8-state pilot_status(no_labels 를 ready_to_contact/awaiting 로 분할) ⑪ invalid correction=invalid_by_file_basename→reason code(값 0) ⑫ conflict→adjudication_handoff(human lead·자동 다수결 금지) ⑬ calibration_gap=intake calibration_delta.next_needed(live gold·KO·negative·MERGE_GATE) ⑭ production_gold_count followup→intake **exact passthrough**(handoff 재계산 0·test 15 lock) ⑮ `.gitignore:81 outputs/reviewer_batch/` 실 label gitignored 확인 ⑯ actual sending 0(템플릿/명세만) ⑰ R-ReviewerFollowupOps=handoff bundle+returned-gate+8-state+ops UI 까지(실 contact·실 returned 0 불변) ⑱ R-IdentityHumanLabeling/Agreement/EvalDataset=실 label 경로·denominator 통로 확정(실 label 0) ⑲ **다음 hard blocker=returned labels 자체**(실 reviewer contact+회수)→R-ReviewerPilotExecution 신규 ⑳ ops UI seed contract(OpsReviewBatchStatus)→internal ops dashboard 착수 가능(workflow state 시각화·public IU UI 는 여전히 No-Go). **핵심 발견**: `_scan_intake_dir`/builder 가 mkdir 안 함 → **intake dir 존재 여부가 ready_to_contact(미설정) vs awaiting(설정·빈)의 정직한 신호**. **docs/3_SOURCE_STATUS\* 부재**(docs/3_\*=3_ARCHIVE)·`19_WEB_INTELLIGENCE_IMPLEMENTATION_SPEC` 존재·EVENT_SCHEMA(DB-free) 무변경. **중복 방지:** `run_reviewer_followup_ops`(단일 출처)+ADR#67 pure builder 조합·재구현 0.
**옵션 결정(§3)** — (A) actual reviewer pilot handoff bundle (B) returned-label gate runner (C) pilot status report (D) ops UI seed contract[docs/schema+최소 코드] (E) embedding/LLM scorer runtime (F) production DB activation/semantic merge. **선택: A+B+C+D 채택·E/F 금지.** ADR#70 기록.
**구현(새 파일 1·재구현 0·ADR#69 `run_reviewer_followup_ops` 단일 호출 decorate·단방향 import·DB 0·전송 0)** — 신규 `reviewer_pilot_handoff.py`(pilot handoff orchestrator): `build_pilot_handoff_bundle`(§A operator 배포용 instruction·reviewer 별 assignment summary·label template schema[fill/fixed columns·allowed labels/confidences]·expected filename·intake dir·validation command·allowed labels·pseudonym only·**`_assert_pii_safe` 재귀 forbidden-key 가드**·전송 0)·`_pilot_status`(§5 **8-state**·followup 7-state 매핑+**`_intake_dir_established` 존재로 접촉 전(ready_to_contact)/회수 대기(awaiting_reviewer_return) 분할**)·`build_correction_templates`(§7 invalid 파일별 reason code only·값 0)·`build_adjudication_handoff`(§7 conflict→human lead·**자동 다수결 금지**)·`build_calibration_gap`(§7 gold/KO/negative gap·intake passthrough)·`build_ops_ui_contract`(§8 OpsReviewBatchStatus·`flags{no_merge,no_public_iu,pii_safe,no_llm,no_db_write,gold_provenance_verified}`·public truth 아님)·`run_reviewer_pilot_handoff`(§4 통합: followup 단일 호출 decorate→returned-label gate·gold/calibration **exact passthrough**·`actual_sending_performed`/`pilot_executed`=False)·`REVIEWER_PILOT_AGENT_CONTRACT`·CLI. **ADR#69 커밋분(followup/intake/docs) 미변경**(pilot 은 followup 호출만·최소 변경).
**검증(결정론 57·실호출 0·DB 0·전송 0)** — 신규 테스트 **57**(test_reviewer_pilot_handoff 1-57: pilot handoff readiness 1-8·returned-label gate 9-15·safety 16-24·templates 25-30·ops UI contract 31-36·no-merge/LLM/DB 37-42·contract/policy lock 43-52·**감사 fix-lock 53-57**). backend 비-live **1190 passed/101 skipped/0 failed**(1133+57; full run 앵커 1185[52-test]·1189[56-test]+격리 leaf +1[`reviewer_pilot_handoff` 비-test importer 0 검증])·ingestion **1353p**(불변)·frontend tsc0/lint0/**test12**(무변경·프론트 변경 0)·ruff(E/F/I/B/W−E501) **0**·dead-code(신규 모듈) **미플래그**(539 모듈·repo baseline 238 advisory)·secret scan **PASS**. **live-PG=미실행**(DB 미기동) — 변경이 **DB/session/ORM 무접촉**(pilot write-free·`db_write:False`·session 인자 부재·DB 바운드 도구 미사용)→무영향(baseline 91 불변). **honest 동작 입증**: bundle 완성+intake dir 미존재→`ready_to_contact`(접촉 전)·존재·빈→`awaiting_reviewer_return`(회수 대기)·일부 회수→`partial_returned`·forbidden/malformed→`invalid_returned`(correction request·reason code only)·full+conflict→`conflict_pending`(adjudication handoff·자동 다수결 금지)·full+무충돌+floor 미달→`calibration_pending`(calibration gap)·empty queue→`not_ready`·**production_gold_count=followup→intake exact passthrough(handoff 미증가·test 15)**·merge_allowed False·`actual_sending_performed`/`pilot_executed` False·전송 0(smtp/webhook/mailto 미존재)·raw reviewer id/email 미노출·basename only·절대경로 사용자명 미노출.
**감사(§15)** — adversarial-reality-critic + code-review(high effort). cardinal(handoff cockpit 만으로 실 pilot 됐다/no-labels 성공포장/synthetic→production/model→human/PII 노출/single→gold/conflict 자동 다수결/실 label 없이 gold 증가/MERGE_GATE 전 merge/실제 전송) 전부 차단 유지 확인. **adversarial=PROCEED-WITH-FIXES·발견·수정 2 MEDIUM+1 LOW-MEDIUM**: ① MEDIUM(`build_ops_ui_contract` 가 production_gold_count/merge_gate_ready 노출하며 `production_gold_provenance_verified` caveat 누락→미래 dashboard 가 미검증 gold 를 검증된 truth 로 렌더 가능·forward-looking seed 에 박제)→contract 에 `production_gold_provenance_verified`+`synthetic_gold_count`+`flags.gold_provenance_verified` 추가+test_53. ② MEDIUM(ready_to_contact vs awaiting 가 `Path.exists()` 프록시라 "dir 존재"가 "reviewer 접촉"으로 둔갑·반대로 미설정이면 미접촉 함의)→`_intake_dir_established`(접촉 검증 아닌 경로 설정 프록시 명시)+미사용 `returned_count` 인자 제거+`intake_directory_established` 필드+awaiting next_action 보정+test_56. ③ LOW-MEDIUM(재귀 PII 가드가 bundle/correction 만 덮고 전체 출력·미래 드리프트 미차단 + "actual pilot" 명명 과대→"bundle 존재=pilot 실행" conflation 위험)→`_assert_pii_safe(result)` 전체 출력 1회 호출+`pilot_executed`/`real_reviewers_contacted`/`real_labels_returned` 명시 필드+test_54/55. **code-review=HIGH/MEDIUM 0·LOW 2**: ① LOW(malformed JSONL 은 0행 파싱→ops_ui invalid_label_count=0 이지만 pilot_status=invalid_returned→seed contract 자기모순)→`invalid_file_count`(파일 단위) 추가+test_57. ② LOW(label_rows+intake_directory 동시 입력 시 표시 intake_directory 가 무시된 dir·labels 는 in-memory)=비현실 조합·followup 충실 passthrough→**수용**(코드 변경 0). 코어(gold inflate·merge 활성화·전송 호출·followup/intake 발산·**`_assert_pii_safe(result)` 거짓양성 크래시**) 전부 REFUTED(정상). 발견·수정 단일 출처=closeout stamp `audit_evidence`.
**RISK(§11)** — 종결 0·**신규 2**(실 present blocker만): **R-ReviewerPilotExecution**(MEDIUM·pilot handoff bundle 은 있으나 실 reviewer contact·첫 returned labels 미실행·R-ReviewerFollowupOps 추적층에서 분리된 **실행층** blocker·실 reviewer ≥2 가 bundle 로 작성→회수→pilot_status partial/conflict/calibration/imported 진입 전까지 완전종결 금지)·**R-OpsUIPrematureTruth**(LOW·ops UI seed contract 가 public truth 로 오인될 위험·구조적 flags+provenance caveat 로 완화·internal/public surface 물리 분리 강제는 구현 시 잔여). **R-ReturnedLabelQuality=returned labels 0이라 가설→미등록**(watch only·남발 금지). 부분진전 5: **R-ReviewerFollowupOps**(#69→#70: handoff bundle+8-state pilot_status+returned-label gate+correction/adjudication/calibration handoff+ops UI contract·**실 reviewer contact·실 returned labels 0 불변→완전종결 금지**)·R-IdentityHumanLabeling(handoff→실 label 경로·production_gold_count exact passthrough)·R-ReviewerAgreement(conflict→adjudication handoff)·R-GoldSamplingBias(calibration_gap 표면화)·R-IdentityEvalDataset(returned label→denominator planning·ops UI denominator status). **완전종결 금지**(실 reviewer contact·실 returned labels·실 gold·실 SLA 운영 0 불변).
**다음 hard blocker(실 데이터로 확정)** — ① **actual reviewer contact + 첫 returned labels 회수**(pilot handoff bundle 로 시작·returned-label gate 로 검증·R-ReviewerPilotExecution) → ② reviewer recruitment(운영·SLA·roster) → ③ gold denominator 충족(live 200·KO 50) → ④ MERGE_GATE calibration(precision≥0.98·FPR≤0.01) → ⑤ embedding scorer opt-in 실호출 → ⑥ adjudicator runtime → ⑦ Agent/IU. pilot handoff readiness 는 이 턴에 닫음(실 reviewer 실행·실 gold·실 회수 아님). internal ops dashboard 는 `OpsReviewBatchStatus` contract 위에서 착수 가능(public IU UI 는 No-Go).
**한계** — **이 턴 진전=pilot handoff bundle+returned-label gate substrate·실 reviewer 실행 아님**(production_gold_count 0·followup→intake exact passthrough·handoff 만으로 미증가·`pilot_executed`=False·real_reviewers_contacted 0·실 production reviewer label·실 gold·실 returned labels·실 SLA 운영 0·reviewer 합의 실측 0·calibration_ready/merge_gate_ready False·**실제 email/slack/webhook 전송 0**·embedding/LLM 실호출 0·운영 DB·scheduler·semantic merge·public IU 0). bundle/reminder/correction/adjudication 은 **명세/템플릿**일 뿐 실 전송이 아니다. ops UI seed contract 는 internal workflow state 이지 public truth 가 아니다. ready_to_contact/awaiting/partial 은 시스템 실패가 아니라 정직한 운영 상태다.
**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/reviewer_pilot_handoff.py`·`backend/tests/test_reviewer_pilot_handoff.py`·`backend/app/tools/{reviewer_followup_ops,production_label_intake,reviewer_batch_launch,reviewer_label_operations,near_match_reviewer_queue}.py`(재사용·미변경)·`docs/2_ROADMAP/{00_ROADMAP_INDEX,15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP,19_WEB_INTELLIGENCE_IMPLEMENTATION_SPEC}.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/{RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS,INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT}.md`·`docs/_CANONICAL/02_CURRENT_ARCHITECTURE.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#67/#68/#69.

### [#71] reviewer pilot execution ledger + first returned-labels monitor — ADR#70 handoff readiness 를 **실 pilot 실행 상태 추적**으로 전환(병합 0·LLM 0·embedding 0·운영 DB 0·**실제 전송 0**·실 reviewer contact 0·실 returned labels 0)
- 날짜: 2026-06-27 · 섹터: reviewer pilot execution ledger(옵션 A) / returned labels monitor(B) / operator SLA·checklist(C) / ops UI execution contract(D·docs+schema) · 상태: **R-ReviewerPilotExecution(#70→#71 진전)·R-OpsUIPrematureTruth(#70→#71 진전)·R-ReviewerFollowupOps·R-IdentityHumanLabeling·R-ReviewerAgreement·R-GoldSamplingBias·R-IdentityEvalDataset 부분진전·완전종결=OVERCLAIM·옵션 A+B+C+D 채택·E(embedding/LLM runtime)/F(production merge·DB) 금지·신규 RISK 2(R-ContactEvidenceIntegrity MEDIUM·R-ReviewerContactPII LOW)**
- **선행: ADR#70 안정 기준점 커밋**(`e9cd1ff`·11파일·제공 메시지 그대로·NO UPSTREAM).

**문제(§2 통찰)** — ADR#70 `reviewer_pilot_handoff` 는 operator 가 배포 가능한 handoff bundle·returned-label gate·8-state pilot_status 를 닫았으나, `pilot_executed`/`real_reviewers_contacted` 가 **contact evidence 입력 통로 부재로 하드코딩 False/0** 이다 — "번들 있음"이 "pilot 실행됨"으로 둔갑할 자리(ready_to_contact 가 contacted 로 둔갑). operator 가 실제로 reviewer 에게 bundle 을 건넸는지(contact), 어떤 pseudonym 이 어떤 batch 를 받았는지, 첫 returned label 이 들어왔는지를 PII-safe ledger 로 추적하는 **실행층**이 없다. 목표=실 reviewer 에게 *연락했다는 사실을 임의로 만들지 않고*(operator evidence 없으면 미접촉 유지) execution 상태를 추적하고, labels 가 있으면 즉시 intake/gold/calibration 으로 통과(embedding 실호출·production merge·운영 DB·scheduler·public IU 턴 아님).
**원자 분석(§2·20문항)** — ① handoff bundle 에 실행 필드 자리(`pilot_executed`/`real_reviewers_contacted`/`intake_directory_established`)는 있으나 evidence 입력 통로 0(하드코딩) ② 세 필드는 `reviewer_pilot_handoff.py:485-488` 에서 contact evidence 부재로 구조적 False/0 ③ contact evidence schema=batch_id+reviewer_pseudonym+contact_method_label+contact_status+contacted_at+due_hint+operator_note_code ④ **둔갑 차단**: real_reviewers_contacted=contact_status=contacted 만(evidence 0→0·prepared≠contacted)→R-ContactEvidenceIntegrity ⑤ raw PII 는 `_assert_pii_safe`/`_HANDOFF_FORBIDDEN_KEYS` 재사용+allowlist+값-레벨 가드로 fail-loud→R-ReviewerContactPII ⑥ evidence 는 `.gitignore:82 outputs/reviewer_batch/` gitignore·docs 엔 schema/example only ⑦ **전송 0**(`.env.example` SLACK/EMAIL/WEBHOOK/SMTP 키 0·evidence 는 *기록*) ⑧ returned-label gate 는 contact evidence 와 **독립**(label_rows/intake_directory 만)·execution_status 에서만 결합 ⑨ no-labels→evidence 없으면 awaiting_operator_contact·있으면 contacted_waiting_return ⑩ `run_reviewer_pilot_handoff` 단일 호출이 이미 intake→followup→handoff 체인→execution 은 decorate(재호출 0) ⑪ OpsReviewBatchStatus 에 execution 필드 부재→`InternalOpsPilotExecutionStatus` 확장 ⑫ pilot_status(회수경로 축)와 직교하는 **contact 축**을 execution_status 가 분리 ⑬ actual contact=operator manual(코드는 bundle 생성·evidence 소비·label 검증만) ⑭ SLA=`reviewer_sla` 재사용+per-pseudonym checklist(assigned/contact_status/returned_file_status/missing/due/overdue/next_action) ⑮ labels 전 embedding opt-in=RAG_KG Cond4/5 FAIL(gold 0·calibration 0)→E 금지 ⑯
