## ADR#75 — R1 first reviewer pilot batch freeze + operator launch handoff + internal ops launch readiness

**선행** — ADR#74(R1 gold acquisition operating plan + internal ops R1 gap + source storage strategy)를 안정 기준점으로 커밋(`4de4fc0`·19파일·제공 메시지 그대로·secret PASS·docs_lifecycle conflicts 0·push 0·NO UPSTREAM). 이 커밋을 ADR#75 의 기준점으로 삼음.

**문제(§2)** — ADR#74 는 R1 *plan*(무엇을 얼마나 모아야 하는가)일 뿐 — 실제 reviewer 에게 넘길 **동결된 첫 pilot batch**(frozen reviewer worklist·deterministic signature·expected label files·intake/validation 경로를 하나의 immutable batch 로 묶은 것)·운영자가 그대로 수동 실행하는 **operator launch package**·internal ops UI 의 **launch readiness** 가 없었다. "R1 plan 이 있으니 라벨 수집이 시작됐다"로 착각할 자리가 남는다.

**원자 분석(§2·20문항·구현 전 보고)** — ① reviewer candidate pair source=`source_overlap_discovery.build_captured_overlap_fixture`(**합성** GDELT 형태 fixture·계약/입도 검증용)→`discover_overlap`(순수·오프라인·LLM 0)→`build_near_match_reviewer_queue`(LLM 0) ② captured fixture→**5 distinct near-match pair**(nm:0-2/0-3/1-2/1-3/2-3)·10 packet row(2 reviewer/pair)·구조적 freeze 충분하나 **합성** ③ 실 production 후보=live source overlap(credentials·live fetch·이번 턴 No-Go)→오프라인은 합성 fixture 뿐 ④ freeze→truth claim 오인 위험 있음→`candidate_provenance=synthetic_fixture`·`pilot_batch_is_production_candidate=False`·copy·production_gold_count 0·test 로 차단 ⑤ frozen pair=`build_label_template`(REVIEWER_ALLOWED_KEYS allowlist·fail-loud)+`_assert_pii_safe`→score/rationale/predicted_status 부재 ⑥ pair_id/source_role/title/canonical_url/observed_at/language 사용 가능·source_name/topic/time_window 부재→**날조 안 함** ⑦ `_batch_signature` deterministic sha256(정렬 pair 정체성+config·wall-clock/PII/score 제외) ⑧ expected files↔intake_dir↔validation_command 일치(`build_intake_plan` +intake_dir override→게이트 스캔 경로 단일 수렴) ⑨ template/instruction/manifest 동일 queue/batch_id 파생(발산 0) ⑩ validation_command=reviewer_batch_launch --validate 참조 ⑪ operator launch checklist 수동 실행 가능 ⑫ actual sending 0 ⑬ reviewer raw PII 없이 handoff(pseudonym only) ⑭ internal ops UI frozen/ready/awaiting 표시 가능(신규 endpoint+패널) ⑮ actual labels 있으면 gate 단일 호출이 이미 end-to-end intake→`launch_status=labels_present` ⑯ R1 gap↔frozen size 연결(current_r1_gap=max(0,200−prod)·frozen 5·target 200) ⑰ frozen 5<<target 200→**pilot_n**·R1 blocked_no_labels 유지 ⑱ community/market/storage 미혼입(frozen pair=source_role만·storage=docs-only) ⑲ R-GoldAcquisitionPlanOnly 부분진전(freeze machinery+operator package+ready_for_manual_launch·완전종결 금지) ⑳ 다음 hard blocker 순서=실 production candidate(live overlap)→실 reviewer contact/recruitment→actual returned labels. **핵심 정직성 결정: 합성 fixture 를 production 후보로 둔갑 0**(freeze=machinery 증명·라벨 회수해도 dataset_source=synthetic→production gold 미승격·machinery 강제).

**옵션 결정(§3)** — (A) actual returned labels re-check (B) R1 first pilot batch freeze (C) operator launch handoff package (D) internal ops launch-readiness visibility[제한적] (E) embedding/LLM scorer runtime (F) production DB·semantic merge·public IU. **선택: A+B+C+D(제한적) 채택·E/F 금지.** ADR#75 기록.

**구현(신규 코드 1[+test 1]·기존 보강·재구현 0·`run_actual_input_gate` 단일 호출 re-check·순수 builder freeze·DB 0·전송 0·secret 값 미열람)** — 신규 `r1_reviewer_pilot_batch.py`(freeze+handoff orchestrator): `run_actual_input_gate` 단일 호출 re-check(no_actual_input/external_input_required/production_gold_count 0 정직·입력 날조 0)·결정적·오프라인 후보 worklist(`build_captured_overlap_fixture`→`discover_overlap`→`build_near_match_reviewer_queue`·합성·LLM 0·network 0)를 순수 builder(`build_label_template`/`build_assignment_manifest`/`build_intake_plan`/`build_pilot_handoff_bundle`)로 동결·`_frozen_pair_list`(allowlist 파생·dedupe·pair_id 정렬·reviewer-facing safe)·`_batch_signature`(deterministic sha256·정렬 pair 정체성+batch config·PII/score/rationale/title 제외)·`_launch_status`(5-state: blocked_no_candidates/ready_for_manual_launch/awaiting_manual_launch/awaiting_returned_labels/labels_present·frozen+게이트 actual-input 축 파생)·`build_operator_launch_checklist`(수동 배포/회수/검증 단계+manual-only contact 지시+PII/secret 금지 reminder+no-go 경고·전송 0·label/contact evidence/roster 생성 0)·R1 gap(`r1_gold_acquisition_plan._r1_status`+`REQUIRED_PRODUCTION_GOLD` 재사용·current_r1_gap)·`candidate_provenance=synthetic_fixture`·`pilot_batch_is_production_candidate=False`·전체 출력 재귀 PII 가드·CLI. `reviewer_batch_launch.py`(`build_intake_plan` +`intake_dir` override·additive·기존 호출 무영향·게이트 스캔 경로 단일 수렴). `schemas/internal_ops.py`(+`InternalOpsR1PilotBatchStatus` 22필드·`InternalOpsFlags` 재사용·response_model 화이트리스트). `api/internal_ops.py`(+`GET /api/internal/ops/r1-pilot-batch`·이중 게이트·read-only·503 sanitize·기존 `/pilot-execution`·`/preflight`·`/r1-gold-acquisition` 무변경). frontend: `lib/api/types.ts`(+`InternalOpsR1PilotBatchStatus`)·`lib/ops/opsPilotExecutionView.ts`(+`toR1BatchDisplayRows`/`r1BatchWarnings`/`OPS_R1_BATCH_COPY`)·`app/internal/ops-pilot/page.tsx`(+launch-readiness 패널·warnings dedupe[중복 No-Go copy React key 충돌 방지])·`lib/ops/__tests__/opsPilotExecutionView.test.mjs`(+6). **ADR#74 커밋분(r1_gold_acquisition_plan) 미변경**.

**검증(결정론 backend 신규 44·frontend 신규 6·실호출 0·DB 0·전송 0·secret 값 미열람)** — 신규 backend **44**(test_r1_reviewer_pilot_batch **36**[actual input re-check 3·pilot batch freeze 8·reviewer-facing safety 3·operator launch package 5·internal ops contract 2·no merge/LLM/DB 2·launch_status state machine 6·_frozen_pair_list 2·**adversarial HIGH-1 synthetic 태깅·MEDIUM-1 dry-run hard-stop·signature NIT 2 fix-lock 4**]+test_internal_ops_api **+8**[/r1-pilot-batch flag 404·sanitized contract·launch readiness·no-go flags·forbidden+PII 0·read-only 405·키집합 화이트리스트·prod fail-closed 503]). frontend node:test **+6**(opsPilotExecutionView r1 pilot batch view: forbidden 가드·launch readiness rows·worklist-not-truth/manual/missing/synthetic warnings·copy·synthetic≠production·re-introduce throw). backend 비-live **1391 passed/101 skipped/0 failed**(1347+44)·ingestion **1353 passed**(불변·ingestion/ 미변경)·frontend **tsc 0·lint 0·test 38**(기존 32+6)·ruff(E/F/I/B/W−E501) **0**·secret scan **PASS**(9664 files)·docs_lifecycle conflicts **0**. **live-PG=미실행**(DB 미기동·도구가 DB/session/ORM 무접촉·`db_write:False`→무영향). **honest 동작 입증**: actual input 부재→`no_actual_input`/`external_input_required`·`r1_status=blocked_no_labels`·frozen 5(합성)·signature deterministic·`launch_status=ready_for_manual_launch`·`pilot_batch_is_production_candidate=False`·production_gold_count 0·current_r1_gap 200·forbidden 키 0.

**감사(§15)** — closeout subagents(architecture/pipeline/actual_input_gate/r1_pilot_batch_freeze/candidate_sufficiency/batch_signature/reviewer_launch_package/operator_handoff/returned_label_placement/label_validation_command/internal_ops_launch_readiness/r1_gold_acquisition/source_storage_strategy/community_reaction_boundary/rag_kg_entity_readiness/internal_ops_auth_boundary/ops_ui_contract/frontend_internal_ops/public_truth_boundary/reviewer_pii/secret_boundary/code/test/evidence/risk_closure/adversarial review). cardinal(R1 plan 실행 둔갑/batch freeze 없이 reviewer 전달 보고/contact evidence 없이 contacted 둔갑/actual labels 없이 production_gold 증가/synthetic·model→production 둔갑/single reviewer→gold/MERGE_GATE 전 merge/RAG·KG 조기 build/same_event truth 노출/score·rationale·predicted_status 노출/community·market anchor/실제 전송) 차단 확인. **adversarial PROCEED-WITH-FIXES**(BLOCK 0·HIGH 1+MEDIUM 1+LOW 3): **HIGH-1** reviewer-facing label template 이 합성 큐인데 `dataset_source=live_derived` 로 자가당착 태깅→회수 라벨이 production gold 로 둔갑 가능→`build_label_template(queue, dataset_source=SOURCE_SYNTHETIC)` 로 고정(회수 라벨 dataset_source=synthetic→intake chain[production=production AND live_derived]이 production gold 미승격·**machinery 강제**·`frozen_label_dataset_source` 노출+test lock)·**MEDIUM-1** launch_status/checklist 가 합성 batch 실 reviewer 배포 유도(hard stop 부재)→"SYNTHETIC FIXTURE — dry-run only·production gold 수집 금지" hard-stop 을 next_action/checklist no_go_warnings **맨 앞**+`dry_run_only` 플래그·**LOW-1/2/3**(signature title 제외=pair 정체성만 의도적·절대경로 override display-mask·same_event 구조가드) 문서화. **code-review LGTM-WITH-NITS**(triple-consistency dict==pydantic==TS **22==22==22**·flags 8==8==8·additive 안전·API 패턴 정합·NIT signature reviewers_per_pair 민감도/order-invariance 테스트 추가).

**RISK(§11)** — 종결 0·**신규 1**(실 present blocker만): **R-BatchFreezeAsTruth**(LOW·동결된 합성 fixture pilot batch 가 production 후보·event truth 로 오인될 위험·완화=candidate_provenance=synthetic_fixture·pilot_batch_is_production_candidate=False·dataset_source=synthetic→production gold 미승격·same_event_truth_exposed=False·worklist-not-truth copy·test lock). **남발 금지**(R-FrozenBatchNoCandidates=후보 존재로 미등록·R-ManualLaunchStall=R-GoldAcquisitionPlanOnly 에 흡수). 부분진전: **R-GoldAcquisitionPlanOnly**(#74→#75: 첫 pilot batch freeze+operator launch package+ready_for_manual_launch·**실 returned labels 0 불변→완전종결 금지**)·**R-ReviewerPilotExecution**(#74→#75: batch freeze→execution ledger 연결+returned label 적재/검증 경로 가시·**실 reviewer contact·실 returned labels 0 불변→완전종결 금지**)·**R-IdentityHumanLabeling**(reviewer-facing worklist frozen+template/placement/validation 연결+production/synthetic 분리·**실 production reviewer label 0→완전종결 금지**)·**R-ReviewerAgreement**(expected files 의 pair 당 reviewer 중복+conflict/adjudication 정책·**실 reviewer 합의 0**)·**R-GoldSamplingBias**(pilot_n↔R1 target gap 가시+분포 정직[합성]·**실 production sampling 0**)·**R-IdentityEvalDataset**(frozen batch→eval/gold intake 가능+R1 target gap 명시·**MERGE_GATE evidence 0**).

**다음 hard blocker(실 데이터로 확정)** — ① **실 production candidate**(live source overlap·credentials·합성 탈피·R-SourceOverlapScarcity) → ② **실 reviewer contact/recruitment** → ③ **actual returned labels**(R1·gate 자동 end-to-end) → ④ gold denominator(live 200·KO 50·pos/neg 67·hard-neg 20·R1) → ⑤ MERGE_GATE calibration(R2) → ⑥ embedding scorer opt-in 실호출(R3) → ⑦ entity/KG/GraphRAG(R4~R6) → ⑧ Agent/public IU(R7). 별도 축: internal ops per-user auth+배포 경계(R-InternalOpsAuthBoundary). R1 first pilot batch freeze+operator launch package+launch readiness **착수**는 이 턴에 닫음(실 reviewer 입력·실 gold·public IU 아님).

**한계** — **이 턴 진전=R1 first reviewer pilot batch freeze+operator launch handoff+internal ops launch readiness·실 reviewer 입력 아님**(production_gold_count 0·gate exact passthrough·frozen batch 가 미증가·**입력 디렉터리 부재→no_actual_input/external_input_required/blocked_no_labels**·실 production reviewer label·실 gold·실 returned labels·실 contact evidence 0·**실제 email/slack/webhook 전송 0**·embedding/LLM 실호출 0·운영 DB·semantic merge·public IU·RAG/KG/Entity runtime 0). **frozen pilot batch 는 합성 captured fixture**(실 source 아님)·`candidate_provenance=synthetic_fixture`·`pilot_batch_is_production_candidate=False`·**frozen 5<<target 200=pilot_n**·라벨 회수해도 dataset_source=synthetic→production gold 미승격(machinery 강제). frozen batch 는 **reviewer worklist 동결이지 event truth 가 아니다**(same_event 미함의). internal ops launch readiness 는 internal workflow state 이지 public truth 가 아니다(admin-token+flag+nav 미노출+server-env 4중 게이트).

**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/r1_reviewer_pilot_batch.py`·`backend/tests/test_r1_reviewer_pilot_batch.py`·`backend/app/tools/reviewer_batch_launch.py`·`backend/app/schemas/internal_ops.py`·`backend/app/api/internal_ops.py`·`backend/tests/test_internal_ops_api.py`·`frontend/src/lib/api/types.ts`·`frontend/src/lib/ops/opsPilotExecutionView.ts`·`frontend/src/app/internal/ops-pilot/page.tsx`·`frontend/src/lib/ops/__tests__/opsPilotExecutionView.test.mjs`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS.md`·`docs/2_ROADMAP/{00_ROADMAP_INDEX,15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP,19_WEB_INTELLIGENCE_IMPLEMENTATION_SPEC}.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT.md`·`docs/_CANONICAL/02_CURRENT_ARCHITECTURE.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#72/#73/#74.

## ADR#76 — R1 live production candidate acquisition gate + production-candidate batch readiness + internal ops dual-track

**선행** — ADR#75(R1 first reviewer pilot batch freeze + operator launch handoff + internal ops launch readiness)를 안정 기준점으로 커밋(`d253031`·19파일·제공 메시지 그대로·secret PASS·docs_lifecycle conflicts 0·closeout SIGNATURE_MATCH·push 0·NO UPSTREAM). 이 커밋을 ADR#76 의 기준점으로 삼음.

**문제(§2)** — ADR#75 frozen pilot batch 는 **합성** captured fixture(dry-run artifact)다. R1 production gold 의 실제 시작점은 합성 batch 가 아니라 **live-derived production candidate** 다. "합성 batch 가 있으니 R1 라벨링이 시작됐다"로 착각할 자리가 남는다(R-SyntheticProductionContamination/R-ProductionCandidateScarcity). 필요한 것은 actual returned labels 이전에 **실 production candidate**(live source overlap·publishable×publishable)와, synthetic dry-run batch 와 live production-candidate batch 를 **분리** 표시하는 internal ops dual-track 이다.

**원자 분석(§2·20문항·구현 전 보고)** — ① live source path=`cross_source_live_overlap_smoke.run_cross_source_live_overlap_smoke(live_query=True)`(Guardian×NYT adapter·`run_provider_query`+`discover_overlap`·cross-source near-match queue) ② Guardian/NYT smoke 재사용 가능(`ADAPTER_WIRED_PROVIDERS={guardian,nyt}`) ③ credential presence secret-safe(`probe_env_var`/`env_status`/`build_provider_readiness_report`·present/missing bool·값 0·network 0) ④ live opt-in 명확(`live_query=False` 기본·실 HTTP 는 transport=None+양 credential present 일 때만·CLI `--live-query`·상시 allow-live env 없음) ⑤ live call 없이 production candidate **불가**(오프라인=합성 fixture 뿐) ⑥ synthetic/live-derived 구조 분리(`SOURCE_SYNTHETIC=synthetic_fixture` vs `SOURCE_LIVE=live_derived`·smoke 는 실 records 일 때만 live_derived) ⑦ candidate_provenance allowed={live_derived,synthetic_fixture,none}·production 후보=live_derived 강제 ⑧ production_candidate_batch=True 조건=live_derived AND live_call_performed AND publishable×publishable frozen ≥1 ⑨ publishable 강제(`_is_publishable_production_pair`·official/article/news·`discover_overlap` 도 이미 publishable 필터) ⑩ community/market/catalog/search anchor 거부(registry 분류+가드) ⑪ live pair same_event truth 혼입 0(label=unlabeled·labeler_prediction_hidden·`_assert_pii_safe`) ⑫ scorer score/rationale/predicted 누출 0(`labeler_visible=False`·reviewer template allowlist·worklist 는 semantic_scoring=False) ⑬ live pair 0→6-state blocked 분해(no_credentials/no_live_opt_in/no_live_overlap/no_publishable_pairs) ⑭ live pair 적으면 production pilot_n(`production_frozen_pair_count<<200`·R1 collecting) ⑮ production batch↔synthetic batch internal ops UI 분리(dual-track) ⑯ production batch 도 production_gold_count 미증가(gate passthrough) ⑰ actual returned labels 우선(gate re-check 먼저·returned/imported→Lane A 우선) ⑱ R-SourceOverlapScarcity 부분진전(acquisition attempted-or-blocked 형식화+readiness+live_candidate_count 측정·완전종결 금지) ⑲ R-BatchFreezeAsTruth 추가 완화(synthetic non-production+production batch 분리+UI synthetic_not_production+same_event 은닉·완전종결 금지) ⑳ 다음 hard blocker=live candidate acquisition(opt-in+credential)→reviewer contact→returned labels. **핵심 정직성 결정: 합성→production 둔갑 0·실 live 후보 없으면 blocked 정직 산출**(이번 턴 live_query=False→`blocked_no_live_opt_in`·credential present 발견[Guardian/NYT secret-safe]→남은 차단은 명시적 opt-in 하나).

**옵션 결정(§3)** — (A) actual returned labels re-check (B) live production candidate acquisition (C) production-candidate batch freeze[조건부] (D) internal ops dual-track visibility (E) embedding/LLM scorer runtime (F) production DB·semantic merge·public IU·GraphRAG. **선택: A+B+C(조건부)+D 채택·E/F 금지.** ADR#76 기록. **live call 실행 여부: 이번 턴 실 네트워크 호출 미실행**(`live_query=False` 기본·자율 턴 per-turn 외부호출 opt-in 없음·결정론·코드베이스가 live call 을 non-CI opt-in 으로 취급)→머신러리 완전 구축+테스트·산출은 `blocked_no_live_opt_in` 정직.

**구현(신규 코드 1[+test 1]·기존 보강·재구현 0·`run_actual_input_gate`+`run_cross_source_live_overlap_smoke`+`build_provider_readiness_report` 재사용·단방향 import·DB 0·전송 0·secret 값 미열람)** — 신규 `r1_production_candidate_acquisition.py`(acquisition gate + 조건부 freeze orchestrator): Lane A `run_actual_input_gate` re-check(returned/imported→`returned_labels_take_precedence`)·Lane B credential presence(`build_provider_readiness_report`·secret-safe·network 0)+live 후보 획득(`run_cross_source_live_overlap_smoke`·`live_query` opt-in·기본 시도 0)·6-state `_production_candidate_status`(blocked_no_credentials/blocked_no_live_opt_in/blocked_no_live_overlap/blocked_no_publishable_pairs/live_candidates_found/production_batch_frozen)·source role guard `_is_publishable_production_pair`(official/article/news·community/market/catalog/search/unknown anchor 거부·fail-closed)·조건부 freeze(live publishable 만·`build_label_template(dataset_source=SOURCE_LIVE)`·ADR#75 `_frozen_pair_list`/`_batch_signature`/`build_operator_launch_checklist` 재사용)·Lane C synthetic dry-run track(`run_r1_reviewer_pilot_batch` 1회·분리 인용)·R1 gap(`_r1_status`+`REQUIRED_PRODUCTION_GOLD`)·dual-track sanitized contract·전체 출력 재귀 PII 가드·CLI(`--live-query` opt-in). `cross_source_live_overlap_smoke.py`(+additive `reviewer_queue` 키·**packet_items[LabelingPacketItem] 제외 JSON-safe 투영**·production freeze 소비용·기존 계약 무변). `schemas/internal_ops.py`(+`InternalOpsR1ProductionCandidateStatus` 23필드·`InternalOpsFlags` 재사용·response_model 화이트리스트). `api/internal_ops.py`(+`GET /api/internal/ops/r1-production-candidates`·이중 게이트·read-only·`live_query=False` 고정[read API 시도 0]·503 sanitize·기존 4 endpoint 무변경). frontend: `lib/api/types.ts`(+`InternalOpsR1ProductionCandidateStatus`)·`lib/ops/opsPilotExecutionView.ts`(+`toR1ProdCandidateDisplayRows`/`r1ProdCandidateWarnings`/`OPS_R1_PROD_COPY`)·`app/internal/ops-pilot/page.tsx`(+dual-track 패널·warnings 병합 dedupe)·`lib/ops/__tests__/opsPilotExecutionView.test.mjs`(+6). **ADR#75 커밋분(r1_reviewer_pilot_batch) 미변경**.

**검증(결정론 backend 신규 43·frontend 신규 6·실호출 0·DB 0·전송 0·secret 값 미열람)** — 신규 backend **43**(test_r1_production_candidate_acquisition **34**[actual input re-check 5·live acquisition 6-state 8·source role guard 6·reviewer-facing safety 3·dual-track contract 4·no merge/LLM/DB 2·signature/synthetic 통합 3]+test_internal_ops_api **+8**[/r1-production-candidates flag 404·sanitized contract·dual-track 분리·no-go flags·forbidden+PII 0·read-only 405·키집합 23 화이트리스트·prod fail-closed 503]+test_cross_source_live_overlap_smoke **+1**[additive reviewer_queue 노출 회귀]). frontend node:test **+6**(opsPilotExecutionView r1 production candidate dual-track: forbidden 가드·synthetic↔production 분리 rows·synthetic-not-production/worklist-not-truth/live-pairs-required/No-Go warnings·copy·live pair 없으면 미동결·re-introduce throw). backend 비-live **1434 passed/101 skipped/0 failed**(1391+43)·ingestion **1353 passed**(불변·ingestion/ 미변경)·frontend **tsc 0·lint 0·test 44**(38+6)·ruff(E/F/I/B/W−E501) **0**·secret scan **PASS**·docs_lifecycle conflicts **0**. **live-PG=미실행**(live_query=False 기본·DB 미기동·도구가 DB/session/ORM 무접촉·`db_write:False`→무영향). **honest 동작 입증**: actual input 부재→`no_actual_input`/`external_input_required`·`r1_status=blocked_no_labels`·credential present(Guardian/NYT secret-safe)→`production_candidate_status=blocked_no_live_opt_in`·`live_call_performed=False`·`production_candidate_batch_ready=False`·`candidate_provenance=none`·synthetic dry-run 분리(`synthetic_dry_run_batch_ready=True`/`synthetic_batch_not_production=True`)·production_gold_count 0·current_r1_gap 200·forbidden 키 0.

**감사(§15)** — closeout subagents(architecture/pipeline/actual_input_gate/live_production_candidate_acquisition/provider_readiness/credential_secret_boundary/source_overlap/production_candidate_batch/synthetic_vs_production_separation/source_role_guard/r1_pilot_batch_freeze/candidate_sufficiency/batch_signature/reviewer_launch_package/operator_handoff/internal_ops_dual_track/r1_gold_acquisition/gold_floor_gap/community_reaction_boundary/rag_kg_entity_readiness/internal_ops_auth_boundary/ops_ui_contract/frontend_internal_ops/public_truth_boundary/reviewer_pii/secret_boundary/source_loop/code/test/evidence/risk_closure/adversarial review). cardinal(합성→production candidate 둔갑/live evidence 없이 production_candidate_batch=True/production candidate 없이 reviewer production labeling 요청/actual returned labels 없이 production_gold 증가/community·market·catalog anchor/score·rationale·predicted_status 노출/same_event truth 노출/internal ops public route 노출/실 전송/`.env` 값 읽기) 차단 확인.

**RISK(§11)** — 종결 0·**신규 2**(실 present blocker만): **R-ProductionCandidateScarcity**(MEDIUM·live-derived publishable candidate pair 0·R1 의 실제 시작점 부재·완화=acquisition gate+6-state blocked+readiness 측정·완전종결=충분한 live 후보 확보 시)·**R-SyntheticProductionContamination**(LOW·synthetic/dry-run artifact 가 production path 진입 위험·완화=candidate_provenance=live_derived 강제·`build_label_template(dataset_source=SOURCE_LIVE)` 분리·dual-track UI·test lock). **남발 금지**(R-LiveProviderDependency=R-Gdelt429/R-SourceOverlapScarcity 에 흡수·미등록). 부분진전: **R-SourceOverlapScarcity**(live acquisition attempted-or-blocked 형식화+provider readiness+live_candidate_count 측정[0]·**충분한 live 후보 0→완전종결 금지**)·**R-RealSourceLoopUnproven**(production-candidate path 가 live-derived 사용·synthetic≠production·**actual live→reviewer→label loop 미완→완전종결 금지**)·**R-BatchFreezeAsTruth**(synthetic non-production+production batch 분리+UI synthetic_not_production+same_event 은닉·**scaled production batch·배포 UI 분리 미증명→완전종결 금지**)·**R-GoldAcquisitionPlanOnly**(production-candidate freeze 경로 가능[live 후보 시]+blocked 정직·**actual returned labels·reviewer contact 0 불변→완전종결 금지**)·**R-IdentityHumanLabeling**(production candidate worklist→label template+production/synthetic/model 분리·**실 human label 0→완전종결 금지**).

**다음 hard blocker(실 데이터로 확정)** — ① **실 live production candidate 확보**(opt-in `--live-query`+Guardian/NYT credential[present 확인됨]→cross-source publishable overlap·R-ProductionCandidateScarcity) → ② **실 reviewer contact/recruitment** → ③ **actual returned labels**(R1) → ④ gold denominator(live 200·KO 50·pos/neg 67·hard-neg 20·R1) → ⑤ MERGE_GATE calibration(R2) → ⑥ embedding scorer opt-in 실호출(R3) → ⑦ entity/KG/GraphRAG(R4~R6) → ⑧ Agent/public IU(R7). live production candidate acquisition gate+dual-track readiness **착수**는 이 턴에 닫음(실 live 호출·실 후보·실 gold·public IU 아님).

**한계** — **이 턴 진전=R1 live production candidate acquisition gate+production-candidate batch readiness+internal ops dual-track·실 live 호출 아님**(production_gold_count 0·gate exact passthrough·**live_query=False 기본→실 네트워크 시도 0**·credential present 확인은 secret-safe presence만[값 0]·`production_candidate_status=blocked_no_live_opt_in`·실 production candidate·실 reviewer contact·실 returned labels·실 gold 0·**실제 email/slack/webhook 전송 0**·embedding/LLM 실호출 0·운영 DB·semantic merge·public IU·RAG/KG/Entity runtime 0). **production-candidate batch 는 live-derived publishable×publishable 만**(합성 절대 불가·`candidate_provenance=live_derived` AND live_call_performed AND publishable ≥1)·이번 턴 live 후보 0→미동결. production candidate 도 **reviewer worklist 동결이지 event truth 가 아니다**(same_event 미함의·production_gold_count 미증가). synthetic dry-run batch 와 production-candidate batch 는 internal ops UI/API 에서 **분리**(합성→production 둔갑 0). internal ops dual-track 은 internal workflow state 이지 public truth 가 아니다(admin-token+flag+nav 미노출+server-env 4중 게이트·read API live_query=False 고정).

**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/r1_production_candidate_acquisition.py`·`backend/tests/test_r1_production_candidate_acquisition.py`·`backend/app/tools/cross_source_live_overlap_smoke.py`·`backend/app/schemas/internal_ops.py`·`backend/app/api/internal_ops.py`·`backend/tests/test_internal_ops_api.py`·`backend/tests/test_cross_source_live_overlap_smoke.py`·`frontend/src/lib/api/types.ts`·`frontend/src/lib/ops/opsPilotExecutionView.ts`·`frontend/src/app/internal/ops-pilot/page.tsx`·`frontend/src/lib/ops/__tests__/opsPilotExecutionView.test.mjs`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS.md`·`docs/2_ROADMAP/{00_ROADMAP_INDEX,15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP,19_WEB_INTELLIGENCE_IMPLEMENTATION_SPEC}.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT.md`·`docs/_CANONICAL/02_CURRENT_ARCHITECTURE.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#73/#74/#75.

## ADR#77 — R1 live query executed + cross-source near-match gap[원인 미확정] + blocked-reason honesty fix + product bridge gating

**선행** — ADR#76(R1 live production candidate acquisition gate + production-candidate batch readiness + internal ops dual-track)를 안정 기준점으로 커밋(`00c70a9`·20파일·제공 메시지 그대로·secret PASS·docs_lifecycle conflicts 0·closeout SIGNATURE_MATCH 25==25·push 0·NO UPSTREAM). 이 커밋을 ADR#77 의 기준점으로 삼음.

**문제(§2)** — ADR#76 은 opt-in live acquisition gate 를 만들었으나 `blocked_no_live_opt_in` 에 머물렀다. 실제로 실행해 (a) live→discover 루프가 실데이터로 닫히는지, (b) 다음 hard blocker 가 무엇인지 확정해야 한다. user 가 이번 턴 live query 실행을 **명시 승인**(범위=근거기반 최소증분).

**원자 분석(§2·20문항·구현 전 보고·요지)** — ① `--live-query` 안전 실행 가능(opt-in+양 cred present+transport=None 일 때만 실 HTTP) ② 외부 호출=Guardian Content API+NYT Article Search 각 1회·단일 topic·1d ③ credential presence secret-safe(`build_provider_readiness_report`·`probe_env_var`·값 0·network 0·이름 GUARDIAN_API_KEY/NYT_API_KEY) ④ governance: `run_provider_query` 가 host_gate=None 이어도 rate cooldown(429 영속·no tight retry) 강제·host 당 1회→min-spacing 위반 구조적 불가 ⑤ overlap 0→blocked_no_live_overlap ⑥-⑨ freeze=live_derived AND publishable≥1·raw body 미저장·packet_rows 만 ⑩ UI: read API live_query=False 고정→UI 는 마지막 비-live 상태(Q10 gap 정직 표기) ⑪-⑬ 실패 strategy=topic/window/provider/GDELT429/RSS/search/Korean ⑭-⑰ LLM/RAG/KG/IU 계약은 docs only·runtime No-Go ⑱-⑳ R-ProductionCandidateScarcity/R-RagKgPrematureBuild 부분진전·다음 blocker=live candidates→reviewer contact→returned labels. **docs/3_SOURCE_STATUS* ABSENT(기록)·Lane D 계약 docs 기존 존재(§6b-R/§6b-S/§4·신규 파일 불요).**

**옵션 결정(§3)** — (A) actual returned labels re-check (B) opt-in live query execution (C) acquisition strategy refinement (D) LLM/RAG/Web product bridge gating (E) embedding/LLM scorer runtime (F) production DB·merge·public IU·GraphRAG. **선택: A+B(user opt-in 승인)+C+D 채택·E/F 금지·범위=근거기반 최소증분(user 결정).** ADR#77 기록.

**live query 실행(§5·user opt-in·bounded·secret-safe·raw body 0)** — `r1_production_candidate_acquisition --live-query` 1회. **결과(실측)**: `live_call_performed=True`·providers_ready=[guardian,nyt]·**`live_candidate_count=100`**(cross-source same-date publishable pair)·**`publishable_pair_count=0`**·`production_candidate_status=blocked_no_publishable_pairs`·root cause **`no_title_overlap`**(near 0·fingerprint 0). live→discover **경로 실데이터 1회 실행**(usable 산출 0)·100=cross-source publishable **비교쌍**(≈10×10 Cartesian·≠same-event match)·**detectable same-event overlap 여전히 0**(scarcity 재확인)·그 0 의 **원인 미확정**[(i) paraphrase recall 한계 OR (ii) broad-topic different-events·단일 broad-topic 1회로 구분 불가·ADR#64 가 "100 쌍=비교대상·n=2 로도 구분 불가" 명시]·frontier=deterministic near-match 0(원인 미확정)→(i)면 INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT §4 ④ adjudicator[R3·gated]·(ii)면 targeted same-event acquisition.

**구현(코드 1 fix[+test 3]·docs 확장·신규 파일 0·재구현 0)** — `r1_production_candidate_acquisition.py`: `_primary_next_action`+`_PCAND_NO_TITLE_OVERLAP_ACTION`(`blocked_no_publishable_pairs` 의 primary next_action 을 `live_candidate_count>0`+`no_title_overlap` 시 **원인 양가(paraphrase OR different-events·미확정)** vs role 거부로 분기·운영자 "source role guard 약화" 오안내 교정하되 단정적 paraphrase 로도 승격 안 함·`next_manual_action` UI 표면 정직). docs 확장(신규 파일 0·기존 docs 우선): `RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS.md`(§6b-R 헤더+§6b-R1c stale 마커 갱신+§6b-R1d live run+near-match gap[원인 미확정]+acquisition strategy+Lane D grounding)·`INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT.md §4`(ADR#77 bullet·④ adjudicator 조건부[(i)] 필요성). **Lane D 계약(LLM evidence packet/RAG ingestion gate/KG edge eligibility/community reaction/public IU)은 §6b-R matrix+§6b-S table+§4 에 이미 존재→grounding 만 추가(신규 sprawling 파일 금지·최소증분).**

**검증(결정론 backend 신규 3·실호출: live query 1회만·DB 0·전송 0·secret 값 미열람)** — 신규 backend **3**(test_r1_production_candidate_acquisition: no_title_overlap→**indeterminate(양가)** action·role 거부→role-guard action·`_primary_next_action` 분기 직접). 관련 3파일 **110 passed**(r1 **37**[34+3]+internal_ops_api+smoke)·ruff(E/F/I/B/W−E501) **0**·secret scan **PASS**·docs_lifecycle conflicts **0**·**backend 비-live 전체 1437 passed/101 skipped/0 failed**(1434+3)·frontend tsc **0**(미변경). ingestion=미변경(backend 후 재확인). **live query=1회 실행**(bounded·rate cooldown 강제·raw body 0).

**감사(§17)** — closeout subagents(architecture/pipeline/actual_input_gate/**live_query_execution**/provider_readiness/credential_secret_boundary/source_overlap/production_candidate_batch/synthetic_vs_production_separation/source_role_guard/**acquisition_strategy**/llm_evidence_packet/rag_ingestion_gate/kg_edge_eligibility/community_reaction_boundary/public_iu_gate/internal_ops_dual_track/r1_gold_acquisition/internal_ops_auth_boundary/ops_ui_contract/frontend_internal_ops/public_truth_boundary/reviewer_pii/secret_boundary/source_loop/code/test/evidence/risk_closure/adversarial review). cardinal(live evidence 없이 production_candidate_batch=True/community·market·catalog anchor/source role guard 약화/score·rationale·predicted_status·same_event 노출/실 전송/`.env` 값 읽기/uncalibrated merge) 차단 확인.

**RISK(§13)** — 종결 0·**신규 2**(실 present blocker): **R-CrossSourceNearMatchGap**(MEDIUM·100 publishable 비교쌍/near-match 0·**원인 미확정**[paraphrase recall OR broad-topic different-events]·해소=먼저 좁은 topic/window 재실행으로 (i)/(ii) 구분 후 lever·완전종결=near-match 후보 확보 시)·**R-ProviderPairNarrowness**(LOW·watch·Guardian×NYT 단일 pair·provider 확장이 near-match 올리는지 미증명). 부분진전: **R-ProductionCandidateScarcity**(live query 실행·100/0 실측·정확 사유·**충분한 후보 0→종결 금지**)·**R-SourceOverlapScarcity**(100=비교쌍·**detectable same-event overlap 0 재확인**→희소 미해소[closure ≥1 미충족]·near-match 가 frontier·종결 금지)·**R-RealSourceLoopUnproven**(live→discover **경로 실데이터 1회 실행**[usable 0]·reviewer→label loop 미완→종결 금지)·**R-RagKgPrematureBuild**(Lane D 계약 grounding·runtime No-Go 유지·종결 금지).

**다음 hard blocker(실 데이터로 확정)** — ① **near-match 0 의 원인 (i)/(ii) 구분**(좁은 same-event-targeted topic/window 재실행·bounded·일부 쌍이 hard band 진입하는지)→그에 따른 lever(gated R3 semantic adjudicator[if i·MERGE_GATE/gold 전 No-Go] 또는 targeted acquisition[if ii]·R-CrossSourceNearMatchGap) → ② 실 reviewer contact → ③ actual returned labels(R1) → ④~⑧ gold/MERGE_GATE/embedding/KG/IU(R2~R7). live query 1회 실행+frontier 정밀화는 이 턴에 닫음(원인 확정·실 후보 freeze·실 gold·public IU 아님).

**한계** — 이 턴 진전=live query 1회 실행+cross-source near-match gap 실측(**원인 미확정**)+blocked-reason 정직성 fix+Lane D grounding·**실 production candidate freeze 아님**(live_candidate_count 100=비교쌍·publishable near-match 0·candidate_provenance=none·production_gold_count 0·detectable same-event overlap 0). adjudicator runtime(embedding/LLM/KG/GraphRAG)·public IU·merge·운영 DB write 0·실 전송 0. internal ops UI read API live_query=False 고정→UI 는 마지막 비-live 상태(Q10 gap·정직 표기·다음 증분). host_gate=None 으로 실행(host 당 1회→min-spacing 위반 불가·반복/sweep 시 host gate 주입은 다음 증분).

**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/r1_production_candidate_acquisition.py`·`backend/tests/test_r1_production_candidate_acquisition.py`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS.md`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT.md`·`docs/2_ROADMAP/{00_ROADMAP_INDEX,15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP,19_WEB_INTELLIGENCE_IMPLEMENTATION_SPEC}.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/_CANONICAL/02_CURRENT_ARCHITECTURE.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#74/#75/#76.

## ADR#78 — targeted live acquisition + near-match gap diagnostic (원인 양가·미확정) + LLM/RAG/KG product bridge contracts

**선행** — ADR#77(R1 live query executed + cross-source near-match gap[원인 미확정] + blocked-reason honesty fix)를 안정 기준점으로 커밋(`6ee7c31`·11파일·제공 메시지 그대로·secret PASS·docs_lifecycle conflicts 0·closeout SIGNATURE_MATCH 16==16·push 0·NO UPSTREAM). 이 커밋을 ADR#78 의 기준점으로 삼음.

**문제(§2)** — ADR#77 은 broad topic 1회로 near-match 0(원인 미확정)을 실측했으나 100쌍 제목 미보존이라 원인을 가를 수 없었다. 원자 분석(20문항·실 코드 read): near-match 0 의 단일 실패 feature 는 **title-token Jaccard**(date/role/canonical PASS)·detector 는 의도적 고정밀·저재현(`_title_tokens`=소문자+21 stopword+len>1·**stemming/entity 정규화 없음**)·near 는 **reviewer 라우팅** gate 이지 merge gate 아님(merge=fingerprint+gold+MERGE_GATE)→near recall 개선은 false-merge 위험 0. 진단의 실데이터 grounding 엔 bounded live 재실행 필요. provider landscape: Guardian/NYT 외 wired query-capable publishable=GDELT(429 제약)·SEC EDGAR·Federal Register; key-free 다출처 RSS fleet(BBC/AP/AlJazeera/Verge/TechCrunch + KO Yonhap/hankyung/maekyung/ZDNet KO/ETNews·feed-only); Naver/NewsAPI/GNews/Serper/Tavily/Exa=cataloged·NOT wired(search=URL-candidate-only).

**옵션 결정(§3)** — (A) actual returned labels re-check (B) near-match gap root-cause diagnostic (C) targeted same-event live acquisition (D) acquisition strategy + provider expansion + Korean lane (E) LLM/RAG/KG contract hardening (F) embedding/LLM scorer runtime (G) production DB·merge·public IU·GraphRAG runtime. **선택: A+B+C(user opt-in 승인·bounded)+D+E(contract) 채택·F/G 금지·범위=근거기반 코어(user 결정).** ADR#78 기록.

**구현(§4·근거기반 코어·최소 신규 파일)** — ① smoke `emit_band_diagnostic`(additive·band 분포·max Jaccard·최고중첩 below-floor 샘플=**공유 정규화 토큰만**·raw body 0). ② 신규 `r1_targeted_live_acquisition.py`(Lane B 진단 분류기 `classify_near_match_gap`[원인 양가 보존·단정 0] + Lane C orchestrator[seed 검증·ADR#76 production gate 재사용으로 6-state·freeze·R1 gap·contract] + Lane D `build_provider_expansion_plan`/`build_korean_source_strategy` + Lane E `_contract_readiness`). ③ 신규 contract 2: `LLM_EVIDENCE_PACKET_CONTRACT.md`(LLM 가 볼/추론/인용/단정 못하는 것·MERGE_GATE dependency·runtime No-Go)·`RAG_KG_ENTITY_GATE_CONTRACT.md`(RAG ingestion gate·KG edge eligibility[same_event=MERGE_GATE·community=reaction_to only]·public IU gate). ④ internal ops 최소 배선: `InternalOpsAcquisitionFrontierStatus` schema + `GET /api/internal/ops/r1-acquisition-frontier`(read API live 0) + TS types + view(`toR1FrontierDisplayRows`/`r1FrontierWarnings`·필수 §11 copy) + 테스트. 화면 page.tsx render 는 **후순위**(근거기반 코어·Q10 gap 정직 표기).

**라이브 실측(§6·user opt-in·bounded·governed)** — `--live-query` 1회 실행(host_gate 주입·no-bypass): **fed_rate**("Federal Reserve interest rate decision"·7d)=guardian ok 10/nyt ok 10·**cross-source 비교쌍 30**·band 전부 below_floor·**max title Jaccard 0.0526**·최고중첩 쌍조차 공유 토큰이 generic filler("it"/"over"/"day")·event entity 아님. **scotus_ruling·ukraine_war=host_gate_blocked**(반복 host min-spacing·정직 governance). live_call_count 2. 진단: `all_below_hard_floor`·confidence **indeterminate**·가설 same_event_missed/different_events/title_normalization/provider_narrow 전부 plausible(어느 쪽도 단정 0)·unknown supporting. production: `blocked_no_publishable_pairs`·freeze 0·candidate_provenance none·**production_gold_count 0·r1_gap 200**. 안전: merge/llm/embedding/db/전송 0·public IU 0·same_event_truth_exposed 0·raw body 0·secret 0(provider plan 의 'api_key' 문자열은 env var **이름**·값 아님).

**정직한 해석(§5·단정 금지)** — 단일 기관(Fed)·7d 로 좁혀도 hard band 진입 0·최고 쌍이 entity 아닌 generic 토큰만 공유 → 이 seed 에선 (ii)"기관 우산 아래 다양한 기사"로 **약하게** 기울지만 **단정 불가**(n=1 유효 seed·2개 host-gate 차단·7d 기관쿼리 한계). (i)recall/normalization 도 생존(stemming/entity 정규화 부재). 가장 깨끗한 미실행 실험=단일 **discrete breaking event·1d·당일 동시보도** — host floor 때문에 seed 는 턴/시간에 분산 필요(multi-turn/scheduled).

**검증** — backend 비-live 전체 GREEN·신규 backend 테스트 27(targeted acquisition)+smoke 2(band)+frontend ops view 7·frontend tsc 0·ruff(E/F/I/B/W−E501) 0·secret scan PASS·docs_lifecycle conflicts 0. (수치는 PROJECT_STATUS 최종 보고와 동기.)

**RISK(§14)** — 부분진전: R-CrossSourceNearMatchGap(원인 진단·양가 보존·targeted 1 seed 실측·종결 금지[원인 미분리]), R-ProviderPairNarrowness(Guardian×NYT 한계 평가+expansion plan·종결 금지[대안 미테스트]), R-ProductionCandidateScarcity(targeted 시도·live_candidate 측정·종결 금지[충분 후보 미확보]), R-RagKgPrematureBuild(contract 보강·runtime No-Go·종결 금지). 신규: R-KoreanR1SourceGap(KO live-query source 미배선·RSS feed-only)·R-DeterministicNearMatchRecall(detector 고정밀·저재현이 same-event 누락 가능)·R-LiveAcquisitionRateBudget(반복 live 가 host/rate 제약·seed 분산 필요). 종결 0.

**다음 hard blocker** — ① **단일 discrete breaking event·1d·band 캡처**로 (i)/(ii) 추가 분리(반복 seed 는 host floor 때문에 turn/scheduled 분산) → ② 안 되면 normalization recall(KO/EN-aware 경량 stemming/alias·deterministic semantic_candidate_scorer top-k) + provider breadth(key-free RSS fleet·Naver adapter wiring[KO floor]) → ③ 실 reviewer contact → ④ actual returned labels(R1) → ⑤~ gold/MERGE_GATE/embedding/KG/IU(R2~R7). credential/opt-in 은 blocker 아님.

**한계** — 이 턴 진전=targeted live 1 seed 실측+near-match gap 진단(원인 **양가·미확정**)+Lane D/E contract. **실 production candidate freeze 아님**(publishable near-match 0)·실 reviewer contact 0·actual returned labels 0·production_gold_count 0·detectable same-event overlap 0. adjudicator runtime(embedding/LLM/KG/GraphRAG)·public IU·merge·운영 DB write·실 전송 0. internal ops read API live 0→UI 는 insufficient_debug_artifact(정직). page.tsx render 후순위(Q10 gap).

**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/r1_targeted_live_acquisition.py`·`backend/app/tools/cross_source_live_overlap_smoke.py`·`backend/tests/test_r1_targeted_live_acquisition.py`·`backend/app/schemas/internal_ops.py`·`backend/app/api/internal_ops.py`·`frontend/src/lib/{api/types.ts,ops/opsPilotExecutionView.ts}`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/{LLM_EVIDENCE_PACKET_CONTRACT,RAG_KG_ENTITY_GATE_CONTRACT,RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS,INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT}.md`·`docs/2_ROADMAP/{00_ROADMAP_INDEX,15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP,19_WEB_INTELLIGENCE_IMPLEMENTATION_SPEC}.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/_CANONICAL/02_CURRENT_ARCHITECTURE.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#75/#76/#77.

## ADR#79 — discrete-event acquisition + deterministic recall probe (reviewer-routing recall·merge 분리) + provider breadth

**선행** — ADR#78(targeted live acquisition + near-match gap diagnostic[원인 양가·미확정] + LLM/RAG/KG product bridge contracts)를 안정 기준점으로 커밋(`03829e4`·20파일·제공 메시지 그대로·secret PASS·docs_lifecycle conflicts 0·closeout SIGNATURE_MATCH 25==25·push 0·NO UPSTREAM). 이 커밋을 ADR#79 의 기준점으로 삼음.

**문제(§2)** — ADR#77/#78 이 실측한 near-match 0(all below hard floor)의 원인 (i)detector miss(같은 사건·recall 한계) vs (ii)broad-topic different-events 가 단일 broad/7d run 으로 미분리. 원자 분석(20문항·실 코드 5개 정독): detector `_title_tokens`=소문자+21 stopword+len>1·**stemming/entity alias/number 정규화 전부 없음**(정규식 `[0-9A-Za-z가-힣]+`는 한글 토큰은 잡으나 형태소 분해·KO stopword 없음)→같은 사건 paraphrase 가 표면 변형만으로 floor(0.2) 아래로 떨어질 수 있음. **near=reviewer 라우팅 gate≠merge gate**(merge=`cluster_records`/`semantic_identity_fingerprint`=exact token-set+date+gold+MERGE_GATE)→recall 완화는 false-merge 위험 0. ADR#78 `_acquisition_strategy_next` 가 이미 recall probe 를 다음 레버로 지목("stemming+entity alias+scorer top-k·no LLM"). 기존 `fake_semantic` scorer 는 char-bigram 블랙박스("not validated recall")인 반면 **recall probe 차별점=feature-attributed 정규화**(어느 alias/stem 이 매치를 만들었나 보고)→(i)/(ii) 판별 레버. provider: Guardian/NYT 외 wired query-capable=GDELT(429·cooldown-honored 회복)·SEC EDGAR·Federal Register; RSS fleet=feed-only(현재 breaking breadth); `naver_news_search`=registry 등재(type news·api_key_required)이나 **fetcher 미배선**(KO floor 최고 레버).

**옵션 결정(§3)** — **선택: A(actual input 재확인)+B(discrete-event live·승인 시 bounded — user opt 'synthetic only'→live 미실행)+C(deterministic recall probe·핵심·필수)+D(provider/KO plan)+E(frontier 영속·제한적)+F(contract guard) 채택·G/H(embedding/LLM/merge/public IU/DB runtime) 금지.** per-turn live 승인 질의→**user 'synthetic만, live 생략'** 선택(approval 미이월·정직). ADR#79 기록.

**구현(§4·최소 신규 파일)** — ① 신규 `near_match_recall_probe.py`(핵심): feature-attributed 결정론 정규화(case fold·org **phrase** alias[federal reserve→federalreserve·다토큰 인접 매칭]·acronym alias[fed→federalreserve·모호 단어 who/us/un/eu 제외]·light stemming[rates→rate·operations→operation·shipping→ship]·number normalize·routing stopword). **merge 경로 미호출**(`cluster_records`/`semantic_identity_fingerprint` import/참조 0·AST 테스트로 잠금)·`recall_probe_applies_to_merge=False`·`merge_allowed=False`·score internal-only·body-free 요약. ② 신규 `r1_discrete_event_acquisition.py`(op `r1_discrete_event_acquisition_and_recall_probe`): discrete seed 엄격 검증(`validate_discrete_event_seed`·단일 이산사건·tight window 1d/2d·event phrase 요구·broad umbrella[federal reserve/ukraine war 등] 거부)+ADR#78 gate/diagnostic/provider/Korean 재사용+recall probe 통합(synthetic)+`refine_root_cause_with_recall_probe`((i)/(ii) 구조 진전·단정 0)+§4 output. ③ internal ops 배선: `InternalOpsDiscreteAcquisitionFrontier` schema(22 field)+`GET /api/internal/ops/r1-discrete-acquisition`(read API live 0·flag off 404·503 no path leak)+TS interface+view(`toR1DiscreteFrontierDisplayRows`/`r1DiscreteFrontierWarnings`·§9 copy)+테스트. **dict==pydantic==TS 22==22==22**.

**recall probe 실측(synthetic known-paraphrase fixture·network 0·결정론)** — `fed_acronym`("Fed raises rates again"↔"Federal Reserve lifts interest rates"): baseline Jaccard **0.125**(merge-path 놓침)→probe **0.333**(routing 올림)·lift +0.208·공유 `[federalreserve,rate]`·**entity 공유** federalreserve·features [acronym_alias,phrase_alias,stem]·**newly_routed True**. `scotus_phrase`(SCOTUS↔Supreme Court): baseline **0.111**→probe **0.286**·entity [supremecourt]·newly_routed True. `stem_generalization`("Officials probe banks"↔"Official probes bank"): baseline 0→probe **1.0**·**alias 없이 light stemming 만으로 lift**(entity 0·curated table 밖 일반화). `diff_control`(Fed↔Hurricane): baseline 0.0→probe **0.0**·**newly_routed False**(무토큰중첩 음성 미lift). 집계: `pairs_newly_routed_by_probe=3`(entity 2 + non-entity stem 1)·sharing_entity 2. **구성된 known case 에서 정규화가 below-floor 같은-사건을 routing 으로 올림을 결정론 시연**(=(i) recall-miss 레버 작동·alias 테이블 밖 stem 일반화 포함)·**단 representative/held-out/live 일반화는 미측정**(deferred). **adversarial 검토 반영(이 턴 수정)**: 짧은 canonical 동음(raw 'sec'=seconds/Section)이 거짓 entity 로 승격되던 결함을 **provenance 게이트**(`_collapse_phrases` collapsed-flag + alias origin 양쪽 + canonical 어휘 AND)로 차단·무의미 tautology 단언 교정·stem 일반화/same-entity-honesty/API whitelist 테스트 추가. discrete tool dry: seed 3 valid(code_proposed_shape)·live 0·`insufficient_debug_artifact`·production blocked_no_live_opt_in·freeze 0·**gold 0·gap 200**·merge/llm/embedding/db/전송 0.

**정직한 해석(§5·단정 금지)** — recall probe 는 **synthetic 에서 (i) 레버가 실재·작동함을 증명**할 뿐, 실 ADR#77/#78 live below-floor 쌍이 (i)인지 (ii)인지는 **discrete-event 1d LIVE candidate pair 에 probe 를 적용해야** 알 수 있다(이번 턴 user opt synthetic-only→미실행). ADR#78 fed_rate 의 generic-only 공유는 그 seed 에선 (ii)로 약하게 기울지만 7d broad confound 때문에 여전히 indeterminate. same_event 단정 0·merge 경로 불변.

**검증** — backend 전체 **1535 passed/101 skipped/0 failed**·신규 backend 테스트 31(recall probe·provenance entity 게이트·stem 일반화·same-entity-honesty 포함)+29(discrete acquisition)+8(internal ops API endpoint·whitelist 포함)·frontend tsc 0·lint 0·node:test +7(ops view 39→46)·ruff(E/F/I/B/W−E501) 0·secret scan PASS·docs_lifecycle conflicts 0. (수치는 PROJECT_STATUS 최종 보고와 동기.)

**RISK(§13)** — 부분진전: R-DeterministicNearMatchRecall(normalization recall probe 구현·reviewer-routing only·false-merge 분리 AST 테스트·**synthetic known case 에서 recall 개선 측정**[newly_routed 2]·종결 금지[live 미측정]), R-CrossSourceNearMatchGap(recall probe 레버 시연·(i)/(ii) 구조 진전·overclaim 0·종결 금지[live 미분리]), R-ProviderPairNarrowness/R-ProductionCandidateScarcity/R-RagKgPrematureBuild/R-KoreanR1SourceGap(ADR#79 참조·종결 금지). 신규: R-NormalizationRecallLeakage(recall probe score 가 reviewer/public 으로 누출될 위험·LOW·테스트로 차단[score_exposed False·body-free·validate fail-loud]). 종결 0.

**다음 hard blocker** — ① **단일 discrete breaking event·1d·LIVE run + recall probe 를 live candidate pair 에 적용**해 (i)/(ii) 경험적 분리(승인+host/rate governed·seed 는 turn/scheduled 분산) → ② provider breadth(key-free RSS fleet·GDELT cooldown-honored) + Naver adapter wiring(KO floor) → ③ 실 reviewer contact → ④ actual returned labels(R1) → ⑤~ gold/MERGE_GATE/embedding/KG/IU(R2~R7). LLM 도 credential 도 blocker 아님.

**한계** — 이 턴 진전=recall probe 구현+**synthetic known case 검증**+discrete-event acquisition 머신리(seed 검증)+(i)/(ii) 구조 진전+ops 배선. **실 live run 0**(user opt synthetic-only)·실 production candidate freeze 0·actual returned labels 0·production_gold_count 0·**recall probe 는 synthetic 에서만 검증**(live pair 미적용). adjudicator runtime(embedding/LLM/KG/GraphRAG)·public IU·merge·운영 DB write·실 전송 0. internal ops read API live 0→`insufficient_debug_artifact`(정직). page.tsx render 후순위.

**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/{near_match_recall_probe,r1_discrete_event_acquisition}.py`·`backend/tests/{test_near_match_recall_probe,test_r1_discrete_event_acquisition,test_internal_ops_api}.py`·`backend/app/schemas/internal_ops.py`·`backend/app/api/internal_ops.py`·`frontend/src/lib/{api/types.ts,ops/opsPilotExecutionView.ts,ops/__tests__/opsPilotExecutionView.test.mjs}`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/{RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS,INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT,LLM_EVIDENCE_PACKET_CONTRACT,RAG_KG_ENTITY_GATE_CONTRACT}.md`·`docs/2_ROADMAP/{00_ROADMAP_INDEX,15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP,19_WEB_INTELLIGENCE_IMPLEMENTATION_SPEC}.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/_CANONICAL/02_CURRENT_ARCHITECTURE.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#76/#77/#78.

## ADR#80 — live discrete-event run + recall probe를 LIVE pair에 적용 + 3분류 + provider breadth

**선행** — ADR#79(discrete-event acquisition + deterministic recall probe[reviewer-routing recall·merge 분리]·**synthetic 검증만**)를 안정 기준점으로 커밋(`7f3ef11`·20파일·지정 subject·secret PASS·docs_lifecycle conflicts 0·closeout SIGNATURE_MATCH 25==25·unresolved 0·push 0·NO UPSTREAM). 이 커밋을 ADR#80 의 기준점으로 삼음.

**문제(§2·10문항 원자 분석)** — ADR#79 recall probe 는 **synthetic fixture 에만** 적용·실 live below-floor 쌍이 (i)detector-miss 인지 (ii)different-events 인지 미분리. 코드 6개 정독 결과: live pair 의 `title_left/right` 는 `cross_source_live_overlap_smoke` 내부 `discover_overlap(emit_candidate_pairs=True)` 의 `disc["candidate_pairs"]` 에만 존재(smoke 출력엔 shared_tokens 교집합만 노출·전문 미노출)·`summarize_recall_probe(pairs)` 가 그 candidate_pairs 와 **정확히 동일 구조** → 최소 변경 = **title 이 사는 smoke 레이어 1곳**에 probe 적용·상위는 passthrough(전문 노출 확대 0). host_gate 막힘=정직 block→`live_blocked`. lift→production freeze=reviewer-routing 후보 freeze(gold/merge 아님). lift 0→breadth vs detector 는 `comparison_pair_count` 로 가름. per-pair score 는 smoke internal `recall_probe_diagnostic` 에만·internal ops 는 max aggregate 만(§8).

**옵션 결정(§3·§4)** — **선택: A(actual labels)+B(discrete-event live·승인 시 bounded)+C(live pair recall probe·핵심)+D(provider/KO)+E(frontier)+F(contract guard) 채택·G/H(embedding/LLM/merge/public IU/DB/KG runtime) 금지.** per-turn live 승인 질의→**user 'Option 2 — bounded 실 네트워크 live run'** 선택(1 seed·1d·Guardian/NYT 한정·host_gate/rate 준수·raw body 0·secret 0·flaky 명시·코드/provider/seed/data 실패 분리). ADR#80 기록.

**구현(§3·전부 additive·신규 파일 0)** — ① `cross_source_live_overlap_smoke.py`: additive `emit_recall_probe`+`recall_routing_floor`·`_build_recall_probe_diagnostic`(cross-source candidate_pairs 에 `summarize_recall_probe`·body-free)→ 출력 `recall_probe_diagnostic`(기본 off=ADR#64/#78 동작 보존). ② `r1_targeted_live_acquisition.py`: 플래그 passthrough·`_aggregate_recall_probe_diagnostic`(seed별 max/newly-routed/entity 합)→ `live_recall_probe_diagnostic`+`max_live_recall_probe_score`+`live_pairs_newly_routed_by_probe`+`live_pairs_sharing_entity_after_probe`. ③ `r1_discrete_event_acquisition.py`: `emit_recall_probe=True` 로 호출·`_classify_live_recall_lift` **3분류**(`live_recall_lift_found`/`live_no_recall_lift`/`live_blocked_by_rate_or_opt_in`·코드 실패 vs provider/data 실패 분리)·`refine_root_cause_with_recall_probe` 가 live verdict 갱신·§3 output. ④ internal ops: `InternalOpsDiscreteAcquisitionFrontier` +4 필드(`max_live_recall_probe_score`·`live_pairs_newly_routed_by_probe`·`live_recall_lift_status`·`live_frontier_verdict`·**aggregate only**)+TS+view·필수 문구("Newly routed does not mean same event"·"Production gold remains 0 until human labels are returned"). **dict==pydantic==TS 26==26==26**. merge_allowed=False·recall_probe_applies_to_merge=False·same_event 단정 0·per-pair score reviewer/public 미노출 전 경로 불변(AST merge-path 분리 유지).

**🔴 실 LIVE RUN(§4·user 승인 opt 2·측정·flaky)** — seed=SCOTUS "Supreme Court ruling"·**1d**·Guardian+NYT·**2 calls**·host_gate(HostRateGate·guardian 5s/nyt 12s·no-bypass)·raw body 0·secret 0(credential present/missing boolean 만 확인·값 미열람). 결과 `RESULT_CLASS: LIVE_OK`(코드 정상): **comparison_pair_count=100**(publishable cross-source 비교쌍)·max_title_jaccard 0.1765·`all_below_hard_floor`·**`live_recall_probe_applied=True`**·**`live_recall_lift_status=live_no_recall_lift`**·`max_live_recall_probe_score=0.1765`(<0.2 routing floor)·**`live_pairs_newly_routed_by_probe=0`**·sharing_entity 0·`blocked_no_publishable_pairs`·freeze 0·gold 0·gap 200·merge/llm/embedding/db_write/same_event_truth_exposed/raw_source_body_exposed=False·exact "score" 키 0.

**정직한 해석(§5·단정 금지)** — synthetic 에서 작동한 (i) recall-miss 레버가 **100개 실 SCOTUS 1d cross-source pair 에서 lift 0** → synthetic 성공(0.333)이 이 live seed(0.1765·lift 0)에 **일반화되지 않음을 실측**. comparison_pair=100>0 → overlap 부재 아님·**(ii) different-events 또는 정규화 사전 한계** 쪽 신호이나 **reviewer 라벨 없이 same/different event 단정 0**. "Supreme Court ruling" seed 가 broad-lean(100개가 서로 다른 판결/측면일 개연)이라 더 좁은 단일-판결 seed 재측정 필요. merge 경로 불변·코드 실패 아님(data 결과).

**검증** — **backend 전체 1549 passed/101 skipped/0 failed**(975.89s·ADR#79 1535+14)·신규 backend 테스트 smoke +4·targeted +4·discrete +6·API 기존 갱신(22→26 field whitelist)·frontend tsc 0·lint 0·node:test +3(ops view 46→49)·ruff(E/F/I/B/W−E501) 0·secret scan PASS·docs_lifecycle conflicts 0·dict==pydantic==TS 26==26==26. (수치는 PROJECT_STATUS 최종 보고와 동기.)

**RISK(§9)** — 신규 4: R-LiveRecallProbeGeneralization(MEDIUM·synthetic lift 가 live 에 일반화 안 됨 실측·종결 금지), R-DiscreteEventSeedBias(LOW·cherry-pick seed (i) 부풀림 위험), R-AcquisitionFrontierPersistence(LOW·frontier persistence scope creep), R-KOAnalyzerDependency(LOW·KO 형태소 분절 부재). 부분진전: R-DeterministicNearMatchRecall(live 적용·**live lift 0**·종결 금지[live 미작동·(i)/(ii) 미분리]), R-CrossSourceNearMatchGap(live 데이터 진전·종결 금지), R-ProviderPairNarrowness(n=2 lift 0→breadth 신호), R-ProductionCandidateScarcity/R-NormalizationRecallLeakage/R-RagKgPrematureBuild/R-KoreanR1SourceGap/R-LiveAcquisitionRateBudget(종결 금지). 종결 0.

**다음 hard blocker** — ① **provider breadth**(key-free RSS 다출처 fleet·GDELT cooldown-honored·Naver/NewsAPI adapter wiring[KO floor]) — live lift 0 이 breadth 부족인지 정규화 한계인지 가름 → ② **더 좁은 single-ruling/decision 1d seed**에 recall probe 적용해 entity-공유 routing band pair 측정 → ③ 실 reviewer contact → ④ actual returned labels(R1) → ⑤~ gold/MERGE_GATE/embedding/KG/IU(R2~R7). LLM 도 credential 도 blocker 아님.

**한계** — 이 턴 진전=recall probe 를 **실 live pair 에 적용**(머신리 작동 입증)+3분류+ops 배선+**실 live run 1회**(lift 0 측정). **실 (i)/(ii) 분리 0**(live lift 0은 (ii)/사전한계 쪽이나 미단정)·실 production candidate freeze 0(blocked_no_publishable_pairs)·actual returned labels 0·production_gold_count 0. adjudicator runtime(embedding/LLM/KG/GraphRAG)·public IU·merge·운영 DB·실 전송 0. internal ops read API live 0→`live_blocked_by_rate_or_opt_in`(정직). page.tsx render 후순위.

**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/{cross_source_live_overlap_smoke,r1_targeted_live_acquisition,r1_discrete_event_acquisition}.py`·`backend/app/schemas/internal_ops.py`·`backend/tests/{test_cross_source_live_overlap_smoke,test_r1_targeted_live_acquisition,test_r1_discrete_event_acquisition,test_internal_ops_api}.py`·`frontend/src/lib/{api/types.ts,ops/opsPilotExecutionView.ts,ops/__tests__/opsPilotExecutionView.test.mjs}`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/{RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS,INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT,RAG_KG_ENTITY_GATE_CONTRACT}.md`·`docs/2_ROADMAP/{00_ROADMAP_INDEX,15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP,19_WEB_INTELLIGENCE_IMPLEMENTATION_SPEC}.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/_CANONICAL/02_CURRENT_ARCHITECTURE.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#77/#78/#79.

## ADR#81 — provider breadth + named single-event seed + KO source path (acquisition support·실 live 미실행)

**선행** — ADR#80(live discrete-event run + recall probe 를 LIVE pair 에 적용 + 3분류)를 안정 기준점으로 커밋(`87b14f9`·21파일·지정 subject `feat(events): apply recall probe to live discrete-event pairs and classify frontier (ADR#80) …`·secret PASS·docs_lifecycle conflicts 0·closeout SIGNATURE_MATCH 26==26·unresolved 0·push 0·NO UPSTREAM). 이 커밋을 ADR#81 의 기준점으로 삼음.

**문제(§2·20문항 원자 분석)** — ADR#80 실 live run lift 0(`max_live_recall_probe_score=0.1765`<0.2·newly_routed 0·sharing_entity 0). 원인 분해(프로젝트 사망 아님): (a) seed "Supreme Court ruling" = 기관+일반행위 **category-lean**(comparison 100 = 단일 판결 아님·entity-sharing 0 = 정규화 후 100쌍 중 0쌍이 entity 토큰 공유 = seed 비특이성 + 영어 alias 표 협소[14+11]), (b) provider = Guardian×NYT 둘뿐(2 일반지 헤드라인 분기), (c) KO 미연결(KO floor 50·KO gold 0). **결정적 발견: source_registry.yaml 에 이미 57 소스 와이어링** — "Guardian×NYT only" 는 live run 의 한계였지 wiring 의 한계가 아님.

**옵션 결정(§3)** — **선택: A(actual input 재확인)+B(provider breadth inventory)+C(named single-event seed bank)+E(KO source path)+F(internal ops frontier·제한)+G(community reaction contract·docs) 채택. D(bounded live)=`blocked_no_live_opt_in`**(/compact 에 이번 턴 live 명시 승인 없음→§7 기본값·named seed queued·승인은 next step 질의). **H(LLM/RAG/KG runtime)+I(public IU runtime) 금지.**

**구현(§3·전부 additive·신규 3 도구+1 orchestrator)** — ① `provider_breadth_inventory.py`: source_registry(`load_registry`) → **57 소스=9 카테고리**(query_capable_publishable 7·feed_only_publishable 7·official_source 5·search_url_candidate 4·ko_official_news 6·community_reaction_only 9·market_signal_only 6·catalog_enrichment_only 9·unknown_quarantine 4·anchor_eligible **25**)·curated anchor-eligibility ∩ registry type·`source_role_guard_preserved`(non-anchor 카테고리 `anchor_eligible=False` 강제)·credential secret-safe(`env_status`·present/missing 만·값 0). ② `named_event_seed_bank.py`: validator는 **구조 필드+소규모 exact denylist+placeholder reject 만** 강제(의미적 discreteness 검증 아님)·그 위 **수작업 큐레이트** bank(fomc_rate_decision·ecb_rate_decision **accepted**·scotus/M&A/sanction 템플릿 placeholder reject·broad 자가검증 5/5 reject)·`same_event_asserted=False`·`event_occurrence_verified=False`·provenance=code_proposed_named_shape. ⚠ **정직 한계**(adversarial): exact denylist 는 "기관명+단어 추가"로 우회 가능·**fomc=연 8회 반복 announcement TYPE**(unique one-off 아님·SCOTUS category 와 동족)이라 discreteness 는 *단일 scheduled announcement+operator 날짜 pin* 의존 **미측정 가설**·outlet 수렴은 예측이지 측정 아님(라이브 미실행). ③ `ko_source_readiness.py`: KO 소스 14종(news 5 LIVE key-free·Naver 어댑터 2·KO official·community reaction·trend quarantine)·credential secret-safe(`probe_env_var`)·**KO tokenization risk**(`[0-9A-Za-z가-힣]+` Hangul-aware 이나 형태소/stemming/KO alias 부재→KO-KO undercount·breadth-only until analyzer·crash-safe)·KO floor plan(human label 이 hard blocker·solved=False). ④ `r1_provider_breadth_acquisition.py` orchestrator: discrete base(ADR#80)+3 도구 합성→§4 output+§10 frontier `InternalOpsProviderBreadthFrontier`(**dict==pydantic==TS 30==30==30**·per-pair score/same_event/PII/secret 미노출)·`GET /api/internal/ops/r1-provider-breadth`(read API live 0). 필수 copy: "Provider breadth is acquisition support, not truth"·"Named seed is candidate generation, not same-event proof"·"Community reaction is not an event anchor"·"Production gold remains 0…"·"R2~R7 remain No-Go".

**live 정책(§7·이번 턴 미실행)** — /compact 에 이번 턴 live 실행 명시 승인 없음 → `live_query_executed=False`·`live_run_status=blocked_no_live_opt_in`·`next_action=ask_for_bounded_live_run_approval`·selected_seed_for_next_live_run=**fomc_rate_decision**(named single-event·discrete scheduled announcement·key-free official+aggregator 보도 수렴 예상). 실 네트워크 호출 0·secret 값 미열람·raw body 0.

**community reaction contract(§9·docs only·runtime 0)** — `RAG_KG_ENTITY_GATE_CONTRACT §4a` 신설(allowed: reaction_to verified event·sentiment/controversy/time-series·대표 snippet[ToS 시]·provenance·uncertainty; forbidden: anchor·same_event proof·rumor as fact·PII·ToS 위반·community 단독 public IU)·rumor amplification guard·provider breadth 가 community 를 anchor 로 승격 안 함. 검증된 event 0 → 부착 대상 0.

**검증** — **신규 backend 테스트 55**(provider_breadth_inventory **17**[+2 guard drift/exception 교차검증]·named_event_seed_bank 10·ko_source_readiness 11·r1_provider_breadth_acquisition 9·internal_ops_api +8)·ADR#79/#80 회귀 무변경(208 통과)·**backend 전체 1605 passed / 101 skipped / 0 failed**(992.85s 측정 1603+가드 2)·ingestion 무변경·frontend tsc 0·lint 0·node:test 49→**58**(+9 breadth view)·dict==pydantic==TS 30==30==30·secret scan PASS(21 files)·docs_lifecycle conflicts 0.

**RISK(§14)** — 신규 4: R-ProviderBreadthScopeCreep(LOW·57 소스 혼합 역할이 anchor guard 약화 위험·테스트 차단), R-SearchCandidateTruthLeakage(LOW·SERP snippet 을 truth 로 위험·`search_url_candidate` 분류 차단), R-NamedSeedSelectionBias(LOW·named seed cherry-pick (i) 부풀림), R-LiveRunReproducibility(LOW·live 결과 self-attested·repo persist 부재·R-AcquisitionFrontierPersistence 와 연계). 부분진전: R-ProviderPairNarrowness(breadth inventory 완성·alternative provider 미실측·종결 금지), R-KoreanR1SourceGap(KO path/adapter status 연결·KO gold 0·종결 금지), R-ProductionCandidateScarcity(named seed/breadth 경로 확장·freeze 0·종결 금지), R-CrossSourceNearMatchGap/R-DeterministicNearMatchRecall/R-RagKgPrematureBuild(종결 금지). 종결 0.

**다음 hard blocker** — ① **승인된 bounded live run**(named seed fomc_rate_decision·1~2 seed·1d·publishable provider·host/rate 준수) 으로 named-seed 가설 실측 → ② provider breadth 를 comparison pool 에 실제 wiring(key-free anchor + KO news) → ③ live-derived production candidate freeze → ④ 실 reviewer contact → ⑤ actual returned human labels(R1·코드로 못 옮김) → ⑥~ gold/MERGE_GATE/embedding/KG/IU(R2~R7). **종착 blocker = human labeling**(breadth/named seed/KO 는 모두 선행조건).

**한계** — 이 턴 진전=세 레버(provider breadth·named single-event seed·KO source path)를 **실 acquisition frontier 머신리로 끌어내림**(57 소스 분류·named seed bank·KO readiness·orchestrator·internal ops frontier). **실 live 미실행**(blocked_no_live_opt_in)·실 production candidate freeze 0·actual returned labels 0·production_gold_count 0·R1 FAIL·R2~R7 No-Go·semantic 실병합/public IU/운영 DB/embedding/LLM/실 전송 0. live result persistence 부재(R-LiveRunReproducibility·향후 sanitized body-free snapshot 방향만).

**관련 문서** — `backend/app/tools/{provider_breadth_inventory,named_event_seed_bank,ko_source_readiness,r1_provider_breadth_acquisition}.py`·`backend/app/schemas/internal_ops.py`·`backend/app/api/internal_ops.py`·`backend/tests/{test_provider_breadth_inventory,test_named_event_seed_bank,test_ko_source_readiness,test_r1_provider_breadth_acquisition,test_internal_ops_api}.py`·`frontend/src/lib/{api/types.ts,ops/opsPilotExecutionView.ts,ops/__tests__/opsPilotExecutionView.test.mjs}`·`docs/5_REFERENCE/{RAG_KG_AGENT_READINESS,INTELLIGENCE_UNIT_CONTRACT,RAG_KG_ENTITY_GATE_CONTRACT}.md`·`docs/2_ROADMAP/{00_ROADMAP_INDEX,15_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP,19_WEB_INTELLIGENCE_IMPLEMENTATION_SPEC}.md`·`docs/_RISK/RISK_REGISTER.md`·`docs/_CANONICAL/02_CURRENT_ARCHITECTURE.md`·`PROJECT_STATUS.md`, ADR#78/#79/#80.
